# STS1000 "Meridian" — Schematic-to-Layout Readiness Review

> ⚠️ **HISTORICAL SNAPSHOT (2026-06-21) — partly superseded.** This review predates the
> **STM32H563VIT6/LQFP100 → STM32H563ZIT6/LQFP144** migration and the 2026-07-05 overhaul.
> References here to U12 as VIT6/LQFP100, the MCP23017 expanders, GPS INA228 @0x44, and the
> board-wide INA228 SDA/SCL swap describe the **June state** and are retained as a point-in-time
> record. Several blockers are now RESOLVED in the working tree (SDA/SCL swap, U37/U44 address
> collision). For the current defect list see **`sts1000_schematic_design_review.md`**; for the
> current pin/net facts see **`ntp_server_peripheral_map.md`** and
> **`sts1000_firmware_hardware_interface.md`**. Do not "fix docs" against this file.

_Multi-agent review. Goal: readiness for PCB layout handoff — NOT fabrication. Verify findings against datasheets/files before acting._

> Generated by 20 per-sheet agents + 5 cross-cutting agents. Confidence levels are per-finding; treat Low/Unknown items as requiring human confirmation.


## 1–2. Design intent & project inventory

## STS1000 "Meridian" — Design-Intent Summary & Project Inventory (pre-layout readiness, board-level)

Scope: whole-board design intent extracted from `/docs` + root/hardware `CLAUDE.md`, cross-checked against the KiCad project files present on disk. This is the orientation block for per-block reviews; it is NOT itself a netlist/datasheet verification of any part. Designators below are as the docs assign them; several still carry `<!-- TODO verify designator -->` markers in the docs (flagged).

---

### 1) Design-intent table

| Area | Intended behavior / requirement | Source doc | Evidence | Related blocks/nets | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| Product purpose | GPS-disciplined Stratum-1 NTP/NTS/PTP grandmaster, single-board, PoE-powered | root `CLAUDE.md`; `software_spec §1` | "GPS-disciplined Stratum-1 NTP/NTS/PTP grandmaster clock" | whole board | PASS (intent) |
| Operating modes | Boot on OCXO (mux A); switch to Rb (mux B) only when EXTREF_MON in-band AND RB_LOCK asserted; revert fail-safe; holdover; warm-up gating before advertising S1 | `periph §2.1, §15.5`; `software_spec §3.4/§3.5` | "Switch OCXO→Rb only when both #2 and #3 hold"; firmware HSI-bridge + CSS | MUX_SEL PB6, EXTREF_MON PB14, RB_LOCK PB13, OSC_IN PH0 | PASS (intent) |
| Power input — PoE bt | 802.3bt-capable front end; classify Type 2 (at, ~25.5 W) min, Type 3 (bt) for margin; Rb is permanent and concurrent | `periph §6`; `hardware CLAUDE.md` | OCXO+Rb steady ~12–14 W, peak ~25–30 W; Class 3 (~13 W) insufficient | U7/U8 FDMQ8205A, U9 NCP1095, magjack J1 | PASS (intent); classification = config open item |
| Power rails | 3V3 main + 5V intermediate from bucks; OCXO fixed low-noise rail (always on); Rb adjustable buck (5–24 V, EN-gated); 5V_DISP gated; all housekeeping on always-on 3V3_STM (gated 3V3_P eliminated) | `periph §6`; `net_naming` | rename table; "3V3_P rail was removed" | U28/U29, U38/U39, U40A, U33, all I²C devices | PASS (intent) |
| Comms interfaces | Ethernet RMII (AF11) + 1588 HW timestamp; USART3 GPS; UART4 RTCM; UART7 Rb; SPI4 (NOR+TFT+digipot); I²C1 housekeeping; USB-FS CDC console | `periph §1,§3,§5,§10`; `software_spec §2` | pin tables per bus | U11, U21, U43/U62/TFT, I²C bus | PASS (intent) |
| Connectors | RJ45 magjack (J1), USB-FS (J5), DE-9 FE-5680A housekeeping (J6), 3× coax SMA (J7/J8/J9: 10 MHz-in, GPS-ant, 10 MHz bench-out), pin headers J2/J3/J4/J10/J11 | `bom §J`; BOM CSV L214–224 | CSV: J1 Bel 0826-1X1T, J5 USB4120-03-C, J6 DE9, J7/8/9 Conn_Coaxial | connectors.kicad_sch | WARNING — J2/J4/J7/8/9/J10/J11 footprints still generic/SELECT |
| Sensors | 8× INA228, 2× TMP117, IIS2MDC + LIS2DH12 e-compass, PIR (PaPIRs), FT6336U touch, fan tach | `periph §4,§8`; checklist §11–13 | INA map; e-compass note | I²C1 bus, U54/U55 | PASS (intent); LIS2DH12 SA0, PIR PN open |
| Timing ref — OCXO | OH300-61003CV-010.0M, 10 MHz, always on, DAC1_OUT1 (PA4)→loop filter→Vc center 1.65 V, Vc sense PA3; Vc caps C0G/film never X7R | `periph §2`; checklist §2 | "Vc must be biased to ~1.65 V"; "C0G/NP0 or film — never X7R" | Y3, U38/U39, R123 22Ω, U37 INA228#5 | PASS (intent) |
| Timing ref — Rb | External FE-5680A only (no onboard Rb); 10 MHz over coax→SMA front end; power/serial/lock/PPS on DE-9; adjustable buck, RB_PWR_EN gate | `periph §2.2,§15`; `vcc_rb_supply` | "There is no onboard Rb option"; "10 MHz does NOT enter this connector" | U40A, U43, U41A OV latch, J6, J7 SMA | PASS (intent); FE-5680A variant pinout open |
| Timing ref — GNSS | ZED-F9T-00B, USART3, TIMEPULSE→PA0/TIM2, TIMEPULSE2→PC6/TIM3, full reset/safeboot/dsel; V_BCKP held through VCC cycles | `periph §3`; checklist §6 | F9T pin table | U21, U22 LDO, U23 INA228#3 | PASS (intent) |
| Isolation / safety | Autonomous 26 V Rb OV latch (LMV393 + BJT, MCU-independent); POE_KILL board cold-cycle; external windowed WDT→POE_KILL; digital isolator on PoE status only-if isolated PD (open) | `periph §6,§9`; `vcc_rb_supply`; `external_wdt` | "trips at 26 V…no MCU action"; WDT→POE_KILL | U41A, U64 TPS3430, PE15 | PASS (intent); NCL/NCM/LCF isolation open |
| Environmental | −40/+85 °C MCU; consumer −40/+85 parts checked vs enclosure thermal; supercap ≤~75 °C placement; fan thermal loop fail-safe to full speed | root `CLAUDE.md`; `periph §8`; checklist §10 | "floating FAN_PWM defaults to maximum airflow" | DSF305Q3R0, TMP117 ×2, fan | PASS (intent); LIS2DH12/supercap thermal = layout-verify |
| Debug / programming / secure boot | SWD (PA13/14/PB3) + NRST; USB CDC-ACM driverless console + SMP recovery; STiRoT→MCUboot→app; ATECC608B (0x60) for keys/NTS | `periph §10`; `software_spec §1.1` | "STiRoT (immutable ST root)…ATECC608B" | U12, U60, J5 USB | PASS (intent) |
| Mechanical | Single board, enclosure deploy ("Observatory at Williams Manor"); e-compass at board edge/external puck; vertical display mount | root `CLAUDE.md`; `periph §4 note` | e-compass keep-out + mount note | IIS2MDC, MSP4030 | UNKNOWN — no mechanical/enclosure doc in /docs |
| Layout-sensitive circuits | OCXO Vc path, Rb FB node, IIS2MDC GND pour, GPS SMA ESD (RF+bias), source termination at driver, RF island | `hardware CLAUDE.md §Layout-critical` | full rule list | see §3 below | PASS (rules captured); execution = layout |
| Expected connector pinouts | FE-5680A DE-9 (J6) power/serial/lock/PPS only — varies by surplus variant, verify before layout; SMA = 10 MHz only | `periph §2.2,§14`; checklist §14 | "FE-5680A connector pinouts vary by variant" | J6, J7 | WARNING — variant pinout unresolved |
| Test points | ETH_PPS_OUT (PB5) scope tap; 10 MHz bench fanout SMA (J9); USB console | `periph §1,§2.1,§8`; checklist §16 | "PTP pulse output — verification/scope tap" | PB5, U53, J9 | PASS (intent) |
| Known risks | Back-power via I²C ESD clamps (fixed by 3V3_STM), glitch-free mux hang on dead Rb (fixed by selector+HSI bridge), Rb digipot in FB node, GPS SMA dual-duty ESD | root `CLAUDE.md §gotchas` | enumerated gotchas | I²C bus, U52, U43, GPS SMA | PASS (documented) |

---

### 3) Top layout-readiness risks (board-level)

1. **OCXO Vc / loop-filter path** — phase-noise-critical; Vc caps must be C0G/NP0 or film (X7R microphonics FM the carrier), keep DAC/digital noise off the high-impedance Vc node, R123 22 Ω source term at the OCXO output only. Highest single timing-quality risk.
2. **Rb adjustable-buck FB node (VCC_RB)** — digipot wiper/SPI noise on a high-Z FB node can destabilize/over-volt a multi-thousand-dollar Rb; fixed bounding resistors (not the digipot) must set absolute min/max for every wiper code incl. POR/mid-scale/SPI-fault; autonomous 26 V OV latch placement near the buck output. Highest part-damage risk.
3. **IIS2MDC e-compass placement/return path** — needs continuous current-free GND pour, max distance from Rb physics package / OCXO oven / bucks / PoE magnetics / fan motor / DC-rail currents (board edge or external puck). Likely the hardest placement constraint to satisfy on a dense single board.
4. **GPS SMA ESD/surge** — single coax carries 1.5 GHz RF (needs Cj ≤ 0.2–0.3 pF) AND 5 V antenna bias (needs V_RWM ≥ ~6.5 V); requires polymer suppressor + separate coaxial GDT for outdoor run. No single standard ESD part meets both.
5. **PoE / high-voltage power section** — FDMQ8205A bridge, NCP1095, MIC28516 bucks, VOUT_N primary return with HV caps (REVIEW-HV), 25–30 W peak; creepage/clearance, thermal copper, and shunt-current width must be sized before layout. INA228 shunt values still TBD per rail.
6. **RF island (3V0_RF) + clock-mux/fanout integrity** — controlled-impedance 10 MHz routing, island partition for U50 LTC6752xS5 slicer + U51 LDO, 50 Ω term switching (U49), source-match at U53 fanout; keep the ext-ref path isolated from RMII 50 MHz domain.
7. **Supercap thermal derating** — DSF305Q3R0 must sit ≤ ~75 °C (2.55 V peak at 2.5 V/85 °C rating); placement away from Rb/OCXO/buck heat.

#### Notable doc-vs-state mismatches to resolve before per-block review (not yet datasheet-verified here)
- **Digipot identity:** docs specify MCP41U83T-503E/ST (U43), but custom libs contain AD5270/AD5292 symbols and ADI footprints (CP_16/RM_10/RU-14) — confirm which symbol U43 actually uses.
- **Software spec §2.1/§2.2 is STALE vs peripheral map §2.2/§13:** it still lists `REF_SRC_SEL (PA10)` and `REF_SLICER_SEL (PC0)` and a DB9 clock source, all of which the pin map says were deleted (PA10→PG_INT_N, PC0→EXP_RST_N). Software spec also lists V_BCKP backup on PD2/PD3 — now SPI_DPOT_CS / RB_OV_RESET. Authority rule: pin map wins; software_spec needs propagation.
- **Standing KiCad actions unverified:** drop legacy R44 at PC12; rename `PG_IN_N`→`PG_INT_N`; confirm INT/EXP_RST_N land on PA10/PE0/PC12/PC0. Doc TODO comments suggest R44 may already be repurposed as a 49.9 Ω PHY term — must be checked in the actual schematic.
- **Many designators in checklist/hardware CLAUDE.md carry `<!-- TODO verify designator -->`** (C/D/Q/FB references on clock-mux, RF, antenna, Rb-RS232, display ESD sheets) — designator stability must be confirmed against the re-annotated schematic before any per-block sign-off.
- **Untracked new custom libs** (PGB1010603MR.kicad_sym, IND_PGB_0603_LTF*.kicad_mod) added on this branch but not yet referenced in the docs/checklist — confirm where the PGB1010603MR ESD/PTC part is used.
- **No enclosure/mechanical doc** exists in /docs; mechanical intent (mounting, panel cutouts, antenna/coax egress, vertical display mount) is only implied. Layout will need this.

## 3. Layout-readiness executive summary

- ICs reviewed (approx): **76**
- Footprints checked (approx): **136**
- BOM lines: **535** (see §7 per-subsystem + §8)
- Subsystems reviewed: **20/20**
- **Blockers: 68**
- **High-risk items: 59**

**Overall status: NEEDS SCHEMATIC/LIBRARY CORRECTIONS BEFORE LAYOUT**

Top layout-readiness risks:
- **[PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)] POE_KILL net / R21 / Q3 / KILL_N** — KILL_N net = {Q1.C(C_3), Q5.C(C_3), R22.2} only — it has NO pull-up. Canonical sts1000_poe_kill.md requires R21 100k from V_KBIAS to KILL_N so KILL_N defaults HIGH=RUN. As wired, R21.1=V_KBIAS, R21.2=Net-(Q3-C); R21 is in Q3's collector, not on KILL_N. Q3 (BC857W PNP) is also reversed vs doc: doc wants E=V_KBIAS, C=HOLD; as built E=HOLD node (C9/R25/R27), C=via R21 to V_KBIAS, B=via R22 to KILL_N. A PNP sustain switch with its emitter on the floating HOLD node and no KILL_N pull-up cannot implement the documented default-RUN / self-sustaining-kill behavior. The whole AUX kill actuator is non-functional / indeterminate at power-up.
- **[PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)] D1 / missing input TVS across VOUT_P-VOUT_N** — No high-voltage surge TVS clamps the rectified PD bus (VOUT_P->VOUT_N = NCP1095 VPP->VPN). Canonical doc mandates D1=SMBJ58A TVS VPP->VPN (doc lines 78,125). In the schematic D1 is a BAV70LT1G small-signal array used for GBR steering, and no SMBJ58A/SMAJ/1.5SMC part exists on VOUT_P. D2/D3 are only 6.8V SOT-363 arrays in the gate-drive net, not a bus clamp. PD input has no avalanche surge protection for IEEE 802.3bt / IEC 61000-4-5 transients; only bulk C10 10uF/100V + C8 0.1uF/100V are present.
- **[PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)] U10 (and all INA228) SDA/SCL swap** — Net 'I2C_SCL' (carries MCU PB8=I2C1_SCL clock, U12.95) lands on U10 pin4 = SDA; net 'I2C_SDA' (PB9, U12.96) lands on U10 pin5 = SCL. INA228 DGS pinout is pin4=SDA, pin5=SCL (TI datasheet, verified) and the embedded symbol is correct. So the bus is crossed: the I2C clock physically reaches the INA228 data pin and vice-versa. Same crossover appears on U10,U23,U26,U30,U31,U32,U37,U44 — board-wide; it surfaces on this sheet at U10 (#1, 0x40). I2C to all power monitors will not enumerate.
- **[5V/3V3 main power supply (sheet 3v3-main-power.kicad_sch)] U29 AP3441 (CM5IO:AP3441SHE-7B symbol)** — Custom symbol pin map is scrambled vs datasheet DS39754. Datasheet pins: 1=FB,2=PG,3=VIN,4=SGND,5=EN,6=LX,7=PGND,8=NC. Symbol has 4=PGND,5=nc,6=LX,7=EN,8=SGND. Net result as wired: the real EN pin (datasheet pin5) is tied to the symbol's no-connect -> the regulator can never be enabled; real PGND (pin7) is driven by 5V_PSU_PG (EN net) -> power ground forced to 5V; real SGND (pin4) goes to PGND net; real NC (pin8) goes to SGND net. Board-killing. Same wrong symbol is used for U38 (OCXO buck) elsewhere -> propagates.
- **[5V/3V3 main power supply (sheet 3v3-main-power.kicad_sch)] U30/U31/U32 INA228 (and ALL eight INA228 board-wide)** — I2C SDA/SCL swapped between master and every slave. STM32 PB8(pin95)->net I2C_SCL, PB9(pin96)->net I2C_SDA (correct: PB8=I2C1_SCL, PB9=I2C1_SDA on STM32H5). But every INA228 has SDA(pin4) on net I2C_SCL and SCL(pin5) on net I2C_SDA. Master clock line lands on slave data pins and vice-versa -> bus non-functional. Confirmed identical on U10/U23/U26/U37/U44 too.
- **[Supercap backup supplies (U34/U35 TPS61094 ×2 + DSF305Q3R0 3F supercaps)] C90 / C91 (DSF305Q3R0)** — Footprint is the placeholder string "Radial", not a real KiCad footprint. The DSF305Q3R0 is a specific radial can (3.5 mm pin pitch, defined diameter/height). Cannot be laid out as-is.
- **[Supercap backup supplies (U34/U35 TPS61094 ×2 + DSF305Q3R0 3F supercaps)] fp-lib-table (project)** — fp-lib-table is EMPTY, but U34/U35 reference footprint via library nickname "TPS61094DSSR:SON50P300X200X80-13N". The .kicad_mod exists in hardware/libraries/ as a loose file, not in a TPS61094DSSR.pretty library, so the nickname will not resolve at layout/PCB-update.
- **[Ethernet magnetics/input (sheet: ethernet-input.kicad_sch)] J1** — Magjack 0826-1X1T-HS-F has NO footprint assigned (Footprint field empty in symbol and netlist; fp-lib-table is empty; no in-repo land pattern). Cannot place/route this part — hard blocker for layout.
- **[Ethernet magnetics/input (sheet: ethernet-input.kicad_sch)] J1** — Symbol is instantiated from the `0826-1X1T-GH-F` library but Value/MPN/datasheet = `0826-1X1T-HS-F` (a different gigabit variant). Pin NAMES match the HS-F drawing, but the footprint/land pattern must be the HS-F's, not GH-F's.
- **[Ethernet magnetics/input (sheet: ethernet-input.kicad_sch)] U1** — TPD4EUSB30 footprint is the bare string "10-USON" with no library prefix and no fp-lib-table — unresolved, cannot place.
- **[MCU core (STM32H563VIT6, U12)] U12 pin94 BOOT0 (R49/R50)** — BOOT0 is tied to a resistive divider: R49 10k to 3V3 + R50 10k to GND, so BOOT0 idles at ~1.65 V. That is an indeterminate logic level for the boot-mode strap (must be a hard 0 or 1). With the project no-DNP policy both resistors are populated, so the part may boot to bootloader or flash unpredictably and is noise-sensitive.
- **[MCU core (STM32H563VIT6, U12)] U12 footprint assignment** — The placed U12 instance has Footprint = "100-LQFP" (no library prefix) which does NOT exist in the repo; only LQFP-100_STM.kicad_mod (+ -L/-M) exist, and the symbol's own default is "LQFP-100_STM" (also unprefixed). There is no fp-lib-table anywhere in the project. The footprint will not resolve for layout.

## 4. Blockers before layout

| # | Where | Ref | Issue | Recommended fix | Confidence |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch) | POE_KILL net / R21 / Q3 / KILL_N | KILL_N net = {Q1.C(C_3), Q5.C(C_3), R22.2} only — it has NO pull-up. Canonical sts1000_poe_kill.md requires R21 100k from V_KBIAS to KILL_N so KILL_N defaults HIGH=RUN. As wired, R21.1=V_KBIAS, R21.2=Net-(Q3-C); R21 is in Q3's collector, not on KILL_N. Q3 (BC857W PNP) is also reversed vs doc: doc wants E=V_KBIAS, C=HOLD; as built E=HOLD node (C9/R25/R27), C=via R21 to V_KBIAS, B=via R22 to KILL_N. A PNP sustain switch with its emitter on the floating HOLD node and no KILL_N pull-up cannot implement the documented default-RUN / self-sustaining-kill behavior. The whole AUX kill actuator is non-functional / indeterminate at power-up. | Rewire to doc: R21 100k pull-up KILL_N->V_KBIAS (default RUN). Q3 PNP: E=V_KBIAS, B=via R22 from KILL_N, C=HOLD node (C9\|\|R25 to VOUT_N, R27 divider top). Then HOLD->R27/R29->VAUX. Re-verify on netlist that KILL_N has exactly one pull-up and both Q1.C and Q5.C pull it low. | High |
| 2 | PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch) | D1 / missing input TVS across VOUT_P-VOUT_N | No high-voltage surge TVS clamps the rectified PD bus (VOUT_P->VOUT_N = NCP1095 VPP->VPN). Canonical doc mandates D1=SMBJ58A TVS VPP->VPN (doc lines 78,125). In the schematic D1 is a BAV70LT1G small-signal array used for GBR steering, and no SMBJ58A/SMAJ/1.5SMC part exists on VOUT_P. D2/D3 are only 6.8V SOT-363 arrays in the gate-drive net, not a bus clamp. PD input has no avalanche surge protection for IEEE 802.3bt / IEC 61000-4-5 transients; only bulk C10 10uF/100V + C8 0.1uF/100V are present. | Add an SMBJ58A (or SMCJ58A for energy margin) TVS from VOUT_P to VOUT_N at the bridge output, placed at the PD input. Confirm standoff (>57V port) and clamp below NCP1095 VPP abs-max and FET VDS 100V. | High |
| 3 | PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch) | U10 (and all INA228) SDA/SCL swap | Net 'I2C_SCL' (carries MCU PB8=I2C1_SCL clock, U12.95) lands on U10 pin4 = SDA; net 'I2C_SDA' (PB9, U12.96) lands on U10 pin5 = SCL. INA228 DGS pinout is pin4=SDA, pin5=SCL (TI datasheet, verified) and the embedded symbol is correct. So the bus is crossed: the I2C clock physically reaches the INA228 data pin and vice-versa. Same crossover appears on U10,U23,U26,U30,U31,U32,U37,U44 — board-wide; it surfaces on this sheet at U10 (#1, 0x40). I2C to all power monitors will not enumerate. | Swap the two net labels at the INA228 bank (or re-route): I2C_SCL must reach pin5(SCL), I2C_SDA must reach pin4(SDA). | 4 | 5V/3V3 main power supply (sheet 3v3-main-power.kicad_sch) | U29 AP3441 (CM5IO:AP3441SHE-7B symbol) | Custom symbol pin map is scrambled vs datasheet DS39754. | 13 | GNSS receiver (ZED-F9T) — U21 ZED-F9T-00B, U22 LT3045 LDO, U23 INA228 @0x44 | U22 pin 6 (PGFB) / net Net-(U22-PGFB) | LT3045 PGFB (pin 6) is shorted to the LDO input: net Net-(U22-PGFB) contains U22 pin1(IN), pin2(IN), pin6(PGFB), FB3, C46, fed from 5V via FB3. PGFB is the power-good comparator feedback input (PG asserts when PGFB>0.3V, 7mV hyst). Tying it to VIN makes PG report 'good' off the 5V input regardless of whether VOUT(3.3V) is actually present, so the 3V3_GPS_LDO_PG flag to U55 GPA0 is meaningless. | 14 | GNSS receiver (ZED-F9T) — U21 ZED-F9T-00B, U22 LT3045 LDO, U23 INA228 @0x44 | U22 pin 4 (PG) / net 3V3_GPS_LDO_PG | LT3045 PG is an open-collector/open-drain output. | 40 | I2C peripherals + display power | U63 (PCA9306) SCL2/SDA2 — nets I2C_DISP_SCL / I2C_DISP_SDA | No pull-up resistors on the 5V_DISP (VREF2/high-voltage) side of the PCA9306. The low side has R202/R203 (4.7k to 3V3_STM), but the display side has none in the schematic. | Add 2 pull-ups (2.2k-4.7k) from SCL2 and SDA2 to 5V_DISP, OR positively confirm the LCDwiki MSP4030 module populates touch-bus pull-ups and document that dependency. | High |
| 41 | Fault/UI aggregation (MCP23017 ×2: U55 @0x20, U54 @0x21) | U54 GPA7 (pin 24) = DISP_TOUCH_INT | Input signal mapped to MCP23017 GPA7, which Microchip (DS20001952 Rev D, June 2022, and the article cited in this part's own symbol Description) states must NOT be used as an input on the I2C MCP23017: an input transition coincident with an I2C read can corrupt SDA and hang the bus. This is the shared housekeeping I2C bus (~21 nodes incl. all 8 INA228, TMP117, ATECC608B), so a hang takes down all power/thermal monitoring. | Reassign DISP_TOUCH_INT off GPA7 to any GPA0-6 / GPB0-6 pin (U54 is 16/16 full, so move one of the other inputs to U55's spare GPB2-7, or route DISP_TOUCH_INT directly to a spare MCU EXTI). Keep GPA7/GPB7 as outputs or NC only. | High |
| 42 | Fault/UI aggregation (MCP23017 ×2: U55 @0x20, U54 @0x21) | U54 GPB7 (pin 4) = INA_ALERT_VCC_RB | Input on GPB7 (output-only restricted pin) — same SDA-corruption/bus-hang hazard. This carries the Rb-rail INA228 #6 ALERT. | Move INA_ALERT_VCC_RB to a non-bit-7 GPIO (rebalance U54/U55 bit map; U55 GPB2-7 are spare). | High |
| 43 | Fault/UI aggregation (MCP23017 ×2: U55 @0x20, U54 @0x21) | U55 GPA7 (pin 24) = POE_PG | Input on GPA7 (output-only restricted pin) — same hazard. Carries PoE power-good. | Move POE_PG to one of U55's spare GPB2-7 inputs (GPB7 must stay output/NC). | High |
| 44 | Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch) | D7 | TVS on VCC_RB is an uncommitted placeholder value '1.5SMCxxA'. | 48 | Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch) | J4 pin 11 | J4.11 is tied to DISP_RST (LCD controller reset), but on the MSP4030/LCDwiki 14-pin module pin 11 is CTP_RST (capacitive-touch-panel reset), not LCD_RST (pin 4). | 49 | RGB status indicator (D5) | D5 | Assigned footprint 'Library:LED_IN-P55TATRGB' does not exist: there is no fp-lib-table in the project at all, and no matching .kicad_mod in hardware/libraries. | 50 | netlist | INA228 group (U10,U23,U26,U30,U31,U32,U37,U44) pins 4 & 5 | Board-wide SDA/SCL pin swap: every INA228 wires pin 4 (SDA per TI datasheet) to net I2C_SCL and pin 5 (SCL) to net I2C_SDA. All 8 power monitors would be non-functional (clock on the data pin), breaking the entire monitoring and fault-aggregation subsystem. | Rework the INA228 sub-sheet wiring so pin 4 -> I2C_SDA and pin 5 -> I2C_SCL on all eight parts. | High |
| 51 | netlist | INA_ALERT_3V3, _3V3_GPS, _3V3_STM, _5V_DISP, _OCXO, _VCC_RB, _V_ANT, _V_POE | All 8 INA228 ALERT pins (pin 3, open-drain per datasheet) drive MCP23017 U54 Port B with no external pull-up. | 52 | library | U43 MCP41U83 symbol (hardware/libraries/ntp-server-stm32.kicad_sym, symbol "MCP41U83", pins 1-7) | Symbol pin-number-to-function map disagrees with Microchip DS20007000 TSSOP-14 pinout for pins 1-7. Symbol: 1=VDD,2=SDO/A1,3=SCK/SCL,4=SDI/SDA,5=nCS/A0,6=SPI2C,7=DGND. Datasheet order: 1=CS/A0,2=SDI/SDA,3=DGND,4=SPI2C,5=VDD,6=SDO/A1,7=SCK/SCL. | 53 | library | U62 MX25L25645GM2I-08G symbol (hardware/libraries/ntp-server-stm32.kicad_sym) | VCC pin is defined with an empty pin number (number ""). | 55 | power | L7 (Rb buck inductor, Rb Power sheet / sts1000_bom.csv) | Value column says 40uH but assigned MPN is SRP1265A-6R8M which is a 6.8uH part (identical MPN to L2). MIC28516 adaptive-on-time Rb buck stepping VOUT_P (37-57V) down to ~15V at 6-10W needs a deliberately chosen inductor; 6.8uH vs 40uH changes ripple/saturation/CCM by ~6x. | Recompute the Rb buck inductor for the actual VCC_RB set-point, ripple and peak current, then assign a real MPN whose inductance matches the Value (and satisfies Isat at the 15-20W warm-up surge). Update docs §5 and BOM together. | High |
| 56 | power | R106 + 3V3_STM net | 3V3_STM (the 'always-on housekeeping' rail powering STM32 VDD x5 and all I2C peripherals) is connected to 3V3 ONLY through R106 = 0.5 ohm sense shunt (INA228 U31 0x41 across it). It is NOT a separately-regulated rail, so it cannot be 'always-on independent of the main 3V3'; both collapse together. A 0.5 ohm shunt on the full STM rail also drops ~250mV at 0.5A into the STM32 VDD and burns ~125mW. | Resize the shunt to ~10-25 mohm (matching the rail current for the chosen INA228 ADCRANGE). Separately, correct the docs: 3V3_STM is downstream of 3V3, not independent. If genuine always-on independence (survive 3V3 gating) is required, add a dedicated LDO. The back-power-safety argument in peripheral_map only holds because 3V3 itself is always-on (U29), not because 3V3_STM is separate. | High |
| 57 | power | D7 (VCC_RB TVS, Connectors/Rb) | TVS on the Rb rail is a placeholder MPN '1.5SMCxxA' with no chosen clamp/standoff voltage. | 58 | interfaces | B1: I2C1 / LTC4311 U56 EN + PA9 | U56 ENABLE (pin 3) is hard-tied to 3V3_STM (always enabled). | 59 | interfaces | B2: RMII / LAN8742 U11 config straps | U11 MODE0 (pin8), MODE1 (pin7), MODE2 (pin11=CRS_DV), PHYAD0/RXER (pin10) have NO pull resistor at the PHY pin — they connect only through R31-34 (100 ohm) to the MCU RMII pins, which are high-Z at power-on reset. | 60 | interfaces | B3: Missing footprints on connectors and NOR | J1 (magjack 0826-1X1T-HS-F), J5 USB-C has a footprint but J7/J8/J9 (SMA coax, generic 'Conn_Coaxial'), J6 (FE-5680A housekeeping) and U62 (MX25L25645G NOR) have no assigned footprint. | 62 | interfaces | B6: Net-name / doc drift (non-blocking but fix before layout-freeze) | PB14 net is 'CLK_OUT'-style misnamed '10MHz_CLK_OUT' though it is the EXTREF_MON capture of mux input B; PH0 net is named 'CLK_OUT' for an oscillator input; PE4 net 'RB_RS232_CMOS_SW' vs doc 'RB_SER_MODE'. ### High-risk items (layout may begin only if accepted as risk)

| # | Where | Ref | Issue | Fix | Confidence |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch) | C6,C7,C9,C11 (PoE HV caps) | BOM marks C6 (1nF), C7 (1uF), C9 (1uF), C11 (47pF) as '100V?' with status REVIEW-HV and no MPN. C7/C9 are 0603 X7R 1uF rated only '100V?'; these sit on V_KBIAS/HOLD (VOUT_N+12V) so 100V is likely fine, but C6 is on COSC (NCP1095 osc, low V) yet marked 100V?. Voltage ratings and dielectrics are unconfirmed and parts unsourced. | Pin exact MPN+voltage: COSC C6 can be 16-50V C0G; AUX filter C11 47pF needs >=50V C0G; bias C7/C9 1uF >=50V (16V if truly on +12V bias is marginal-use 50V). Resolve REVIEW-HV before layout. | Medium |
| 2 | PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch) | C8 reference (VPP decouple) | Doc specifies C8 100nF VPP->VPN. Netlist has C8.1=VOUT_P, C8.2=GND(=RTN). RTN!=VPN in the pass-switch-off state (RTN rises to VPP). For the NCP1095 VPP local decouple the RTN(GND) reference is acceptable, but it differs from the documented VPP->VPN. Minor, but confirm intended reference for the input decoupling vs surge return. | Confirm C8 reference: VPP->RTN is the conventional decouple; update doc if RTN is intended, else move to VPN. | Medium |
| 3 | PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch) | R16 / R30 shunts (25m, 150m) | R16 (RSNS 25m, NCP1095 PSNS overcurrent sense) and R30 (150m, INA228 #1 V_POE shunt) are BOM status SHUNT-REVIEW with no MPN and '0.5% per rail TBD'. R16 footprint listed 1206 in BOM but doc/RSNS practice expects a tight-tolerance sense part; R16 value sets NCP1095 ILIM (VOC 1.2V/IOC 6.4A). 25m -> hard-limit ~48A, soft ~6.4A: confirm R16 actually targets the intended current limit for ~30W cold-start. | Select R16 with math: VOC 1.2V/R16 = hard ILIM; size for cold-start inrush+Rb. Select R30 for INA228 full-scale at max PoE input current (Class6 ~1.1A @48V). Assign sense-grade MPN + footprint (2010/1206 Kelvin). | Medium |
| 4 | PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch) | GBR / FDMQ8205A body-diode reversion (doc open item 1) | NCP1095 GBR(11) drives only D1(BAV70 common-cathode), whose anodes steer the U3-U6 N-FET gate-drive bias (via D2/D3). During AUX kill, GBR low must force the FDMQ8205A array (U7/U8) to body-diode rectification so VOUT_P (and V_KBIAS) survives. This is an unverified dynamic behavior of a custom discrete ideal-diode gate-drive; if GBR-low instead collapses the active gates incorrectly it could oscillate offline<->reset. FDMQ8205A is a passive quad-MOSFET array (2x P-ch + 2x N-ch), so correct external gate commutation is essential and must be bench-validated. | Bench-verify GBR-low reverts U7/U8 to body-diode mode with VOUT_P maintained; confirm U3-U6 (BC846BPDW) drive polarity and D2/D3 clamp on the N-FET gates. Document the ideal-diode gate-drive theory of operation. | Low |
| 5 | PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch) | D4 Zener (12V) unsourced | D4 sets V_KBIAS = VOUT_N+12V (bias rail for the kill driver). | 7 | PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch) | Q2 FDMC8622 pass FET — Net-(Q2-S) multi-pad | PSNS(U9.9) and R16 top tie to Q2 pins 1,2,3 (S_1,2,3) and PGATE(U9.10) to Q2 pin4(G); Q2 pins5,6,7,8 (D) to GND/RTN. | 8 | 5V/3V3 main power supply (sheet 3v3-main-power.kicad_sch) | U29 PG / net 3V3_PSU_PG (R94 2.2k, R92 10k) | 3V3 buck Power-Good is unreadable: U29 PG (open-drain, pin2) -> R94 (2.2k) -> 3V3_PSU_PG node -> R92 (10k) -> GND, with MCP23017 U55 GPA4 sensing the node. | 12 | Supercap backup supplies (U34/U35 TPS61094 ×2 + DSF305Q3R0 3F supercaps) | U34/U35 VOUT (C92/C94/C96 and C93/C95/C97) | 3x22uF = 66uF nominal on each VOUT vs TI recommended COUT 20-30uF effective (NOM 20, MAX 30). | 13 | Supercap backup supplies (U34/U35 TPS61094 ×2 + DSF305Q3R0 3F supercaps) | L4 / L5 | Inductor value 2.2uH is correct per datasheet but the BOM line has no MPN, no footprint, no saturation/DCR selection (status SELECT). | Select a 2.2uH inductor from TI's recommended list (e.g. Coilcraft XGL4020-222, Cyntec VCHA042A-2R2) with Isat >> peak (>0.5A is trivial here), assign footprint. | High |
| 14 | Supercap backup supplies (U34/U35 TPS61094 ×2 + DSF305Q3R0 3F supercaps) | U34/U35 EN, MODE | EN and MODE are pulled high to VOUT (100k) rather than to VIN. At cold start VOUT=0 -> EN=MODE=low -> Forced bypass (VOUT=VIN via bypass FET) -> VOUT rises -> EN/MODE pull up -> Auto buck/boost. Self-bootstrapping works, but pulling enable from the rail the part is generating is non-obvious and depends on the bypass-mode cold-start path; also 100k vs the internal 800k pulldown gives only ~0.89xVOUT at the pin. | Verify VIH against the cold-start sequence in SPICE/bench; consider referencing EN/MODE pull-ups to VIN (3V3, always present when board is powered) for an unambiguous enable, or confirm TI's recommended autonomous strap. Confirm 100k meets >800k pull-strength requirement (it does) and VIH at 0.89xVOUT. | Medium |
| 15 | Ethernet magnetics/input (sheet: ethernet-input.kicad_sch) | C1 | SHIELD-to-digital-GND chassis-coupling cap is rated only 16V (4.7nF X7R 0402). This node bridges chassis/cable-shield to board ground and will see ESD/surge/common-mode HV in field use; 16V is grossly under-rated. | Use a high-voltage cap (≥1kV, preferably 2kV like the LAN8742 checklist Cmagterm) in a larger case; keep R1 1M bleed. | High |
| 16 | Ethernet magnetics/input (sheet: ethernet-input.kicad_sch) | U1 | TPD4EUSB30 is a USB-3.0-targeted ESD array (not Ethernet/MDI-qualified, not AEC-Q101). | 22 | MCU core (STM32H563VIT6, U12) | U12 pin14 NRST | NRST connects only to the SWD header J3.5. | 23 | MCU core (STM32H563VIT6, U12) | U12 pin21 VREF+ / U14 MCP1502T-33 / R48 / C37 / C38 | VREF+ decoupling at the MCU pin is only C37 1nF; the 2.2 uF reservoir C38 sits on the far side of series R48 50 ohm (on the MCP1502 OUT). ST recommends 1 uF + 100 nF directly at VREF+. The MCP1502 has a small max direct CL, so the 50 ohm + 2.2 uF is the reference-stability network - but it isolates the bulk charge from the pin. During ADC SAR sampling VREF+ will droop/settle through 50 ohm into 1 nF, degrading ADC accuracy (this MCU steers the OCXO via ADC-sensed Vc, so VREF integrity is timing-critical). | Put the SAR charge-reservoir AT the VREF+ pin: e.g. reference OUT -> small cap -> series R -> 1 uF + 100 nF at VREF+/pin21. Dissipations (B 37 mW, R 48 mW, G 16 mW) are within a 0402's ~63-100 mW rating, so this is not an immediate thermal failure, but it directly contradicts the canonical design and removes the intended margin. | Decide and reconcile: either change R59/R60/R61 footprints to 0603 to match the doc, or update doc §4/§10 to ratify 0402 with the derating math. Keep schematic and doc consistent. | High |
| 59 | RGB status indicator (D5) | D5 | Blue design point is 24.8 mA = the 25 C absolute-max DC forward current; I_F derates to 0 at 80 C T_OP. If the front-panel local ambient is warm, the blue die is over-driven. Doc §7 flags this but it is unverified. | Bench-confirm LED local ambient under worst-case enclosure load; if warm, drop I_blue to ~20 mA and re-derive R59/R60/R61 via the 3:2:1 ratio. | Medium |

## 5. Board-wide netlist findings

## Board-wide Netlist Review — STS1000 "Meridian"

Source: `hardware/ntp-server-stm32/ntp-server-stm32.net` (442 nets, Eeschema 10.0.1 export 2026-06-21T16:28:44). Parsed programmatically (regex extraction of every `(node …)`); no net was skipped. Cross-checked against `docs/ntp_server_peripheral_map.md`, `docs/sts1000_net_naming.md`, `CLAUDE.md` INA map, and TI INA228 datasheet (SLYS178/SBOS… Table 7-2, pinout table).

### Headline result
The four standing actions are essentially DONE/verified, the back-powering hazard is genuinely resolved, **but two real wiring defects survive**: (1) a board-wide INA228 SDA/SCL pin swap (8 parts), and (2) eight INA228 open-drain ALERT lines with no pull-up. Plus three doc-vs-as-built mismatches that will mislead firmware (INA228 address map, U55 Port-B map, missing PIR proximity-wake).

### Standing-action verification
| Action | Result | Evidence |
|---|---|---|
| Drop legacy **R44** at PC12 | DONE — R44 is now a LAN PHY term (3V3_LAN↔TRD0_N), not on PC12. `INA_ALERT_INT_N` has a single pull-up **R199→3V3_STM** on U12.80 (PC12). | netlist R44, R199 |
| **`PG_IN_N`→`PG_INT_N`** rename | DONE — no `PG_IN_N` net exists; `PG_INT_N` = R200.2, U12.69(PA10), U55.15/16. | netlist search |
| INT nets + EXP_RST_N on PA10/PE0/PC12/PC0 | VERIFIED all four: PG_INT_N→**U12.69 PA10**; BTN_INT_N→**U12.97 PE0**; INA_ALERT_INT_N→**U12.80 PC12**; EXP_RST_N→**U12.15 PC0**. | netlist |
| Stale `INA_ALERT_N` 1-pin defect (naming doc §55) | GONE. | netlist search |

### Net-findings table
| Net | Connected pins | Expected | Observed issue | Risk | Fix | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| `I2C_SCL` / `I2C_SDA` (INA228 group) | **All 8 INA228** wire pin 4 (=SDA per datasheet) → `I2C_SCL` and pin 5 (=SCL) → `I2C_SDA`. e.g. U10.4 SDA→I2C_SCL, U10.5 SCL→I2C_SDA; same on U23/U26/U30/U31/U32/U37/U44 | INA228 pin4=SDA→I2C_SDA, pin5=SCL→I2C_SCL (TI datasheet pinout) | **SDA/SCL crossed on every INA228** (symbol pinfunctions are correct, so wiring is wrong). MCU PB9=SDA→I2C_SDA, PB8=SCL→I2C_SCL and MCP23017/TMP117/ATECC are all correct → only the INAs are flipped | **BLOCKER** — all 8 power monitors non-responsive (clock on data pin); breaks the entire monitoring/fault-tree subsystem | Swap the two pins on the INA228 symbol's wiring (or rebuild the INA228 sub-sheet) so pin4→I2C_SDA, pin5→I2C_SCL | FAIL |
| `INA_ALERT_<rail>` ×8 | INA228 pin3 ALERT (open-drain, per datasheet) → MCP23017 U54 Port B only; **no pull-up resistor on any of the 8** | Open-drain ALERT needs a pull-up to be readable | Lines float when de-asserted unless MCP23017 GPPU weak (~100k) pull-ups are enabled in firmware | **WARNING** — works only if firmware sets U54 GPPU on GPB0–7; weak 100k is adequate for static latched flags but undocumented dependency, and ERC-fragile | Either fit 8× ~10k pull-ups to 3V3_STM, or document the mandatory GPPU=1 config in software_spec | WARNING |
| INA228 address straps | U10=GND,GND(0x40) U31=GND,VS(0x41) **U30=GND,SDA(0x42) U32=GND,SCL(0x43)** U23=VS,GND(0x44) U26=VS,VS(0x45) **U37=VS,SCL(0x47) U44=VS,SDA(0x46)** | Doc/CLAUDE map: U30=0x43, U32=0x42, U37=0x46, U44=0x47 | **4 of 8 addresses disagree with docs** (U30↔U32 and U37↔U44 swapped). All 16 unique → no bus collision | **WARNING (doc/FW)** — firmware using the doc map reads 5V_DISP when it expects main-3V3, and OCXO↔Rb swapped | Re-decode against TI Table 7-2; fix either straps or the doc/firmware map so they agree | WARNING |
| `unconnected-(U55-GPB2-Pad27)` | U55.27 GPB2, pintype `bidirectional`, **no `no_connect` flag** (unlike GPB3–7 which carry the flag) | Spare pin should carry a no-connect flag | Inconsistent ERC handling; will throw "input not driven" ERC | **LOW** | Add a no-connect flag on U55 GPB2 | WARNING |
| `INA_ALERT_VCC_RB` | U44.3 ALERT (OD) + **U54.4 GPB7 typed `output`** | MCP23017 GPB7 read as input | Symbol pintype `output` (other ALERT bits are `bidirectional`); KiCad sees two drivers | **LOW** (cosmetic; firmware sets DDR=input) | Set GPB7 symbol pin to bidirectional/input | WARNING |
| `POE_PG` | U9.14 PGO (OD, NCP1095) + U28.24 EN + U55.24 GPA7 (`output`) + **R20 pull-up** | PGO gates buck EN + read by expander | GPA7 typed `output` (cosmetic). PGO pulls buck EN — verify R20 rail/value gives valid EN high | **LOW** | Confirm R20 → correct rail/value; set GPA7 symbol to input | PASS* |
| `3V3` ↔ `3V3_STM` (back-power check) | **R106 is the sense shunt: pin1=`3V3`, pin2=`3V3_STM`**; U31 (INA #2, 0x41) Kelvin-senses across it | All I2C devices on one always-on domain | `3V3_STM` is derived from `3V3` through R106 only — **same always-on rail, not independently gated.** I2C pull-ups (R202/R203) on 3V3_STM; INA228 VS on 3V3 → no gated/always-on split → **no back-power path** | none — claim holds | I2C pull-ups, MCP23017/TMP117/ATECC/e-compass/ADC/NOR/WDT all VDD=3V3_STM; INAs VS=3V3 | PASS |
| Single-pin nets | All 100 single-pin nets are KiCad `unconnected-(…)` no-connect flags; **zero named one-pin-net defects** | No dangling named nets | None | none | — | PASS |
| Exposed pads | EPAD/EP detected: U39.21, U54.29, U55.29 → all **GND**. Bucks U28/U40 use pin33 PGND→GND as pad | EP→GND/thermal | OK at netlist level; physical EP presence on U28/U40 (MIC28516) is a footprint-review item | none | verify EP pads in footprints | PASS |
| Outputs shorted | `VOUT_P`/`VOUT_N` (U7/U8 parallel FDMQ8205A bridges), `GPS_VBAT`/`STM_VBAT` (U34/U35 dual VOUT pins) — all intentional parallels | — | No genuine output-output conflicts | none | — | PASS |

\*PASS pending R20 rail/value confirmation.

### Design-intent mismatches
| Ref | Doc says | Schematic says | Severity |
|---|---|---|---|
| peripheral_map §159 (U55 PortB) | [0]V_ANT_EN_FAULT, [1]freed, [2]V_DISP_EN_FAULT, [3]**PROX_WAKE (PIR)**, [4–7] spare | GPB0=V_ANT_EN_FAULT, **GPB1=V_DISP_EN_FAULT** (doc says [1] freed/[2] V_DISP), GPB2=unconnected, **GPB3=unconnected** | Medium — bit map shifted; firmware bit definitions wrong |
| peripheral_map §159/§411, §287 | PIR **proximity wake** on U55 PortB[3] = secondary wake source | **No PROX_WAKE / PIR / WAKE net exists anywhere**; GPB3 unconnected | Medium — documented feature not implemented in schematic |
| CLAUDE INA map / peripheral_map §157 | U30=0x43 main3V3, U32=0x42 5V_DISP, U37=0x46 OCXO, U44=0x47 Rb | straps decode U30=0x42, U32=0x43, U37=0x47, U44=0x46 | Medium — FW addresses wrong rail |

### Items confirmed clean (no action)
- No `3V3_P` rail remnant (only `3V3_PSU_PG`, a power-good signal name — fine).
- Net naming consistent with `sts1000_net_naming.md`: `INA_ALERT_<rail>` intentionally has no `_N` (doc §18); `MCU_NRST` intentionally ST-named (§15); `GPS_EXTINT` is active-high so no `_N`.
- ATECC608B U56 BUS1=SCL→I2C_SCL, BUS2=SDA→I2C_SDA (correct). MCP23017 U54/U55 SCK→I2C_SCL, SDA→I2C_SDA (correct). TMP117 U57/U58 correct. The INA228 group is the *only* device family with swapped I2C.
- INA228 addresses, even after the swaps, are all unique (0x40,0x41,0x42,0x43,0x44,0x45,0x46,0x47) — no bus collision.

### Open verification I could not close from the netlist
- TI INA228 **Table 7-2** address decode confirmed by family convention (base 0x40; A1/A0 ∈ GND/VS/SDA/SCL) but the PDF table could not be rendered in this environment (no `pdftoppm`). The 0x40/0x41/0x44/0x45 rows match both straps and doc, anchoring the decode; the 0x42/0x43/0x46/0x47 swap conclusion follows. Confirm against datasheet page 19 before edits.
- R20 value/rail on `POE_PG` (EN pull-up for buck U28) not value-verified here.

Sources: [TI INA228 datasheet](https://www.ti.com/lit/ds/symlink/ina228.pdf) (pinout: pin4=SDA, pin5=SCL, pin3=ALERT open-drain; Table 7-2 address map).

## 7. IC-by-IC review (grouped by subsystem)


### PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)  —  _verdict: Blocked_

## PoE Front End + Power Tree Input — Pre-Layout Review (sheet `PoE.kicad_sch`)

**Verdict: BLOCKED.** Three blockers: (1) the documented POE_KILL self-sustaining kill network is miswired — `KILL_N` has no pull-up and Q3/R21 are connected differently from the canonical design, so default-RUN and the AUX-actuated cold-cycle are indeterminate; (2) the mandated input surge TVS (SMBJ58A across VPP→VPN) is absent — D1 is a BAV70 used for GBR steering, not the bus clamp; (3) the INA228 I2C bus is crossed (clock on SDA pin, data on SCL pin) on U10 and every other INA228.

Architecture confirmed correct in principle: FDMQ8205A (U7/U8) is a **passive quad-MOSFET array** (2× P-ch + 2× N-ch), so the discrete ideal-diode gate-drive (U3–U6 BC846BPDW + D2/D3 6.8V arrays) is legitimate; NCP1095 (U9) drives an **external** pass FET (Q2 FDMC8622) via PGATE/PSNS; RDET 26.1k (R15) and Class 6 (RCLASSA 232 R13 / RCLASSB 909 R14) match the datasheet-cited doc and satisfy the "Type 2 min / Type 3 margin" requirement.

#### IC / active-device-by-IC
| RefDes | MPN | Function | Datasheet | Package | Symbol pinout verified | Footprint verified | Power/Gnd pins | Strap/EN/RST pins | Required passives | Layout-critical notes | Status | Conf |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| U7 | FDMQ8205A | Ideal-diode bridge #1 (pairs VC1/VC2) | onsemi fdmq8205a-d | 12-MLP (16-pad array; embedded sym `FDMQ8205A_1`) | Yes — INPUT1=13/14, INPUT2=15/16, OUTP=5-8, OUTN=2/3/10/11, G1=1,G2=4,G3=9,G4=12 | Footprint prop="12-MLP" (generic string, not a lib path) — must confirm exact onsemi 12-MLP land + exposed pad | OUTP→VOUT_P, OUTN→VOUT_N | Gates externally driven (U3/U4) | U3,U4 (BC846 drivers), TR0/TR1 taps | High AC current; place at magjack; gate-drive loops short; 100V VDS | WARNING | High |
| U8 | FDMQ8205A | Ideal-diode bridge #2 (pairs VC3/VC4) | same | 12-MLP | Yes (same as U7) | Same caveat as U7 | OUTP→VOUT_P, OUTN→VOUT_N | Gates ext (U5/U6) | U5,U6, TR2/TR3 taps | Same | WARNING | High |
| U9 | NCP1095DBR2 | 802.3bt PD interface controller, external FET | onsemi ncp1095-d (Rev2) | 16-TSSOP | Yes — VPP1,CLA2,CLB3,AUX4,COSC5,ACS6,DET7,VPN8,PSNS9,PGATE10,GBR11,RTN12,LCF13,PGO14,NCM15,NCL16 (matches web) | TSSOP-16 generic — confirm | VPP→VOUT_P, VPN/RTN | AUX(kill), PGO(buck EN), ACS→VPN (autoclass off) | R13/R14/R15, Q2, R16, C6 | RTN floats to VPP off-state; keep PSNS Kelvin to R16 | WARNING (kill net miswire upstream) | High |
| U10 | INA228AQDGSRQ1 | PoE-input power monitor #1 (0x40) | TI ina228-q1 | VSSOP-10 DGS (lib `INA228AQDGSRQ1`) | Yes — A1=1,A0=2,ALERT=3,SDA=4,SCL=5,VS=6,GND=7,VBUS=8,IN-=9,IN+=10 | DGS-10 | VS→3V3, GND→GND | A0,A1→GND (=0x40); ALERT→GPB0 | R30 shunt (VOUT_P→V_POE) | I2C crossed (see below); shunt Kelvin | FAIL (SDA/SCL swap) | High |

### 5V/3V3 main power supply (sheet 3v3-main-power.kicad_sch)  —  _verdict: Blocked_

## 5V / 3V3 Main Power Supply — Pre-Layout Review

Sheet: `hardware/ntp-server-stm32/3v3-main-power.kicad_sch`. Two switchers: **U28 MIC28516T-E/PHA** (PoE/VOUT_P → 5V, 8A) and **U29 AP3441SHE-7B** (5V → 3V3, 3A). Three **INA228** rail monitors (U30/U31/U32) and one **RT9742** display load switch (U33). FB output-voltage math is **correct** (MIC28516/AP3441 Vref = 0.6 V, verified). Two board-killing defects block layout: a scrambled AP3441 symbol pin map and a board-wide I²C SDA/SCL swap.

### Supercap backup supplies (U34/U35 TPS61094 ×2 + DSF305Q3R0 3F supercaps)  —  _verdict: Needs corrections_

## Supercap backup supplies — pre-layout review

Two independent TPS61094 bi-directional buck/boost supercap managers: **U34** backs up the ZED-F9T `V_BCKP` (GPS ephemeris/RTC), **U35** backs up the STM32H563 `VBAT`. Each is fed from main **3V3** (VIN), charges a **3F DSF305Q3R0** supercap on its SUP pin through a 2.2 µH inductor, and holds its VOUT during a 3V3 loss. Config is fully strapped/autonomous (no MCU control lines), exactly as the masters intend. The topology is sound and self-bootstrapping, but several items must be fixed before layout.

Datasheet: TI **TPS61094** SLVSFH6C (Dec 2021), https://www.ti.com/lit/ds/symlink/tps61094.pdf. Supercap: Cornell Dubilier **DSF305Q3R0**, 3 F / **3.0 V**, radial, 3.5 mm pin pitch, https://www.cde.com/resources/catalogs/DSF.pdf.

#### Strap decode (verified vs datasheet Tables 7-1/7-2/7-3/7-4)
| Pin | Strap (U34 / U35) | Net | Decode | Result | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| OSEL (1) | R116 / R117 = 3.09 k → GND | Net-(U34/35-OSEL) | Table 7-1: 3.09 k | **VOUT_REG = 3.0 V** | PASS |
| VCHG (12) | R112 / R113 = 6.65 k → GND | Net-(U34/35-VCHG) | Table 7-2: 6.65 k | **Charge term = 2.5 V** | PASS (safe for 3.0 V cap) |
| ICHG (11) | R114 / R115 = 9.53 k → GND | Net-(U34/35-ICHG) | Table 7-3: 9.53 k | **Charge I = 25 mA** | PASS |
| EN (3) | R108 / R109 = 100 k → **VOUT** | Net-(U34/35-EN) | high | enabled | WARNING (see note) |
| MODE (2) | R110 / R111 = 100 k → **VOUT** | Net-(U34/35-MODE) | high | Auto buck/boost | WARNING (see note) |

EN/MODE both high ⇒ **Auto buck/boost** (Table 7-4): when VIN(3.3 V) > VOUT_target(3.0 V)+100 mV the buck charges the supercap and VOUT≈VIN via bypass; when VIN fails the boost holds VOUT=3.0 V from the supercap. Normal `V_BCKP`/`VBAT` ≈ 3.3 V (bypass), backup ≈ 3.0 V — inside STM32H5 VBAT (1.65–3.6 V) and ZED-F9T V_BCKP (1.4–3.6 V) ranges.

#### IC-by-IC
| RefDes | MPN | Function | Datasheet | Package | Symbol pinout | Footprint | Pwr/Gnd | Strap/EN/RST | Required passives | Layout-critical | Status | Conf |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| U34 | TPS61094DSSR | GPS V_BCKP supercap mgr | SLVSFH6C | WSON-12 DSS 3.0×2.0×0.8 + EP | PASS (1 OSEL…13 EP match Table 5-1) | `SON50P300X200X80-13N` in libraries/ — **fp-lib-table empty, nickname won't resolve** | VIN=3V3(4); PGND7/AGND8/EP13=GND ✓ | EN/MODE→VOUT 100k; OSEL/VCHG/ICHG 1% to GND ✓ | L4 2.2µH (SW–SUP); C90 3F (SUP); C92/C94/C96 3×22µF VOUT | EP thermal vias; keep SW loop tight; supercap thermal ≤75 °C | WARNING | High |
| U35 | TPS61094DSSR | STM32 VBAT supercap mgr | SLVSFH6C | same | PASS | same fp issue | VIN=3V3(4); GND ✓ | EN/MODE→VOUT 100k; OSEL/VCHG/ICHG 1% to GND ✓ | L5 2.2µH; C91 3F; C93/C95/C97 3×22µF VOUT | same | WARNING | High |

|---|---|---|---|
| Inductor L4/L5 | 2.2 µH | 1 or 2.2 µH (eff 0.7–2.86 µH) | Value PASS; **no MPN/footprint selected** (BOM "SELECT") |
| COUT (VOUT) | 3×22 µF X7R 0805 = 66 µF nom | **20–30 µF effective (NOM 20, MAX 30)** | **WARNING: exceeds recommended max even after DC-bias derate (~45–50 µF eff)** |
| CIN (VIN) | none local; shares 3V3 plane bulk | ≥2.2 µF effective at VIN pin | WARNING: add local VIN cap at each IC for layout |
| CSUP | DSF305Q3R0 3 F (the supercap) | ≥2.2 µF | PASS (supercap is the SUP cap) |
| Config R accuracy | ERJ-2RKF = 1% | 1% required, <10 pF parasitic | PASS |

#### Layout-critical constraints
| Net/class | Current est | Width/notes | Placement / return | Evidence |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| SW (U34/35 ↔ L4/L5) | peak ~0.3–0.5 A (pre-charge 300 mA) | short, wide; minimize loop area | keep SW–L–SUP–IC loop tight; EP thermal vias | DS §10 layout, §7.3.2 |
| Supercap (SUP, C90/C91) | 25 mA charge, backup boost current | radial can, 3.5 mm pitch | **place ≤75 °C** away from OCXO oven/Rb/bucks/PoE mag | CLAUDE.md; DSF datasheet 3.0V/65–85°C life |
| VOUT → V_BCKP / VBAT | µA backup, ~mA charge bypass | moderate | local 22–33µF near IC | DS COUT 20–30µF |
| VIN (3V3) | shared plane | add local ≥2.2µF | — | DS CIN 2.2µF |

#### Design-intent mismatches
| Ref | Doc says | Schematic says | Severity |
|---|---|---|---|
| PA6 / PB1 SOC sense | peripheral_map §lines 265–266: "/2 divider" on both | Direct connection to SUP node, **no divider** | Medium (firmware scaling) |
| peripheral_map §14 open item L398 | "TPS61094 MODE/EN truth table & auto-backup behavior (TI datasheet)" — unverified | Verified: EN/MODE→VOUT = Auto buck/boost, self-bootstrapping | Low (close the open item) |
| Backup output level | CLAUDE.md elsewhere frames TPS61094 generically; this block gives 3.0 V boost target / 3.3 V bypass | OSEL=3.0 V confirmed | Low (document the 3.0 V value) |

#### Backup hold-time vs ephemeris window (requested)
Usable energy per 3 F cap from 2.5 V (VCHG) to ~1.4 V (F9T V_BCKP floor): E≈½·3·(2.5²−1.4²)=**6.4 J**. At V_BCKP ~45 µA (25 °C) → hold ≈ tens of hours; even with temperature-elevated leakage and the 3.0 V boost floor, well beyond the ZED-F9T **~4 h ephemeris validity**. **Hold time is adequate** (supercap is, if anything, generously sized). Confidence Medium (V_BCKP current at max enclosure temp still an open datasheet item per CLAUDE.md).

#### Balancing / charge
Single cell per converter (not a series stack) → **no cell balancing required**; VCHG=2.5 V is the hard charge ceiling and is below the 3.0 V cap rating. Charge current 25 mA → 0→2.5 V on 3 F ≈ 5–6 min after the pre-charge phase. OK.

### Ethernet magnetics/input (sheet: ethernet-input.kicad_sch)  —  _verdict: Needs corrections_

## Ethernet magnetics / input — pre-layout review

Sheet `ethernet-input.kicad_sch`. Devices of significance: **J1** Bel 0826-1X1T-HS-F integrated MagJack, **U1** TI TPD4EUSB30 4-ch ESD array, plus passives R1/C1/C2. (R42–R45 49.9Ω MDI pull-ups, FB1, and U11 LAN8742 itself live on the *Ethernet PHY* sheet but terminate on this sheet's nets, so they are cross-checked here.)

### Headline result
The MDI termination topology is **correct** and matches the Microchip LAN8742A schematic checklist (SC471240) Figures 1/2 and the integrated-magnetics notes. The chosen magjack (0826-1X1T-HS-F) has the **Bob-Smith termination built in** (internal 4×75Ω + 1000pF/2kV to SHIELD — confirmed on the Bel drawing schematic page), so no external 75Ω/1nF-2kV network is needed and its absence on this sheet is *not* a defect. The real blockers are **missing footprints** (J1, U1) and a **symbol-library-variant mismatch** for J1, plus an ESD-part-suitability and a chassis-cap-rating concern.

### IC / active-device-by-IC
| RefDes | MPN | Function | Datasheet | Package | Symbol pinout verified | Footprint verified | Power/Gnd pins | Strap/EN/RST | Required passives | Layout-critical notes | Status | Confidence |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| J1 | Bel **0826-1X1T-HS-F** (gigabit MagJack, PoEp/100W, ext-temp) | Integrated RJ45 + 4× 1CT:1CT magnetics + internal Bob-Smith (4×75Ω + 1000pF/2kV) + 2 LEDs | Bel dr-mag-0826-1x1t-hs-f.pdf (PN 08261X1THS-F, schematic pg "PAGE 2") | THT magjack, 20 sig pins + S1/S2 shield (drawing pg 4 footprint) | YES — symbol pin **names** match datasheet (TRD1±/TRCT1 …, VC1–4, LEDs 17–20, SHIELD S1/S2) | **NO — Footprint field is empty** (symbol default `0826-1X1T-GH-F:BEL_0826-1X1T-GH-F` is overridden blank; no fp-lib-table entry) | Pin 6/12 TRCT1/2→3V3_LAN; pin13–16 VC1–4 = PoE taps | none (auto-MDIX magjack) | internal term; ext R1/C1 chassis-couple, C2 0.022µF CT bypass | Place at board edge; chassis (S1/S2) to chassis-GND island; route MDI 100Ω diff under the part with plane clear-out ~half-way through magnetics; HIPOT 2250VDC isolation barrier keep-out under part | **FAIL** (no footprint) | High |

### Ethernet PHY (LAN8742AI-CZ-TR) — sheet ethernet-phy.kicad_sch  —  _verdict: Needs corrections_

## Ethernet PHY (U11 LAN8742AI-CZ-TR) — Pre-Layout Review

**Verdict: Needs corrections.** Core RMII wiring, strap configuration (REF_CLK-Out mode), supply split, terminations, and decoupling are all correct and datasheet-verified. Two layout blockers (Y1 and J1 have no footprint), one questionable ESD placement (U1), and minor doc/rail nits. No electrical blockers.

#### IC-by-IC

| RefDes | MPN | Function | Datasheet | Package | Symbol pinout verified | Footprint verified | Power/Gnd pins | Strap/EN/RST pins | Required passives | Layout-critical notes | Status | Conf |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|

### MCU core (STM32H563VIT6, U12)  —  _verdict: Needs corrections_

## MCU Core Review — U12 STM32H563VIT6 (LQFP-100), sheet `stm32.kicad_sch`

Connectivity verified from the netlist (`ntp-server-stm32.net`), values/footprints from the netlist + `sts1000_bom.csv`, symbol/footprint from `hardware/libraries/STM32H563VIT6.kicad_sym` and `LQFP-100_STM.kicad_mod`. External truth from ST AN5711 / STM32H562/563 datasheet.

**Verdict: Needs corrections.** Power architecture, decoupling, oscillator, VCAP, and all documented signal-pin mappings are correct. Two layout-blocking items (BOOT0 divider, unresolved footprint) and two reliability items (no NRST cap, weak VREF+ reservoir) must be fixed.

#### IC-by-IC

| RefDes | MPN | Function | Datasheet | Package | Symbol pinout verified | Footprint verified | Power/Gnd pins | Strap/EN/RST pins | Required passives | Layout-critical notes | Status | Conf |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| U12 | STM32H563VIT6 | Cortex-M33 MCU | ST DS (sym links H562 in error) | LQFP-100 14×14 0.5mm, no EP | Yes — 100 pins, no PE1/PB11 (correctly absent) | Footprint geometry OK but **instance name "100-LQFP" does not resolve** | VDD ×5 (11/28/50/75/100)→3V3_STM; VSS ×5 (10/27/49/74/99)+VSSA(19)+VREF-(20)→GND; VDDA(22)←U13 LDO; VREF+(21)←U14; VBAT(6)←backup; VDDUSB(73)←3V3_STM_USB; VCAP(48,98) | NRST(14), BOOT0(94), no other straps | VCAP 2.2µF×2 (C34/C36) ✓; VDDA 10µF+0.1µF (C32/C100) ✓; per-VDD 0.1µF ×12 (C168-C181) + 220nF C176 + 1µF C182 ✓; OSC32 12pF×2 ✓; BOOT0 R49/R50 ✗; VREF+ C37 1nF ⚠; NRST cap missing ⚠ | Place decoupling at pins; VCAP caps must be ceramic w/ correct ESR; VREF+ low-Z to pin | **WARNING** | High |
| U14 | MCP1502T-33E/CHY | 3.3 V series VREF for ADC | Microchip DS20006593 | SOT-23-6 | OUT1/GND2/GND3/EN4/GND5/VDD6 per BOM | SOT-23-6 (KiCad std) | VDD(6)←5V, GND(2/3/5) | EN(4)←Q6 collector (enabled by 5V_PSU good) | OUT→C37/R48/C38; in-path R48 50Ω + C38 2.2µF | Max direct CL limited; series-R reservoir rule (DS §5.1.2) — reservoir is on wrong side of R48 | WARNING | Medium |

### External watchdog (U64 TPS3430, WDT sheet)  —  _verdict: Needs corrections_

## External Watchdog — Pre-Layout Review (U64 TPS3430WDRC)

Schematic sheet: `hardware/ntp-server-stm32/wdt.kicad_sch`. Canonical doc: `docs/sts1000_external_wdt.md`. Datasheet: TI TPS3430 SBVS366 (extracted full text from `ti.com/lit/ds/symlink/tps3430.pdf`).

**Headline:** Core watchdog wiring is correct and matches the datasheet (pinout, VDD1=VDD2 tie, SET0 high, SET1=WDT_EN with R213 boot-disable pulldown, WDO open-drain with R23 10k pull-up, CWD/CRST floated for the 920–1360 ms factory window, tRST 200 ms). Two real defects: (1) **WDI/WDT_KICK has no external pull resistor** — the datasheet explicitly forbids floating WDI in the disabled state; the doc's claimed pulldown "R169" belongs to a different circuit (Rb IO transistor base) and has the wrong value. (2) Several doc designator claims (R169 WDI pulldown; fallback U62/D17/C145) are stale and contradict the netlist. No layout blockers; the WDI pulldown should be added before layout so a pad exists.

#### IC-by-IC

| RefDes | MPN | Function | Datasheet | Package | Symbol pinout verified | Footprint verified | Power/Gnd pins | Strap/EN/RST pins | Required passives | Layout-critical notes | Status | Confidence |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| U64 | TPS3430WDRC (orderable TPS3430WDRCR) | Standalone window watchdog → POE_KILL cold-cycle | TI SBVS366 | VSON-10 DRC 3×3 mm, EP internally GND | YES — symbol pins 1..11 = VDD1/CWD/SET0/CRST/GND/SET1/WDI/WDO/NC/VDD2/GND match DS §Pin Functions (p.5, lines 135–208) | Footprint `Package_SON:VSON-10-1EP_3x3mm_P0.5mm_EP1.65x2.4mm` = standard KiCad lib; DRC EP nominal ~1.65×2.4 mm matches DS land pattern | VDD1(1)+VDD2(10)→3V3_STM (net code 9, with C180/C181); GND(5)+GND(11)/EP→GND | SET0(3)=3V3_STM tied high; SET1(6)=WDT_EN(PA9) + R213 100k pulldown; CWD(2)=NC float; CRST(4)=NC float; NC(9)=no_connect | C180/C181 0.1µF VDD bypass; R23 10k WDO pull-up; R213 100k SET1 pulldown; **MISSING WDI pulldown** | EP to large GND plane (DS p.6); no copper fill under CWD/CRST (preset eval); R23 close to pin 8; C180 close to VDD1 | WARNING | High |

#### Netlist findings

| Net | Connected pins | Expected | Observed issue | Risk | Fix | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| WDT_KICK (code 339) | U12 PB2(37), U64 WDI(7) | WDI driven + defined-level pull (doc §3/§5: R169 100k pulldown) | **No pull resistor present.** WDI relies solely on PB2. DS pin-fn (line 195): "If the watchdog is disabled, then WDI cannot be left unconnected and must be driven to either VDD or GND." No internal pull on WDI. | Low–Med: during the pre-GPIO-config boot instant PB2 is Hi-Z → WDI floats. WDT is also disabled then (SET1 low via R213), and DS says WDI is ignored while disabled, so functional risk is small — but it violates DS guidance and leaves an undefined node. | Add a pulldown (100k per doc, or any 10k–100k) from WDT_KICK to GND near U64 pin 7. Assign it a real refdes (NOT R169 — that's taken). | FAIL |
| WDT_EN (code 338) | U12 PA9(68), U64 SET1(6), R213 pin1 (pin2→GND) | PA9 push-pull + 100k pulldown → boots disabled | None — correct | — | — | PASS |
| WDO_N (code 337) | U64 WDO(8), R23 pin1 (pin2→3V3) + thermal/OV-latch wire-OR | open-drain + pull-up to 3V3 | None — R23 10k in DS 1k–100k range (line 197/278). Verify the other two open-collector sources actually land on this net on their sheets (out of scope here). | — | Confirm thermal-cutoff + Rb-OV-latch O-C outputs join WDO_N (doc §6) | PASS |
| 3V3_STM (code 9) | U64 VDD1(1), VDD2(10), SET0(3) + many | VDD1=VDD2 tied; SET0 high | None — DS line 205/604: VDD1/VDD2 not internally connected, must be tied; both on 3V3_STM. SET0 high = correct for enable mode. | — | — | PASS |
| unconnected-(U64-CWD-Pad2) (code 434) | U64 CWD(2) | NC float → factory window | Correct (float). | — | Keep-out, no fill under pin 2 | PASS |
| unconnected-(U64-CRST-Pad4) (code 433) | U64 CRST(4) | NC float → tRST 200 ms | Correct (float). | — | Keep-out, no fill under pin 4 | PASS |
| unconnected-(U64-NC-Pad9) (code 435) | U64 NC(9) | float | Correct (DS line 203: must float). | — | — | PASS |

### GNSS receiver (ZED-F9T) — U21 ZED-F9T-00B, U22 LT3045 LDO, U23 INA228 @0x44  —  _verdict: Needs corrections_

## GNSS Receiver (ZED-F9T) — Pre-Layout Review

Scope: `gps.kicad_sch` (U21 ZED-F9T-00B, U22 LT3045 GPS LDO, U23 INA228 @0x44) + cross-sheet RF/backup nets. Connectivity taken from `ntp-server-stm32.net`; values/footprints from the sheet; pins/nets cross-checked against `docs/ntp_server_peripheral_map.md`.

**Verdict: Needs corrections.** Two blockers on the U22 LT3045 power-good circuit; one high-risk INA228 address-strap rail mismatch; pin mapping to the STM32 is otherwise correct and matches the peripheral map.

#### IC-by-IC

|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|

### GNSS antenna bias + supervisor (gps-antenna.kicad_sch)  —  _verdict: Needs corrections_

## GNSS Antenna Bias + Supervisor — Pre-Layout Review

Scope: `gps-antenna.kicad_sch` (sheet `/GPS Antenna/`, UUID c4e88dde…). Verified against netlist `ntp-server-stm32.net`, doc `gnss_antenna_bias_supervisor.md`, masters, and external datasheets. Reference-by-designator/pin throughout.

### Headline findings
1. **U27 RT9742 load switch is undocumented and the ordered MPN (RT9742VGJ5) does NOT match the schematic symbol pinout** — the canonical doc describes no such device; the symbol is the standard-pinout `RT9742GGJ5` but the BOM part is the M/V-variant which has a different pin map and **no FLG pin**. This is a layout blocker.
2. **L1 value disagreement:** schematic/BOM = **47 nH** (LQG15HS47NJ02D); doc body §3/§8 say **56 nH**. CLAUDE.md says 47 nH. Affects bias-T choke impedance math.
3. **R89 shunt value/MPN mismatch:** value field `100m` vs MPN `KDV08DR150ET` = **0.15 Ω**.
4. **U26 INA228 ALERT (INA_ALERT_V_ANT) has no discrete pull-up** — relies on MCP23017 weak internal pull-up.
5. **Default-state conflict:** new U27 EN (ANT_BIAS_EN, R88 10k pull-down) defaults the antenna **OFF** at power-up, contradicting doc §7's "antenna defaults ON when F9T pin undriven" rationale (which only governs the downstream Q13/Q14 stage).

### Actual as-built topology (from netlist)
`5V → U27 (RT9742 load switch, EN=ANT_BIAS_EN/PC9) → R89 0.15Ω shunt (sensed by U26 INA228 #4 @0x45) → FB6 → V_ANT rail`. V_ANT then feeds: (a) FB4 → R77 3.3Ω → Q11 E→C (PNP pass + Q12 foldback) → L1 → node A → antenna; (b) the Q13/Q14 ANT_OFF disable stage. INA181 U24 senses across R77 (DETECT leg, U25A); node-A÷2 divider → U25B (SHORT leg). This is materially different from the doc, which shows V_ANT going straight into the Q11/Q12 limiter with no upstream load switch or second shunt.

#### IC-by-IC
| RefDes | MPN | Function | Datasheet | Package | Symbol pinout verified | Footprint verified | Power/Gnd | Strap/EN/RST | Required passives | Layout-critical | Status | Conf |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|

#### Notes / verified-OK
- Q11 (NSS40300MZ4) SOT-223 pin order **1=B,2=C,3=E,tab=C** confirmed (onsemi DS) and matches the BCP51 symbol used + netlist; tab on collector (node A) is acceptable thermally.
- INA181 input orientation correct (IN+ on V_ANT/upstream side of R77), REF=GND unidirectional.
- LMV393 on 5V gives Vicr 0…~4.2V — spans all supervisor inputs; OC outputs to 3V3_GPS are fail-safe.
- I²C SCL/SDA, address straps, supervisor pull-ups, PD4/PC9 mapping all verified against masters.

### OCXO + steering supply (Y3 OH300, U39 TPS7A52 LDO, U38 AP3441 buck, U36 OPA320 Vc buffer, U37 INA228 #5)  —  _verdict: Blocked_

## OCXO + Steering Supply — Pre-Layout Review

Signal chain reconstructed from netlist: **5V → U38 AP3441 buck (≈3.70 V, Net-(D10-K)) → D10 BAT54J → U39 TPS7A52 LDO (≈3.33 V, Net-(D10-A)) → R126 25 mΩ shunt (U37 INA228 high-side) → Y3 OH300 VCC (3.3 V)**. Steering: **PA4/DAC1_OUT1 (OCXO_VC) → R120 100k → U36 OPA320 +IN (loop filter w/ C98, R121 10M, R118/R119/C99 1.65 V bias) → unity buffer → R122 1k → C101 → Y3 Vcontrol (OCXO_V) → PA3 sense (U12.26)**. OCXO output Y3.4 → R123 22Ω → OCXO_CLK_OUT → U52.3 (clock mux I0).

Two functional blockers found (INA228 wrong address strap; AP3441 PG enable chain with no pull-up), plus a project-rule violation (every Vc-path cap is X7R, not C0G/NP0) and an unverifiable custom AP3441 symbol pinout.

#### IC-by-IC

| RefDes | MPN | Function | Datasheet | Package | Symbol pinout verified | Footprint verified | Power/Gnd pins | Strap/EN/RST pins | Required passives | Layout-critical notes | Status | Confidence |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| Y3 | OH300-61003CV-010.0M | 10 MHz 3.3 V CMOS VCOCXO | conwin cx210 (symbol points to wrong cx282/100 MHz sine) | 7-pad SMD (Oscillator_SMD_OCXO_ConnorWinfield_OH300) | Yes — p1 Vcontrol, p3 VCC, p4 OUT, p7 GND; p2/5/6 NC | Lib FP name matches; pad map not opened | VCC=p3 (Net-(U37-IN-)), GND=p7 | n/a | C105 10µF+C106 10nF on VCC; C101 0.1µF on Vc | Oven draws high warmup current; place INA shunt R126 in VCC; keep Vc trace short/guarded | WARNING | Medium |

#### Layout-critical constraints for this block

| Net/class | Current est | Width/impedance | Placement/return-path | Evidence |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| OCXO VCC (Net-(D10-A)/U37-IN-/Y3.3) | OCXO oven warmup high (OH300 warmup ~ up to ~1 A region, steady hundreds mA) | Wide pour; Kelvin across R126 shunt | INA228 R126 directly in series; keep shunt-sense traces Kelvin/differential | OH300 oven, INA228 datasheet sense layout |
| Vc / OCXO_V (Y3.1) | µA | High-Z node; guard ring | Short trace OPA320→R122→Y3.1; keep away from switching nodes; C0G/film caps only | CLAUDE.md hard rule; OPA320 ds |
| U38 buck hot loop VIN-LX-L6-Cout | ≤3 A pulsed | Minimize loop area; star PGND to EP | C102-104 in at U38; L6/Cout tight; switching noise away from Vc/OCXO | AP3441 ds layout |
| OCXO_CLK_OUT (Y3.4→R123→U52.3) | CMOS 10 MHz | 50Ω-ish controlled; R123 at driver | Series term at OCXO; route to mux as quiet clock; reference GND | sts1000_clock_mux.md |
| EP thermals U38/U39 | — | Multiple thermal vias under EP | U39 LDO dissipates (3.70−3.33)×I; U38 buck losses | TPS7A52 / AP3441 ds |

| Ref | Doc says | Schematic says | Severity |
|---|---|---|---|
| U37 INA228 | OCXO INA228 = 0x46 (peripheral_map, CLAUDE.md INA map) | Strapped A1=VS/A0=SCL = 0x47 (= Rb U44) | High (blocker) |
| Vc-path caps | "C0G/NP0 or film — NEVER X7R" (CLAUDE.md, hardware/CLAUDE.md) | C98, C99, C101 all GRM155R71C104 = X7R | High |
| Loop-filter scaling | "scale DAC 0–3.3 V to ±0.4 ppm, set loop τ" (peripheral_map §14) | Unity buffer → Vc = full 0–3.3 V (R121 10M bias negligible); no ±0.4 ppm attenuator | Medium (open item, but resolution/holdover impact) |
| Y3 symbol datasheet | OH300-61003CV 10 MHz CMOS (cx210) | Symbol Datasheet = cx282.pdf / "100 MHz Sinewave OCXO"; Description says 100 MHz sine | Low (doc hygiene; BOM/MPN correct) |
| AP3441 symbol | (no doc pinout) | Custom CM5IO pinout conflicts with LCSC pin table | High (must verify before layout) |

### Clock mux (OCXO/ext-ref -> PH0)  —  _verdict: Needs corrections_

## Clock mux (OCXO/ext-ref -> PH0) - Pre-layout review

Scope: `clock-mux.kicad_sch` (U52 74LVC1G157GW-Q100H selector, U53 74LVC1G34 fanout buffer, R187/R188/R189, C157/C158/C159/C160, FB10). Connectivity verified against `ntp-server-stm32.net`; values/PNs against `sts1000_bom.csv`; intent against `sts1000_clock_mux.md`.

**Bottom line:** Electrical design and connectivity are correct and match the canonical doc (select polarity, R188 default-OCXO pulldown, source-termination at drivers only, Y-node fanout tap before R187, per-pin decoupling, GND on U52 pin 2 only, U53 NC properly unconnected). **Two hard blockers stop layout:** U52 footprint is the wrong package for the GW MPN, and U53 has no footprint at all. Plus several MPN/grade/doc deltas.

#### IC-by-IC

| RefDes | MPN | Function | Datasheet | Package (DS) | Symbol pinout verified | Footprint verified | Power/Gnd | Strap/EN/RST | Required passives | Layout-critical notes | Status | Conf |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| U52 | 74LVC1G157GW-Q100H | 2:1 clock selector (Schmitt in, IOFF, AEC-Q100) | Nexperia 74LVC1G157_Q100 Rev.6 2025-09-09 | **SOT363-2 / TSSOP6, 1.25 mm body, 0.65 mm pitch** | YES: 1=I1,2=GND,3=I0,4=Y,5=VCC,6=S matches DS | **FAIL - SOT457 fp (0.95 mm pitch) on a SOT363 part** | VCC=5 (3V3_CLK), GND=2 | S=6 (MUX_SEL/PB6), R188 100k pulldown -> default I0/OCXO | C158 0.1uF at pin5; series R187 22R at Y | Place adjacent to PH0; keep Y->R187->CLK_OUT short over continuous GND | **FAIL** | High |
| U53 | 74LVC1G34 (doc: 74LVC1G34GW-Q100) | Bench-fanout buffer (non-inverting) | TI sn74lvc1g34 (symbol) / Nexperia 74LVC1G34_Q100 (doc) | SOT353-1 / TSSOP5, 0.65 mm pitch | YES: 1=NC,2=A,3=GND,4=Y,5=VCC = std 1G34 | **FAIL - no footprint assigned** | VCC=5 (3V3_CLK), GND=3 | none | C159 0.1uF at pin5; R189 22R + C160 at Y | Place next to U52; input (pin2) taps Y node before R187 | **FAIL** | High |

### External 10 MHz RF front end (refclock-input.kicad_sch)  —  _verdict: Needs corrections_

## External 10 MHz RF Front End — Pre-Layout Review (`refclock-input.kicad_sch`)

Reviewed against `docs/ntp_server_rf_frontend.md`, `peripheral_map`, netlist `ntp-server-stm32.net`, and `sts1000_bom.csv`. Topology, symbol pinouts, and footprints for the three ICs are correct; the blockers are **a mis-wired LT3045 PGFB (PG non-functional), two unselected clamp diodes (no footprint/MPN), and two missing bypass/decoupling caps required by the doc.**

**Designator map (doc → as-built):** D11→D8(SMA ESD), D12→D19(N2 clamp), D13→D20(island), D14→D21(VCC), D15→D18(switch clamp); R134/R135→R174/R175, R140/R141→R179/R180, R142→R182, R143→R183, R144→R184, R147→R176, R177/R178/R181/R185/R186 unchanged; C133→C150, C134/C137→C154/C156, C135→C155, C136→C151, +VCC byp C152(1µF)/C153(0.1µF); FB9, U49/U50/U51 unchanged.

|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| U49 | TMUX1101DCK (placeholder) | Switched 50 Ω term (SEL=REF_TERM_EN, active-high=ON) | ti.com/lit/ds/symlink/tmux1101.pdf | SC70-5 (DCK) | YES — 1=D,2=S,3=GND,4=SEL,5=VDD matches symbol | YES — SOT-353_SC-70-5 = DCK 5-lead | GND=3, VDD=5 (3V0_RF) | SEL(4)=PC10, fail-safe/OV-tolerant; default-term via R176 100k→3V3 | **0.1 µF VDD decoupler MISSING**; D18 pin-2 clamp present | VDD+GND+term return kept in island/analog GND; grounded-end placement | WARNING | High |

#### Design-intent mismatches
See docMismatches array: U49 package (doc SC70-6 vs actual SC70-5), U51 PG (doc "float/unused" vs wired to U55 GPA2), R177/R186 precision grade (0.1% doc vs 1% BOM), incomplete designator re-annotation in doc body, and cosmetic +3.3V power-symbol glyphs on 3V0_RF/5V nets.

### Rb buck supply (VCC_RB)  —  _verdict: Blocked_

## Rb buck supply (VCC_RB) — pre-layout review

Status: **Blocked.** Core regulation topology, the fixed-resistor safety bound, and the autonomous OV latch are sound and math-verified, but there are multiple hard defects that prevent layout/operation: an INA228 I2C bus swap + address collision, undersized output caps, a digipot VDD-vs-terminal abs-max violation, and two parts with no footprint (L7, U41).

### Verified-correct highlights
- **Fixed-resistor safety bound (critical requirement) PASSES.** FB=0.6V, R147=20k, R148=576, R134(Rctrl)=4.12k. VOUT = 0.6·(1+R1/R2+R1/Rctrl) − (R1/Rctrl)·VCTRL = 24.35 − 4.854·VCTRL. With VCTRL hard-limited 0…VREF(4.096V), VOUT is bounded **4.46V (D=0, wiper at B) … 24.35V (D=1023, wiper at A)** for *every* possible wiper code (POR/mid-scale/SPI-fault). No code exits the bound. Confirmed by independent calc.
- **Autonomous 26V OV latch PASSES (firmware-independent).** Sense R138(120k)/R139(10k)=0.0769 → 26.0V trips. Ref R136(10.5k)/R137(10k) off VREF → 1.998V. Regenerative Q16(NPN)/Q17(PNP) hold via R151(4.7k) off always-on +5V; Q18 clamps RB_PSU_PWR_EN < 0.6V; D11 isolates the comparator so a VCC_RB collapse cannot re-arm. Latches off (not hiccup). Reset via Q15 from RB_OV_RESET (PD3). RB_OV_DET → PE3 (polled). Trip ladder 24.35 < 26 < 28 (TVS standoff) < ~31 (VBR) < ~45 (clamp) is consistent — latch fires before the TVS conducts. (Caveat: OV reference is gated with the buck — see High Risk.)
- **MIC28516 (U40) bias network PASSES.** SVIN←VOUT_P via R162 2.2Ω + C135 1µF; VDD (internal LDO out) bypass C138 2.2µF; PVDD←VDD via R163 2.2Ω + C137 4.7µF; EXTVDD→GND (unused, allowed). Matches Microchip datasheet recommended connection. EN=RB_PSU_PWR_EN, FB net, SS=C119 10nF, ILIM=R140 2.21k, FREQ=R132/R133 divider, BST=C124 0.1µF, PG=RB_PSU_PG (R143 10k→3V3, also to U55).
- **OPA320 (U42)** unity follower correct: +IN←U43 wiper, −IN↔OUT, OUT→R134; V+ = 5V (C122), V−=GND. Pinout matches TI SOT-23-5.
- **MCP1502 (U45)** pinout correct (1=OUT,2/3/5=GND,4=nSHDN,6=VDD=5V).

### FE-5680A RS-232 interface (rb-io sheet)  —  _verdict: Needs corrections_

## FE-5680A RS-232 / Control Interface — Pre-Layout Review (`rb-io.kicad_sch`)

Net-level connectivity is clean and matches the canonical `rb_rs232_interface.md` design intent almost exactly: the SN65C3221E strapping, charge-pump/reservoir cap topology, dual-mode DPDT routing, the opto lock chain, and the DB9 ESD front end all wire as documented. The transceiver symbol pinout is datasheet-correct. The blockers are **layout-infrastructure**: several devices in this block have **no footprint assigned** (K1, L8, L9, D16) and there is **no `fp-lib-table` in the project**, so the custom-lib footprints (U46, U47) will not resolve in the PCB editor. A handful of doc/BOM accuracy items round out the list.

#### Layout-critical constraints for this block

| Net/class | Current est | Width/impedance | Placement / return path | Evidence |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Serial GND single bond (J6-5 → U46-14 → board GND) | signal | wide/short | **single galvanic bond** between Rb domain and board GND; keep Rb high-current return off this path | doc §6 |
| K1 coil drive (+3V3→K1→Q21) | ~36 mA | std | flyback D15 close to coil; coil at 110% rated → keep relay away from hot zones | Omron G6K DC3 91Ω; §5.5 |
| DB9 ESD front end (D13/D14, C146/147, R165/166, L8/9, U47, C141/142) | ESD/surge | — | TVS + shunts AT connector; ferrite between stages; secondary clamp at xcvr; 47pF C0G to preserve edges | doc §6 |
| RS-232 line pins (DOUT/RIN) | ≤1Mb/s | CL≤250pF @1Mb/s | route line pins toward DB9; keep cap+TVS junction C bounded | TI §7.8 |
| Opto isolation (U48) | DC | — | maintain creepage/clearance under body; lock line off the single-bond ground (opto = the break) | doc §6A |
| Charge-pump caps (C139/140/144/145) | — | short | tight to U46 C1±/C2±/V±; 1µF C143 at VCC for IEC-ESD | TI §7.3 |

### SPI peripherals (NOR flash, U62)  —  _verdict: Needs corrections_

## SPI Peripherals — NOR Flash (U62) — Pre-Layout Review

Scope: the SPI-NOR boot/log flash on `spi-peripherals.kicad_sch`. (The sheet also physically carries display/touch ESD/level-shift parts — PCA9306 U63, R210/R211, etc. — but those belong to the display/touch subsystem and are out of scope here except where they share the SPI4 bus.)

**Headline:** the part choice (Macronix MX25L25645GM2I-08G, 256 Mbit / 32 MB, 8-SOP 208mil, industrial) is correct and sourcing-compliant. But the NOR is **not layout-ready**: its symbol has an **unnumbered VCC pin** (so VCC is not mapped to a footprint pad) and **no footprint is assigned**. Decoupling on the VCC pad cannot be confirmed because the pad is unmapped. SPI bus topology, CS/RST/WP pull-ups, and rail are otherwise correct.

#### IC-by-IC

| RefDes | MPN | Function | Datasheet | Package | Symbol pinout verified | Footprint verified | Power/Gnd pins | Strap/EN/RST pins | Required passives | Layout-critical notes | Status | Confidence |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| U62 | MX25L25645GM2I-08G | 256 Mbit (32 MB) SPI NOR flash; MCUboot/secure-boot store, logs, web assets, FW staging | Macronix MX25L25645G 3V 256Mb Rev 2.0 (PM2075) | 8-SOP 208mil (SO8) | Pins 1–7 match JEDEC SO8 serial-NOR pinout; **VCC pin has NO pin number (must be pin 8)** | **No** — Footprint field empty | VCC=pin8 (unmapped!), GND=pin4 (OK, on GND) | nCS=pin1 (SPI_NSS/PE11), nRESET/SIO3=pin7 (NOR_RST_N/PE10, R205 pull-up), nWP/SIO2=pin3 (R207 pull-up, no MCU drive) | VCC decoupling 0.1 µF + bulk on pin8 (cannot confirm — pad unmapped); R205/R207/R212 pull-ups present | Place 100 nF within ~1–2 mm of pin8; keep SCK return tight | FAIL | High |

#### Netlist findings

| Net | Connected pins | Expected | Observed issue | Risk | Fix | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 3V3_STM (U62 VCC) | `U62 pin ""` (+ rail) | U62 VCC = pin 8 on 3V3_STM | VCC mapped to **empty pin number** (`pin ""`); KiCad cannot connect this to footprint pad 8 → VCC pad floats in layout/DRC | Part unpowered / no ERC-DRC catch → dead board | Edit symbol `ntp-server-stm32:MX25L25645GM2I-08G`: assign VCC pin number "8" | FAIL |
| SPI_NSS | U12 PE11(42), R212(pull-up→3V3_STM), U62 nCS(1) | NOR CS with idle-high pull-up | Correct. Hardware NSS PE11, pulled high so NOR deselected during MCU reset/Hi-Z | OK | None | PASS |
| SPI_SCK | U12 PE12(43), U62 SCLK(6), U43 SCK(3), R211(22 Ω series→display) | SPI4 clock shared NOR+digipot(+display via R211) | Multi-drop SCK (NOR + MCP41U83 digipot + display branch). Acceptable; CS-selected | Medium (stub/reflection at >50 MHz) | Keep NOR + digipot stubs short; series R at branch to display already present | PASS |
| SPI_MOSI | U12 PE14(45), U62 SI/SIO0(5), U43 SDI(4), R210(22 Ω series→display) | SPI4 MOSI shared | Correct multi-drop | Low | Same routing care as SCK | PASS |

| NOR_RST_N | U12 PE10(41), R205(pull-up→3V3_STM), U62 nRESET/SIO3(7) | Firmware reset, default-high | Correct: actively driven + pulled high | OK | None | PASS |
| Net-(U62-nWP{slash}SIO2) | R207(pull-up→3V3_STM), U62 nWP/SIO2(3) | WP# tied high (write-protect disabled) | Functionally OK (single-SPI). Net is **auto-named** (`Net-(U62-…)`) — violates naming convention | Cosmetic/maintainability | Name net `NOR_WP_N` | WARNING |

#### Layout-critical constraints for this block

| Net/class | Current est | Width/impedance | Placement / return path | Evidence |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 3V3_STM → U62 VCC | ≤ ~25–40 mA active read | Standard power trace; 100 nF MLCC at pin 8 | Decoupling cap on pin-8 side; short via to GND plane | Macronix DS recommends bypass at VCC |
| SPI4 SCK/MOSI/MISO | signal | ~50 Ω SE; ≤20–40 MHz NOR / display reconfig | Multi-drop bus: keep NOR + digipot (U43) stubs short; the 22 Ω series R210/R211 isolate the display branch only — NOR/digipot see the un-series-terminated trunk | sheet note "Place resistors where traces branch toward connector"; peripheral_map §5 |
| CS/RST | signal | standard | route with bus | — |

#### Design-intent mismatches

| Ref | Doc says | Schematic says | Severity |
|---|---|---|---|
| U62 footprint | Datasheet-verified parts, layout-ready | Footprint field empty everywhere | High |
| U62 VCC | Powered from always-on 3V3_STM | VCC pin has no pin number → not actually mappable to pad | High (blocker) |
| WP net name | Net names must match convention (`sts1000_net_naming.md`) | Auto-named `Net-(U62-nWP{slash}SIO2)` | Low |
| Recovery path (peripheral_map §, line "NOR on always-on 3V3_STM … recovery via NOR_RST_N only") | open item to confirm acceptable | As-built: NOR_RST_N (PE10) wired, no rail-cycle | Info — consistent; confirm MX25L25645G `RESET#` semantics are adequate (it is a hardware reset pin, OK) |

### I2C peripherals + display power  —  _verdict: Needs corrections_

## I2C Peripherals + Display Power — Pre-Layout Review

**Scope note:** The named sheet is `i2c-peripherals.kicad_sch` (the `i2c-peripherals.kicad_sch` path you gave). The I²C housekeeping/sensor group (U57/U58 TMP117, U59 LIS2DH12, U60 ATECC608B, U61 IIS2MDC) lives in this sheet. The **display-power** parts in the FOCUS list (U33 RT9742, U32 INA228, U63 PCA9306) are actually on `3v3-main-power.kicad_sch` / `spi-peripherals.kicad_sch`, and the display ESD arrays U17/U18 (TPD4E05U06) on `connectors.kicad_sch`. I reviewed all of them via the netlist (`ntp-server-stm32.net`) since they form the display-power chain. **All I²C peripherals are on always-on `3V3_STM`** (confirmed in netlist), consistent with the 3V3_P-elimination decision in root `CLAUDE.md` but **contradicting the canonical doc `sts1000_3v3p_i2c_peripherals.md`, which still describes a gated 3V3_P / PERIPH_EN rail** (see Design-intent mismatches).

| U32 | INA228 | VSSOP-10 | Yes | VSSOP10_DGS_TEX | 10 | Yes | PASS |
