### Fault/UI aggregation (MCP23017 ×2: U55 @0x20, U54 @0x21)  —  _verdict: Needs corrections_

## Fault/UI Aggregation Review — MCP23017 ×2 (U55 @0x20, U54 @0x21)

Sheet: `hardware/ntp-server-stm32/i2c-gpio.kicad_sch`. Netlist-verified against `ntp-server-stm32.net`. Canonical doc: `docs/sts1000_fault_aggregation.md`.

**Headline:** Wiring, addressing, single-pull-up-per-INT, reset topology, I²C pin orientation, and rail (3V3_STM) are all correct and match the doc. The legacy-R44 concern is **resolved** (R44 is an Ethernet PHY term, not on INA_ALERT_INT_N). **One hard defect:** three input signals are mapped onto the MCP23017 GPA7/GPB7 pins, which Microchip's own datasheet (Rev D, June 2022) and the article cited in this part's own symbol description say **must not be used as inputs** — an input edge during an I²C read can corrupt SDA and hang the shared housekeeping bus.

#### IC-by-IC

| RefDes | MPN | Function | Datasheet | Package | Symbol pinout verified | Footprint verified | Power/Gnd pins | Strap/EN/RST pins | Required passives | Layout-critical notes | Status | Confidence |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| U55 | MCP23017T-E/ML | 16-bit I²C GPIO expander — 8×PG + 2×EN-fault → `PG_INT_N` | DS20001952 (Rev D, 2022) | QFN-28 6×6mm 0.65mm, 1EP | Yes (28 pins + EP match) | WARNING — KiCad lib `QFN-28-1EP_6x6mm_P0.65mm_EP4.25x4.25mm`; EP nominal in datasheet C-rev drawing ~4.45mm, verify exact EP for ML variant | VDD(5)=3V3_STM, VSS(6)=GND, EP(29)=GND | A0/A1/A2(11/12/13)=GND→0x20; RESET(14)=EXP_RST_N | C168 0.1µF (3V3_STM); R200 10k pull-up on PG_INT_N; R198 10k pull-down on EXP_RST_N | INTA(16)+INTB(15) tied → single open-drain INT; MIRROR=1 in FW; GPA7=POE_PG is on a restricted pin (see findings) | FAIL | High |
| U54 | MCP23017T-E/ML | 16-bit I²C GPIO expander — 8 buttons+touch → `BTN_INT_N`; 8 INA228 ALERT → `INA_ALERT_INT_N` | DS20001952 (Rev D, 2022) | QFN-28 6×6mm 0.65mm, 1EP | Yes (28 pins + EP match) | WARNING — same EP caveat as U55 | VDD(5)=3V3_STM, VSS(6)=GND, EP(29)=GND | A0(11)=3V3_STM, A1/A2(12/13)=GND→0x21; RESET(14)=EXP_RST_N | C169 0.1µF (3V3_STM); R201 10k on BTN_INT_N; R199 10k on INA_ALERT_INT_N | INTA(16)/INTB(15) separate (MIRROR=0); GPA7=DISP_TOUCH_INT and GPB7=INA_ALERT_VCC_RB are inputs on restricted pins | FAIL | High |

#### Netlist findings

| Net | Connected pins | Expected | Observed issue | Risk | Fix | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| INA_ALERT_INT_N | R199.2, U12 PC12(80), U54 INTB(15) | One pull-up + MCU EXTI + INTB | None — R44 is **not** here (R44 = 3V3_LAN↔TRD0_N PHY term). Single 10k pull-up. | None | None — close the "drop R44" open item; note is satisfied | PASS |
| PG_INT_N | R200.2, U12 PA10(69), U55 INTA(16)+INTB(15) | One pull-up + MCU EXTI + tied INTA/INTB | INTA+INTB both open-drain wire-OR onto one net; correct with IOCON.ODR=1 + MIRROR=1 | None (ODR=1 mandatory; push-pull would contend) | Ensure FW sets ODR=1 before INT enable | PASS |
| BTN_INT_N | R201.2, U12 PE0(97), U54 INTA(16) | One pull-up + MCU EXTI + INTA | None | None | None | PASS |
| EXP_RST_N | R198.1, U12 PC0(15), U54 RESET(14), U55 RESET(14) | Shared reset, pull-down default-asserted | Correct: R198 10k pull-down holds both in reset until PC0 driven high | RESET is active-low; held low at POR = both expanders reset until FW — intended | None | PASS |
| I2C_SCL | U54 SCK(8), U55 SCK(8), +19 bus nodes | SCL on pin 8 | Correct (pin 8 = SCL on MCP23017) | None | None | PASS |
| I2C_SDA | U54 SDA(9), U55 SDA(9), +19 bus nodes | SDA on pin 9 | Correct | None | None | PASS |
| (U54 GPA7 pin24) DISP_TOUCH_INT | U54.24, source touch INT | Input | **GPA7 is output-only per Microchip (input edge can corrupt SDA)** | HIGH — bus hang on shared housekeeping I²C; loses all monitoring | Move DISP_TOUCH_INT to a GPA0–6/GPB0–6 pin or an MCU EXTI; rebalance bits | FAIL |
| (U54 GPB7 pin4) INA_ALERT_VCC_RB | U54.4, INA228 #6 ALERT | Input | **GPB7 output-only — same hazard** | HIGH — Rb-rail ALERT can hang bus | Reassign to a non-7 bit | FAIL |
| (U55 GPA7 pin24) POE_PG | U55.24, PoE PG | Input | **GPA7 output-only — same hazard** | HIGH | Reassign to a free U55 GPB bit (GPB2–7 spare) | FAIL |
| NC pins 7,10 (both) | unconnected | NC | Correctly left unconnected (symbol marks hidden NC) | None | None | PASS |
| U55 GPB2–7 (pins 27,28,3,4 …) | unconnected | 6 spare | Spare inputs floating — acceptable for unused expander inputs but set IODIR=out or GPPU on; floating CMOS inputs raise Icc | Low | Enable internal pull-ups (GPPU) or config as outputs in FW | WARNING |

### I2C1 bus + rise-time accelerator (U56 LTC4311)  —  _verdict: Ready (pre-layout) with open verifications_

## I2C1 Bus + Rise-Time Accelerator — Pre-Layout Review

Sheet: `hardware/ntp-server-stm32/i2c-buffer.kicad_sch`. Components on sheet: **U56** LTC4311ISC6-TRPBF (I2C active pull-up / rise-time accelerator), **R202/R203** 4.7k bus pull-ups, **C170** 0.1uF U56 decoupling. This sheet also instantiates the single global I2C1 bus (`I2C_SCL`=PB8/U12 pin95, `I2C_SDA`=PB9/U12 pin96) — note the net *labels* are `I2C_SCL`/`I2C_SDA` not the canonical `I2C1_SCL`/`I2C1_SDA`; see doc-mismatch table.

**Headline:** U56 is wired correctly — pinout, footprint, EN strap, and pull-up rail all verified. The accelerator does NOT isolate (confirmed: it is a 2-channel active pull-up on the *same* bus, exactly as CLAUDE.md states), so the back-powering concern is moot here because R202/R203 and U56 are all on always-on `3V3_STM`. The real open items are bus-loading budget (C_bus vs LTC4311 capability, single 4.7k pair for ~13 devices across the whole board) and minor net-naming drift.

#### IC-by-IC
| RefDes | MPN | Function | Datasheet | Package | Symbol pinout verified | Footprint verified | Power/Gnd pins | Strap/EN/RST pins | Required passives | Layout-critical notes | Status | Confidence |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| U56 | LTC4311ISC6-TRPBF | Dual I2C/SMBus active pull-up (rise-time accelerator), 1.6–5.5 V | analog.com 4311fa | SC70-6 (SC6) | YES — pin1 VCC, pin2 GND, pin3 ENABLE, pin4 BUS2, pin5 GND, pin6 BUS1 (matches lib sym & datasheet pin config) | YES — `SOT-6_SC_LIT.kicad_mod`, 6 pads 0.65 mm pitch, ~1.35×1.35 mm courtyard = SC70-6 | VCC=pin1→3V3_STM; GND=pin2 & pin5→GND (both grounded ✓) | ENABLE=pin3→3V3_STM (tied to VCC = always enabled, active-high) ✓ | C170 0.1uF VCC bypass; relies on R202/R203 as static pull-ups it augments | Place U56 + C170 close together; place U56 near the *electrical midpoint / far end* of the long multi-sheet I2C bus so it accelerates the highest-C node, not at the MCU. Keep BUS1/BUS2 stubs short. | PASS | High |

#### Netlist findings
| Net | Connected pins | Expected | Observed issue | Risk | Fix | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 3V3_STM | U56.1 (VCC), U56.3 (ENABLE), R202.1, R203.1, C170.1, U12 VDD ×5, all housekeeping VCCs | VCC+EN on always-on rail; pull-ups on always-on rail | None — correct. EN=VCC ✓, pull-ups on always-on rail ✓ (avoids ESD back-powering of gated devices) | — | — | PASS |
| I2C_SCL (BUS1) | U56.6, R202.2, U12.95 (PB8), + U10/U23/U26/U30/U31/U32/U37/U44/U54/U55/U57/U58/U59/U60/U61/U63 | One static pull-up + accelerator + all device SCL | ~16 device loads + long multi-sheet routing on ONE pull-up (4.7k). High C_bus is the *reason* U56 exists, but C_bus is not yet budgeted | Med — if total C_bus exceeds LTC4311 range or rise time still fails at 400 kHz, bus marginal | Budget C_bus (sum of all device pin C + trace C); confirm ≤ LTC4311 supported load at target SCL; keep 4.7k (good static value, ~0.7 mA sink @3.3 V) | WARNING (open verification) |
| I2C_SDA (BUS2) | U56.4, R203.2, U12.96 (PB9), + same device set SDA | Same as SCL | Same as above | Med | Same as SCL | WARNING (open verification) |
| GND | U56.2, U56.5 | Both GND pins grounded | None | — | — | PASS |

Note: BUS1↔SCL and BUS2↔SDA assignment is electrically irrelevant (the two channels are identical, independent active pull-ups); current mapping (pin6 BUS1→SCL, pin4 BUS2→SDA) is correct and consistent.

#### BOM validation
| RefDes | MPN | Datasheet found | Package | Footprint | Pkg-FP match | Pinout match | Rating match | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| U56 | LTC4311ISC6-TRPBF | YES (4311fa) | SC70-6 | SOT-6_SC_LIT | YES | YES | VCC abs-max 5.5 V ≫ 3.3 V rail ✓; 1.6–5.5 V op ✓ | PASS | BOM "Footprint" column blank for U56 (line 525); footprint lives in symbol property only — populate CSV for completeness |

#### Layout-critical constraints for this block
| Net/class | Current est | Width/impedance | Placement / return path | Evidence |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| I2C_SCL / I2C_SDA | DC sink ≤ ~0.7 mA static (3.3 V/4.7k) + dynamic accel pulses from U56 | Standard signal width; not impedance-controlled, but minimize total capacitance (short, narrow, avoid long parallel runs over plane gaps) | Place U56 near the high-capacitance end of the bus, not at the MCU. Keep U56 BUS stubs short; keep C170 adjacent to U56 pin1/pin2. Continuous GND reference under the long bus | LTC4311 4311fa (active pull-up monitors edge rate); CLAUDE.md "LTC4311 does not isolate" |
| 3V3_STM (U56 VCC) | µA-class | local 0.1uF | C170 close-coupled to U56 | datasheet bypass guidance |

#### Design-intent mismatches
| Ref | Doc says | Schematic says | Severity |
|---|---|---|---|
| I2C net names | peripheral_map / naming doc reference `I2C1` (PB8/PB9 = I2C1) | Global labels are `I2C_SCL` / `I2C_SDA` (no `1`) | Low — consistent across all sheets, but drifts from canonical "I2C1_*"; confirm intended naming |
| U56 BOM Footprint field | BOM rules want explicit footprint per line | Line 525 U56 Footprint column empty (also Pkg/Pinout flags blank, status `MPN-FROM-VALUE`) | Low — populate before release |


### Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch)  —  _verdict: Needs corrections_

**Net-connectivity is largely clean.** The remaining gating items for layout hand-off are (a) missing/incorrect footprints on connectors, the 10 MHz ESD diodes, and a test point; (b) an unresolved TVS value on VCC_RB; (c) a display-flex pin-11 LCD-RST-vs-CTP-RST question; plus doc/schematic deltas.

### RGB status indicator (D5)  —  _verdict: Needs corrections_

## RGB Status Indicator (D5) — Pre-Layout Review

Topology is sound and the netlist matches the canonical doc exactly: common-anode RGB die (3 ballasts to always-on `5V`), low-side NPN (BC847W) per color, base resistor + 10 k pulldown per color, active-high GPIO drive on PD12/13/14. Electrical design is PASS. **One blocker prevents layout: D5's assigned footprint does not exist in the project** (no `fp-lib-table`, no `.kicad_mod`), and the symbol↔footprint pad mapping for the PLCC-6 therefore cannot be verified.

#### IC / active-device-by-IC

| RefDes | MPN | Function | Datasheet | Package | Symbol pinout verified | Footprint verified | Power/Gnd pins | Strap/EN/RST | Required passives | Layout-critical notes | Status | Confidence |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| D5 | Inolux IN-P55TATRGB | RGB LED, 6-die-pin PLCC-6 (3 anode / 3 cathode) | inolux-corp.com IN-P55TATRGB | PLCC-6 5.0×5.5 mm P1.8 | YES — symbol pins 1=KB,2=KR,3=KG,4=AG,5=AR,6=AB match doc §2/§6 pinout (internally consistent) | **NO — footprint missing** (see blocker) | none (passive LED) | none | R59/R60/R61 ballast; cathodes to Q collectors | Pin-1 orientation must be checked once footprint exists; place at front panel; verify local ambient ≤ ~25 °C for blue 24.8 mA point (§7) | FAIL (footprint) | High (symbol), Unknown (footprint) |
| Q8 | BC847W | NPN low-side switch, Blue (LED_B) | Nexperia/Infineon BC847 series | SOT-323 (SC-70) | YES — pin1=B,2=E,3=C confirmed vs Nexperia datasheet | YES — `Package_TO_SOT_SMD:SOT-323_SC-70` (KiCad std) matches | E(2)→GND | base 10 k pulldown R56 | R55 1k base, R56 10k pd | none | PASS | High |
| Q9 | BC847W | NPN low-side switch, Red (LED_R) | as above | SOT-323 | YES (1=B,2=E,3=C) | YES | E(2)→GND | R58 pulldown | R57 1.5k base, R58 10k pd | none | PASS | High |

BC847W pinout (pin1 B / pin2 E / pin3 C) confirmed against Nexperia BC847W (SOT-323) — matches the KiCad `Transistor_BJT:BC847W` symbol and the schematic mapping for all three.

## 9. Symbol & footprint validation (custom library)

## Custom Symbol + Footprint Library Validation (pre-layout)

Scope: every `.kicad_sym` / `.kicad_mod` in `hardware/libraries/` plus the project-local symbol lib `hardware/libraries/ntp-server-stm32.kicad_sym`. Verified symbol pin **numbers** vs datasheet pinout and footprint pad **numbers/geometry** vs manufacturer land pattern. Datasheet pin tables confirmed by web for INA228-DGS, INA181-DBV, LTC4311-SC6, 74LVC1G157, TPD4E02B04-DQA, MCP41U83-TSSOP14, PGB1010603.

**Headline blockers:** (1) `MCP41U83` symbol (U43, Rb digipot) pin-number map for pins 1–7 disagrees with the Microchip datasheet — wrong pad mapping. (2) `MX25L25645GM2I-08G` symbol (U62 SPI-NOR) has a VCC pin with an empty pin number. (3) ST LGA-12 sensor footprints (U59/U61) and the e-compass need a pin-1-corner cross-check against the ST land-pattern figure. Three custom symbols (`AD5292BRUZ`, `AD5270BRMZ`, `ADCLK925BCPZ`) are orphans not used by the netlist; a stray `2026-06-14_01-24-03.kicad_sym` (`LIS2MDLTR`) is loose in the lib.

#### MCP41U83 (U43) symbol vs datasheet — pin-number conflict (Microchip DS20007000, TSSOP-14)

| Pin | Symbol (`ntp-server-stm32.kicad_sym`) | Datasheet | Match |
|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | VDD | CS/A0 | NO |
| 2 | SDO/A1 | SDI/SDA | NO |
| 3 | SCK/SCL | DGND | NO |
| 4 | SDI/SDA | SPI2C | NO |
| 5 | nCS/A0 | VDD | NO |
| 6 | SPI2C | SDO/A1 | NO |
| 7 | DGND | SCK/SCL | NO |
| 8–14 | P0B,P0W,P0A,VSS,NC,NC,NC | P0B,P0W,P0A,VSS,NC,NC,NC | YES |

Pins 8–14 agree; pins 1–7 are reordered. This is the digipot sitting in the Rb buck FB node — a wrong pad map mis-wires VDD/VSS/SPI/wiper-config and can drive VCC_RB out of the safe envelope. Must be corrected and re-verified against the datasheet pinout figure before layout. (This is exactly the open item flagged in `CLAUDE.md` / `hardware/CLAUDE.md`: "MCP41U83 pin numbers TBD".)

#### Layout-critical constraints for this block (net/class | est | width/impedance | placement | evidence)

| Item | Note | Evidence |
|---|---|---|
| INA228 VSSOP-10 | No exposed pad (correct); Kelvin IN+/IN− to shunt | VSSOP10_DGS_TEX has 10 pads, no EP; INA228-Q1 DS |
| TPS7A52 RGR EP (pad21) | EP is `F.Cu`-only, no paste aperture | RGR20…TEX.kicad_mod pad 21 |
| TPS61094 SON EP (pad13) | EP is `F.Cu`+`F.Mask`, no paste aperture | SON50P300…13N pad 13 |
| LAN8742 / MIC bucks QFN EP | EP pad 25 / thermal vias at layout | QFN50P400…25N pad 25 |
| ST LGA-12 sensors | confirm pin-1 corner + ST land dims; magnetometer needs current-free GND pour (hardware/CLAUDE.md) | LGA-12_STM / 2X2X0P7 |

#### Design-intent mismatches (Ref | Doc says | Schematic/lib says | Severity)

| Ref | Doc | Lib/BOM | Severity |
|---|---|---|---|
| U43 digipot | docs reference MCP41U83 (Rb digipot); AD5292/AD5270 are in sym-lib-table | AD5292BRUZ + AD5270BRMZ symbols exist but are orphan/unused | Low (housekeeping — remove unused libs to avoid the wrong part being placed) |
| Rb digipot pinout | CLAUDE.md open item: "MCP41U83 pin numbers TBD" | symbol pins 1–7 wrong | High |
| U62 SPI-NOR | software_spec requires SPI-NOR (Macronix MX25L) | symbol has empty pin number on VCC; no footprint in BOM | High |
| Magjack/ARJ-199, ZED module | authoritative parts | symbols present, pin/pad maps not independently audited here | Medium (audit before layout) |

## 10. Power-tree review

## Whole-Board Power-Tree Pre-Layout Review — STS1000 "Meridian"

Scope: PoE input → FDMQ8205A bridge → NCP1095 PD → 5 V intermediate buck → 3V3 main → per-rail LDOs/bucks (OCXO, Rb, GPS, RF island, display) → supercap backup. Evidence: `ntp-server-stm32.net` (flattened connectivity), `sts1000_bom.csv`, `docs/ntp_server_peripheral_map.md §6/§7`, vendor datasheets. Confidence tags inline.

### Power-tree table

| Rail | Source (designator) | Vnom | Vmin/max | Est max I | Loads | Enable ctrl | Sequencing | Decoupling | Protection | Layout notes | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| **VOUT_P** (rectified PoE bus) | U7+U8 FDMQ8205A dual bridge (Mode A+B, all 4 pairs from magjack J1) → U9 NCP1095 pin1 VPORTP; hot-swap Q2 FDMC8622 in VOUT_N return | ~37–57 V | 37–57 V (802.3bt) | ~0.6–0.8 A peak @ 25–30 W | U28A (main buck), U40A (Rb buck), C75/C77/C80/C133/C134/C136 (2.2µF/100V X7T), C10 (10µF/100V) | NCP1095 PD gate (Q2) | classification then power-good | 100 V X7T bank present | **No HV bus TVS (SMAJ58A-class) found on VOUT_P** — see B1 | Kelvin RDET/RCLASS to U9; 57 V creepage; Q2 thermal | **WARNING** |
| **5V** (intermediate) | U28A MIC28516 buck from VOUT_P; L2 6.8µH/11.5A (SRP1265A) | 5.0 V | FB-set: 0.6×(1+15k/2.05k)=**5.0 V** | ~3–4 A (feeds 3V3 buck + OCXO buck + LDO refs + fan + 5V_DISP + ant bias) | U29 (3V3), U38 (OCXO pre), U13/U14/U45 refs, U27 (ant), U33 (disp), U2/U41/U42 comparators/buffers, J2 fan | always-on (POE_PG → U28 EN path) | comes up after PD power-good | C64/65/66/71/72 (47µF+10µF) | inrush via U28 SS (C63) | L2 saturation OK (11.5A vs ~4A); high-di/dt loop | **PASS** (verify I budget) |
| **3V3 (main/general)** | U29 AP3441 buck from **5V** | 3.33 V | 0.6×(1+10k/2.2k)=**3.33 V** | ~1.5–2 A | PHY 3V3_LAN(via FB1), all INA228 VS, Rb-IO, RS232 U46, OCXO INA, 3V3_CLK(via FB10), **3V3_STM via R106** | always-on | after 5V | C83/86/87 etc | — | **U29 input = 5.0 V vs AP3441 Vin abs-max 5.5 V → only 0.5 V margin (A1)** | **WARNING** |
| **3V3_STM** ("always-on" housekeeping) | **3V3 through R106 = 0.5 Ω sense shunt** (INA228 U31 across it) — NOT an independent regulator | 3.3 V − I·0.5Ω | tracks 3V3 | ~0.3–0.5 A | STM32 VDD (×5), both MCP23017, LTC4311, TMP117×2, IIS2MDC, LIS2DH12, ATECC608B, NOR U62, PCA9306, TPS3430 WDT, INT pull-ups | none (always = 3V3) | identical to 3V3 | C168–C181, C21–C25 | — | **0.5 Ω shunt on full STM rail → 250 mV drop @0.5 A; and "always-on" is a misnomer — it collapses with 3V3 (B2)** | **FAIL** |
| **3V3_CLK** | 3V3 via FB10 (600Ω ferrite) | 3.3 V | — | <0.1 A | U52 mux, U53 fanout buf | always-on | with 3V3 | C157/158/159 | ferrite isolation | quiet clock-VDD island | **PASS** |
| **3V3_LAN** | 3V3 via FB1 (600Ω ferrite) | 3.3 V | — | ~0.1 A | U11 LAN8742 VDDIO, magjack J1 12/6 | always-on | with 3V3 | C13/19/20/2 | ferrite | — | **PASS** |
| **OCXO 3.3 V** | U38 AP3441 (5V→**3.7 V**, FB 12.4k/2.4k) → U39 TPS7A52 LDO (3.7→3.33 V, FB 12.1k/3.83k, Vref 0.8) | 3.33 V | dropout 115 mV; have 370 mV | ~0.5–1.2 A (warm-up) | Y3 OH300 (OCXO_V via R122), U36 OPA320, INA228 U37 | always-on (low-noise) | first up (warm-up staging) | C102–C115 bank | TPS7A52 ULN LDO for phase noise | Vc-path caps must be C0G/film not X7R; 370 mV headroom OK | **PASS** |
| **VCC_RB** (Rb buck) | U40A MIC28516 from VOUT_P; **L7 spec'd 40µH but MPN = SRP1265A-6R8M = 6.8µH (C1)**; FB digipot-trimmed (R134/R147/R148 + U43 MCP41U83) | 5–24 V (set per Rb, +15 V typ) | bounded by fixed R; OV latch @26 V (U41 LMV393 + D7 TVS) | ~6–10 W steady, 15–20 W warm-up | J6 (FE-5680A), INA228 U44 | **RB_PWR_EN (PB7)** → Q18 → U40 EN | deferred until OCXO warm + supercaps charged | C126–C138 | autonomous 26 V OV latch; D7 TVS **value unspecified "1.5SMCxxA" (B3)** | high-Z FB node keep-out; L7 inductor wrong value blocks layout | **FAIL** (L7 + D7) |
| **3V3_GPS** | U22 LT3045 LDO (from 5V via FB3) | 3.3 V | — | ~0.2–0.4 A | U21 ZED-F9T VCC, INA228 U23, U24 | **GPS_PWR_EN (PC8)** → U22 EN | after 3V3 | C45/47/54/55/56 | LT3045 ULN | — | **PASS** |
| **3V0_RF** (RF island) | U51 LT3045 LDO (from 5V via FB9) | 3.0 V | — | <0.1 A | U49 TMUX, U50 LTC6752 slicer | 5V_PSU_PG-gated EN | with 5V | C156 | island clamp D20/D21 | analog island | **PASS** |
| **V_ANT** (antenna bias) | U27 RT9742 load switch from 5V → bias-T (L1 47nH) | 5 V | — | ~50–150 mA | active antenna via SMA | **ANT_BIAS_EN (PC9)** | runtime | C61/62 | foldback Q12 + R77 sense; INA228 U26 | RF + bias ESD at SMA (separate review) | **PASS** |
| **5V_DISP** | U33 RT9742 load switch from 5V → INA228 U32 (R107 shunt) → FB7 → J4 | 5 V | — | ~0.3–0.5 A (backlight) | LCDwiki MSP4030 module, FT6336U via PCA9306 U63 | **DISP_EN (PC11)**, R104 pull-down default-off | runtime | C40/41 | D6 SMF5V0A TVS at connector | RT9742 inrush vs I_LIM open item | **PASS** |
| **GPS_VBAT / V_BCKP** | U34 TPS61094 (VIN=3V3, VOUT=GPS_VBAT); supercap C90 (DSF305Q3R0 3F) on SUP pin | ~3.3 V bypass / boost from supercap | supercap ≤2.55 V charge | µA holdover | ZED-F9T V_BCKP (pin36) | strapped EN=1/MODE=1 (R108/R110 to VOUT) auto buck/boost | autonomous | C92/94/96 | — | supercap ≤75 °C; **SUP node → ADC PA6 directly, no divider, contradicts §7 (B4)** | **WARNING** |
| **STM_VBAT** | U35 TPS61094 (VIN=3V3, VOUT=STM_VBAT); supercap C91 (3F) on SUP | ~3.3 V | supercap ≤2.55 V | µA | STM32 VBAT (pin6) | strapped EN/MODE auto | autonomous | C93/95/97/33/35 | — | SUP→ADC PB1 direct (B4) | **WARNING** |

### Netlist findings

| Net | Connected pins | Expected | Observed issue | Risk | Fix | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 3V3_STM | R106.2 (0.5Ω from 3V3), U12 VDD×5, all housekeeping ICs, J3.1 | Independently-powered always-on rail (per docs) | Fed from 3V3 only via **R106 = 0.5 Ω sense shunt**; no separate regulator | "Always-on 3V3_STM" collapses with 3V3; 0.5 Ω × ~0.5 A = 250 mV IR drop into STM32 VDD; shunt over a 0.5 A rail dissipates ~125 mW and degrades VDD regulation | Either accept that 3V3_STM≡3V3 (update docs to stop implying independence) **and** drop shunt to ~10–25 mΩ; or give 3V3_STM its own LDO if true always-on independence is intended | **FAIL** |
| VOUT_P | U7/U8 (bridge), U9.1, U28 PVDD/SVIN, U40 PVDD/SVIN, 100V caps | Rectified 37–57 V PD bus with surge clamp | No HV TVS (SMAJ58A / SMCJ58A) on the bus; only D2/D3 (5VWM) on signal pairs | PoE surge/transient (IEC 61000-4-5, cable transients) can exceed 100 V cap rating and stress U28/U40/Q2 | Add bus TVS (e.g. SMAJ58A) VOUT_P→VOUT_N at PD front end per NCP1095 app note | **WARNING** |
| BKP_GPS_SOC_V / BKP_STM_SOC_V | U34.6/U35.6 (SUP), C90/C91, U12.31/U12.36 (ADC), L4/L5 | Supercap SoC sense to ADC | SUP (live switching supercap node) wired **directly** to ADC; §7 specifies "/2 divider" (absent) | Switching noise on ADC; supercap node is fine ≤VDDA but no series R/filter; doc mismatch | Add series R (1–10 k) + filter cap to ADC; reconcile §7 (no divider needed since ≤2.55 V, but add RC) | **WARNING** |
| Net-(U28A-FB)=5V, U29.3 input | U29 VIN on 5.0 V | AP3441 Vin ≤5.5 V abs-max | 5.0 V nominal leaves 0.5 V to abs-max; 5V rail overshoot/ripple eats margin | Marginal abs-max on 3V3 and OCXO bucks (U29, U38) | Verify 5V transient ≤5.5 V, or drop 5V to 4.8–5.0 V w/ tight tolerance; confirm AP3441 OK at 5.0 V | **WARNING** |
| POE_PG | U9.14, U28.24 (EN), U55.24, R20.2 | PD power-good → main buck EN | OK — NCP1095 PG gates U28 enable | none | — | **PASS** |
| RB_PWR_EN | U12.93 (PB7), R156→Q18→U40.24 EN, R160/R164 pull-down, U46.16 | Rb buck EN + warm-up staging | Also drives U46 (SN65C3221 FORCEOFF?) pin16 — confirm intended dual use | Low | Verify PB7 fanout to U46.16 is intentional (RS232 enable tied to Rb power) | **PASS (verify)** |
| GBR | D1.3, U9.11 | NCP1095 gate-of-bridge / aux | D1 = BAV70 (dual diode) on GBR | none obvious | confirm GBR usage per NCP1095 | **PASS** |

### Design-intent mismatches

| Ref | Doc says | Schematic says | Severity |
|---|---|---|---|
| 3V3_STM | "always-on 3V3_STM (independent of gated rails); back-power-safe by being on always-on rail" (peripheral_map §4/§6) | 3V3_STM = 3V3 through R106 0.5 Ω shunt; same regulator, collapses together | **High** — the "independence" premise is false; only meaningful if 3V3 is itself always-on (it is, U29). Wording overstates separation; shunt value wrong |
| Backup SoC sense | §7: "PA6/PB1 /2 divider" | SUP node direct to ADC, no divider | Medium (functionally OK ≤2.55 V; add RC) |
| L7 Rb inductor | docs §5: "L7 40 µH" | MPN SRP1265A-6R8M = 6.8 µH | High (C1) |
| OCXO supply | peripheral_map §2: "10 MHz CMOS → PH0; 3.3 V" / "Vc 0.30–3.00 V" | OCXO rail = TPS7A52 3.33 V ✓; pre-reg U38 3.7 V | Low (consistent) |
| PoE class | "Type 2 min / Type 3 margin" | RCLA=232/RCLB=909 dual-resistor (bt-capable) | Low — verify exact class maps to ≥Type 2 |

### Layout-critical constraints for this block

| Net/class | Current est | Width/impedance | Placement / return-path | Evidence |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| VOUT_P 57 V bus | 0.6–0.8 A | wide, 57 V creepage/clearance | bridge U7/U8 → U28/U40 short; HV caps at buck inputs; Kelvin to U9 RDET/RCLASS | NCP1095 app note; net dump |
| U28A SW (L2), U29 LX (L3), U38 LX (L6) | 4 A / 3 A / 1 A | tight hot-loop, min area | input cap–FET–inductor loop minimal; SW copper minimized | MIC28516/AP3441 layout guidance |
| 3V3_STM shunt R106 | ~0.5 A | Kelvin sense to U31 IN+/IN- | shunt close to INA228 U31; **resize value** | net dump (R106 0.5Ω) |
| OCXO Vc loop-filter caps | n/a | — | C0G/NP0 only (X7R microphonics); short Vc trace PA4→Y3.1 | CLAUDE.md, peripheral_map §2 |
| Rb buck FB node (R134/R147/R148/U43) | high-Z | keep wiper/SPI noise off FB | digipot U43 + buffer U42 close; guard FB | sts1000_vcc_rb_supply.md |
| Supercap C90/C91 | charge/boost | thermal ≤75 °C | away from OCXO oven/Rb/bucks; 2.55 V derate | CLAUDE.md |
| TPS61094 SW (L4/L5) | backup current | min loop | near U34/U35; isolate SUP→ADC with RC | net dump |

### Summary
PoE input → bridge → NCP1095 → 5 V → 3V3 → per-rail LDOs/bucks is topologically sound and FB dividers compute to correct nominals (5.0 V, 3.33 V, OCXO 3.33 V). Backup managers are correctly strapped autonomous (EN/MODE=1/1). **Blocking issues before layout:** (1) L7 Rb inductor value/MPN contradiction; (2) 3V3_STM is the same rail as 3V3 via a 0.5 Ω shunt — both the value and the "independent always-on" doc premise are wrong; (3) D7 Rb TVS clamp voltage unspecified. **Strong warnings:** missing HV bus TVS on the 57 V rail; AP3441 5.0 V-in vs 5.5 V abs-max margin; supercap SUP node tied to ADC without RC/divider (doc says /2 divider). PoE classification uses correct dual-resistor bt scheme but exact class needs datasheet confirmation against Type 2/3 target.

## 11. Interface review

## Interface-by-Interface Pre-Layout Review — STS1000 "Meridian"

Scope: the 13 buses/interfaces in `docs/ntp_server_peripheral_map.md`. Connectivity verified against `ntp-server-stm32.net` (KiCad 10, 551 comps / 442 nets); external facts verified against vendor datasheets where noted. Reference is by designator+pin.

### Master interface table

| Interface | Nets / key designators | Voltage domain | Termination | Pull-ups/downs | Protection/ESD | Impedance | Length matching | Connector notes | Layout notes | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| **I²C1 (PB8/PB9)** | `I2C_SCL`/`I2C_SDA`; U12.95/96; bus nodes U10,U23,U26,U30,U31,U32,U37,U44,U54,U55,U56,U57,U58,U59,U60,U61,U63 | 3V3_STM (all nodes on always-on rail per doc) | none (open-drain) | R202/R203 = 4.7k → 3V3_STM (single main pair, correct) | none on-board (internal); LTC4311 U56 accelerator | n/a (≤400 kHz) | n/a | n/a | LTC4311 U56 EN(pin3) **hard-tied 3V3_STM** | **WARNING** — see B1 |

| **RMII / Eth+PTP** | U11 LAN8742; RMII PA1/PC1/PA2/PC4/PC5/PA5/PA7/PB10/PB12/PB15; MDI TRD0/TRD1; ETH_PPS_OUT PB5 | 3V3 / 3V3_LAN | R31–34 100Ω series on RX/MODE; MDI R42–45 49.9Ω→3V3_LAN (datasheet-correct) | RBIAS R37 12.1k✓; MDIO R36 1.5k✓ | U1 TPD4EUSB30 on MDI | RMII 50Ω SE; MDI 100Ω diff | **TX/RX RMII group + MDI pairs must be length-matched** | J1 0826-1X1T magjack, **no footprint** | strap latch risk on MODE/PHYAD | **FAIL** — see B2 |
| **PoE** | J1 VC1–4 (TR0–3_TAP)→U7/U8 FDMQ8205A bridge→U9 NCP1095; POE_KILL PE15 | 48 V PoE / PD rail | bridge + PD per NCP1095 | POE_KILL R17 pulldown (default-RUN)✓ | center-tap caps; TVS in PoE sheet (not audited here) | high-V isolation/creepage | n/a | magjack VC pins (4-pair) | classify Type 2 min / Type 3 margin | **PASS (cond.)** — see O-PoE |
| **USB-C console** | J5 GCT USB4120; PA11/PA12; `USB_VBUS_SENSE` PE2 | 3V3 logic, 5 V VBUS sense | n/a | CC1/CC2 R66/R64 = **5.1k Rd**✓ (UFP sink); VBUS div R67 121k/R68 100k | U18 TPD4E05U06 (D±,VBUS); U65 ESD on CC | 90Ω diff (USB2.0 FS) | DP/DM pair match | D1±/D2± tied (reversible)✓; SHIELD via C42/R65 to GND✓ | self-powered, DP pull-up gated by PE2 | **PASS** |

| **RF: ext 10 MHz SMA** | J8→C149 AC-couple + D8 SZESD7410→U49 TMUX1101 (term, REF_TERM_EN PC10)→U50 LTC6752xS5→R184 33Ω→mux I1 + PB14 | 3V0_RF island | switched 50Ω (U49) | self-bias slicer | D8 ESD on SMA; D21 VCC guard on U50 | 50Ω at 10 MHz (low) | n/a | J8 SMA **no footprint** | PB14 taps slicer out as EXTREF_MON | **WARNING** — see B3 (net naming) |
| **Display + touch** | ST7796 SPI (PE9 CS, PB0 DC, PA8 RST, PE6 BL); touch via U63 PCA9306; rail 5V_DISP (U33 RT9742, DISP_EN PC11) | 5V_DISP gated; logic 3V3 | R210/R211 22Ω series | DISP_EN R104 pulldown (default-off)✓ | U15/U16/U19/U20 TPD4E02B04 (ctrl/SPI 3.3V); U17/U18 TPD4E05U06 (5 V touch) | SPI ≤40 MHz | n/a | J4 (display FFC/header) | PCA9306 VREF1=3V3_STM/VREF2=5V_DISP/EN=DISP_EN✓ | **PASS** |
| **ADC analog senses** | PA3 OCXO_V (Vc), PA6 BKP_GPS_SOC_V, PB1 BKP_STM_SOC_V | VDDA 3V3 | n/a | SOC /2 dividers (per doc) | n/a | n/a | n/a | n/a | Vc no divider (≤3.0 V); keep Vc-sense away from switchers | **PASS** |
| **DAC (OCXO steer)** | PA4 OCXO_VC → loop filter → Y3 Vc; OCXO out Y3.4→R123 22Ω→mux I0 | VDDA / 3V3_CLK | R123 22Ω source term at driver✓ | Vc bias to ~1.65 V (loop filter) | n/a | n/a | n/a | n/a | **Vc-path caps must be C0G/film, never X7R** — audit in OCXO sheet | **PASS (cond.)** — see O-OCXO |

### Netlist findings

| Net | Connected pins | Expected | Observed issue | Risk | Fix | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| `WDT_EN` | U12.68 (PA9), U64.6 (SET1), R213 | doc §4/§8: PA9 = `I2C_BUF_EN` → LTC4311 EN | **PA9 reassigned to WDT_EN; LTC4311 EN tied to 3V3_STM** | Med — loses firmware I²C bus-recovery; doc/sch disagree | Reconcile: keep PA9=WDT_EN and update docs, OR free a pin for I2C_BUF_EN | FAIL (doc mismatch) |
| `Net-(U11-RXD0/MODE0)` etc. (U11 pins 7,8,10,11) | only R31–34 (to MCU RMII) + U11 strap pins | strap latched at reset by a dedicated pull at the PHY pin | **MODE0/1/2, PHYAD0, RXER straps have NO pull at PHY**; only 100Ω series to high-Z MCU RMII pins | High — PHY mode/address undefined at reset | Add strap pulls (e.g. 10k) at U11 pins 7/8/10/11 to set RMII/100/PHYAD per checklist | FAIL |
| `10MHz_CLK_OUT` | U12.53 (PB14), U52.1 (mux I1), R184 | doc: PB14 = `EXTREF_MON` watching mux input B | Connectivity correct (PB14 taps slicer→I1) but **net name implies an output**, not the EXTREF_MON capture input | Low — naming/clarity defect | Rename net to `EXT_REF_IN`/`EXTREF_MON` | WARNING |
| `CLK_OUT` (PH0) | U12.12 (PH0), R187, mux Y | PH0 = `OSC_IN`/HSE-bypass input | net named `CLK_OUT` for an oscillator **input** | Low — naming defect | Rename to `OSC_IN` | WARNING |
| `R44` = 49.9Ω on TRD0_N | J1.10, R44, U1.2, U11.20 | per CLAUDE.md TODO "drop legacy R44 at PC12 (double pull-up)" | **R44 is now an Ethernet MDI 49.9Ω term**, NOT an INA_ALERT pull-up | Info — stale action | Close the "drop R44" action; INA_ALERT pull-up is R199 only | RESOLVED |
| `INA_ALERT_INT_N` | U12.80 (PC12), U54.15 (INTB), R199 | single 10k pull-up | exactly R199 present; no R44 conflict | none | none | PASS |
| `EXP_RST_N` | U12.15 (PC0), U54.14, U55.14, R198 | shared expander /RESET + pull | correct (R198 pulldown) | none | none | PASS |
| `GPS_RST_N`/`GPS_SAFEBOOT_N` | PD11/PD15 + U21 only | module inputs deasserted at MCU reset | **no external pulls**; relies on F9T internal pull-ups | Low | Confirm F9T internal pulls hold reset/safeboot deasserted while MCU high-Z | WARNING |
| `Net-(J5-SHIELD)` | J5.S1–4, C42, R65 (1M) | chassis bleed RC | OK (C42 + 1M to GND) | none | none | PASS |

### Design-intent mismatches

| Ref | Doc says | Schematic says | Severity |
|---|---|---|---|
| PA9 | §4/§8: PA9 = `I2C_BUF_EN`, LTC4311 EN driven for bus recovery | PA9 = `WDT_EN`→U64.SET1; LTC4311 EN = 3V3_STM | High |
| PHY straps | §1/§14: MODE/PHYAD/nINTSEL strapped at reset | MODE/PHYAD/RXER float through 100Ω to high-Z MCU; no PHY-pin pulls | High |
| PB14 | §2.1: `EXTREF_MON` (TIM12 capture of input B) | net `10MHz_CLK_OUT` (correct node, wrong/misleading name) | Low |
| PH0 | `OSC_IN` | net `CLK_OUT` | Low |
| PE4 | §6: `RB_SER_MODE` | net `RB_RS232_CMOS_SW` (same function) | Info |
| R44/PC12 | CLAUDE.md TODO: drop R44 (double pull-up) | R44 is Ethernet MDI 49.9Ω term; action stale | Info (close it) |

### Layout-critical constraints for these interfaces

| Net/class | Current est | Width/impedance | Placement / return path | Evidence |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| MDI TRD0/TRD1 pairs | signal | 100Ω diff, tight match | PHY↔J1 short, ground moat under magjack, R42–45+bypass near PHY | Microchip LAN8742A QFN checklist |
| RMII bus (REF_CLK + 8 sig) | signal | 50Ω SE, group-matched, REF_CLK guarded | PHY↔MCU, 50 MHz; series R31–34 near PHY | doc §1 |
| OCXO out→mux I0 (R123) | signal | 50Ω, source-term at Y3 | series term at driver; no rx-end R; C0G/film only on Vc path | CLAUDE.md, doc §2 |
| ext-ref 10 MHz island (3V0_RF) | signal | 50Ω to slicer | isolate RF island; D8/U49/U50 near SMA J8 | RF doc |
| GPS RF (1.5 GHz) | RF + 5 V bias | 50Ω | polymer ESD (L10) + bias-T (L1) at J7; GDT off-board | doc §3, gnss_antenna_bias doc |
| USB DP/DM | FS | 90Ω diff | short, ESD U18 at J5 | USB2.0 |
| PoE 48 V (VC taps→bridge) | up to ~0.6 A | wide, creepage | isolation/clearance per 802.3bt | doc §6 |

### Verified-good highlights
- I²C addressing straps correct: INA228 A0/A1 4-level on bus lines; U54=0x21 (A0→VS), U55=0x20 (A0→GND); INT pull-ups R199/R200/R201 + R198 EXP_RST present.
- USB-C is a correct UFP/sink: CC1/CC2 5.1k Rd, VBUS sense divider, reversible D± tie, shield RC.
- GNSS UART/PPS/control mapping matches doc 1:1 (PD8/PD9, PA0, PC6, PD11, PD15, PD7, PD6, PD5); V_USB grounded.
- LAN8742 MDI 49.9Ω→VDD and RBIAS 12.1k match the Microchip reference (initial "series-R-in-MDI" concern dismissed).
- Clock chain: Y3→R123→mux I0; slicer→R184→mux I1+PB14; mux Y→R187→PH0 and →U53 buffer→bench fanout. Topology sound.

Sources: [LAN8742A QFN Schematic Checklist (Microchip)](https://ww1.microchip.com/downloads/en/DeviceDoc/LAN8742A%20QFN%20Rev%20A%20Schematic%20Checklist.pdf), [LTC4311 datasheet (Analog Devices)](https://www.analog.com/media/en/technical-documentation/data-sheets/4311fa.pdf)

## 12–13. Pre-layout constraint package & KiCad rule suggestions

## Pre-Layout Constraint Package + KiCad Net-Class / Rule Suggestions — STS1000 "Meridian"

Scope: ready-for-layout constraints, not fab-ready. Currents are estimates from `peripheral_map §6` and subsystem docs; impedance/length-match targets need a board-house/field-solver pass once the stackup is fixed. Defaults assumed: 1 oz ext / 0.5 oz int Cu, 10–20 °C rise, FR-4, **stackup TBD**. Every Z, diff-pair geometry, and minimum-width-for-rise number below is flagged where it depends on copper weight / stackup that is not yet committed.

Evidence basis: `docs/ntp_server_peripheral_map.md §1–9`, `docs/sts1000_clock_mux.md §7`, `docs/ntp_server_rf_frontend.md §7`, `docs/gnss_antenna_bias_supervisor.md §3,10`, `docs/sts1000_vcc_rb_supply.md §1–4`, `hardware/CLAUDE.md` (layout-critical rules), netlist `ntp-server-stm32.net` (VOUT_P/VOUT_N/V_POE topology).

---

### 1) Net-class / constraint table

| Net / class | Function | Voltage | Est current | Min width | Clearance | Impedance | Length match | Return path | Layer pref | Placement / routing notes | Evidence / assumption |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| **POE_HV (VOUT_P, VOUT_N, V_POE)** | PoE PD output / intermediate rail into U28 MIC28516 main buck, U29, Rb buck, U10 INA228 IN+ | ~37–57 V (PD), VOUT_P after bridge | up to ~0.7 A in (25–30 W peak / ~48 V) | **≥0.4–0.5 mm** pour/poly, prefer plane fill | **≥0.5 mm air, ≥1.0 mm to LV/SELV nets** | n/a | n/a | adjacent plane, tight loop | Keep VOUT_P↔VOUT_N hot loop tiny; bulk caps C6/C7/C9/C11 (VOUT_N) + C8/C10/C75/C77/C80 (VOUT_P) at the bridge/PD; route as poured copper not traces | net `VOUT_P`/`VOUT_N` topology in netlist; `peripheral_map §6`; clearance is mains-adjacent practice (Low confidence on exact creepage — see blockers) |
| **PoE_MAGJACK_PAIRS (RMII MDI / center taps)** | 4 twisted pairs from RJ45 magjack center taps (Mode A+B) to FDMQ8205A bridges U7/U8 | PoE common-mode | per pair share of PD current | ≥0.3 mm | **isolation barrier: ≥1.5 mm primary-secondary, follow magjack pinout** | 100 Ω diff (MDI side) | match within pair | continuous plane under MDI; **plane cutout under the isolation gap only** | Bob Smith termination + common-mode caps at magjack; keep chassis/earth gap under the magjack | `checklist §8/§9`; isolation is standard Ethernet-PoE practice (Medium) |
| **BUCK_HOTLOOP_MAIN (U28 SW→L→Cout, Cin loop)** | MIC28516 main buck switching node | up to ~24 V swing | several A | wide poly, short | keep SW copper minimal | n/a | n/a | dedicated power-GND under loop | **Smallest possible Cin→FET→GND loop**; SW node small copper (EMI vs thermal trade); Cout close to inductor; boot cap C124-equiv at the pin | `checklist §9`, MIC28516 is a sync buck (Medium) |
| **BUCK_HOTLOOP_RB (U40A MIC28516 SW→L7→COUT)** | VCC_RB adjustable buck, 5–24 V @ ~1.5 A | up to 24 V | ~1.5 A steady, surge on Rb warm-up | wide poly | **VCC_RB rated ≥100 V parts; 0.5 mm clearance** | n/a | n/a | tight loop | COUT bank C126/C127/C128 (≥63 V); L7 40 µH; keep wiper/SPI noise off FB node (high-Z) | `vcc_rb_supply.md §1,2`; FB-node rule = `hardware/CLAUDE.md` (High) |
| **VCC_RB_OUTPUT** | Rb supply to FE-5680A connector | 5–24 V (15 V nom) | ~1.5 A | ≥0.5 mm | **0.5 mm; TVS D7 1.5SMCJ28A at connector** | n/a | n/a | adjacent GND | OV latch (U41A) trip @26 V autonomous; D7 at connector pads; R159 shunt Kelvin (see below) | `vcc_rb_supply.md §1,4` (High) |
| **SHUNT_KELVIN (INA228 ×8, INA181)** | current-sense shunts R16/R126 25 m, R72/R106 500 m, R89/R107 100 m, R30 150 m, R102 75 m, R159 20 m; R77 3.3 Ω (INA181) | per rail | per rail | **wide power in/out; Kelvin sense traces thin** | std | n/a | match the two sense traces | **4-terminal Kelvin: IN+/IN− tap the pads symmetrically, never the power copper**; INA181 IN+ on V_ANT/upstream side of R77, IN− load side (reversed = reads 0) | `bom.md` SHUNT-REVIEW list; INA181 orientation = `antenna_supervisor §10` (High) |
| **RMII_BUS (RXD0/1, TXD0/1, TX_EN, CRS_DV, REF_CLK, MDC, MDIO)** | LAN8742 ↔ STM32 RMII, AF11 | 3.3 V | logic | ≥0.15 mm | std | ~50 Ω single-ended (TBD stackup) | **REF_CLK is the critical net; group-match TXD/RXD/CRS_DV to within ~±25 mm of REF_CLK** | continuous GND under all RMII | inner/adjacent-to-plane | Keep REF_CLK (PA1) short, single load; MDIO 1.5 kΩ pull-up to VDDIO; PB10 RXER/PHYAD0 strap kept high-Z thru reset | `peripheral_map §1`; RMII is source-synchronous so loose match OK (Medium) |
| **USB_DP/DM (PA11/PA12)** | USB-FS device console | 3.3 V diff | logic | per 90 Ω geom | std + guard | **90 Ω differential** (TBD stackup) | **intra-pair ≤ ~5 mm** | continuous GND, no split | Short stub, ESD array at connector, away from switchers; series Rs only if host needs | `peripheral_map §10`; 90 Ω USB std (High intent / Medium geometry) |
| **GPS_RF (SMA → bias-T → ZED-F9T RF_IN)** | 1.575 GHz GNSS RF + 5 V DC bias | RF + 5 V | RF + ≤180 mA bias | **50 Ω geometry** | guard ring | **50 Ω single-ended** (TBD stackup) | n/a | **continuous unbroken GND, via-fence the trace** | L1 56 nH bias-T choke (>500 Ω @ L1 band); ESD must be **Cj ≤0.2–0.3 pF polymer + separate coaxial GDT for outdoor run** (standard clock-line ESD fails RF+bias) | `antenna_supervisor §3`; ESD = `hardware/CLAUDE.md` (High) |
| **REF_RF_10M (10MHz_RF_IN SMA → N1 → comparator)** | external 10 MHz reference, sine/CMOS | ≤±7 Vpk transient | µA–mA | 50 Ω geom | guard | **50 Ω SMA→N1** (TBD) | n/a | **one continuous plane SMA→comparator→mux, NO split / star / bridge** | R177 close to N1; D11 (SZESD7410) at SMA pads; C149 immediately after; stitch GND vias along the 50 Ω trace and around U50 | `rf_frontend.md §7` (High) |
| **CLK_PH0 (mux Y → R187 → PH0)** | HSE-bypass clock into STM32 OSC_IN | 3.3 V CMOS 10 MHz | logic | ≥0.15 mm | guard | controlled, short | n/a | **continuous GND under CLK_OUT to STM32** | U52 adjacent to PH0; keep Y→R187→PH0 short & direct; U52 GND = pin 2 only | `clock_mux.md §7` (High) |
| **REF_CLK_NODES (OCXO_CLK_OUT, 10MHz_CLK_OUT, mux Y node)** | OCXO & ext-ref squares into mux | 3.0 V CMOS | logic | ≥0.15 mm | guard | source-term at driver (R98/R123 22 Ω, R144 33 Ω) | n/a | continuous plane | **No receiver-end series R** (term at driver only); keep input stubs short | `clock_mux.md §2,7`; `hardware/CLAUDE.md` (High) |
| **BENCH_10M_OUT (U53 → R189 → C160 → SMA)** | 50 Ω bench fanout | 3.3 V CMOS | 50 Ω load | 50 Ω geom | guard | **50 Ω** | n/a | continuous GND, steer away from PH0 | D16 SZESD7410 at SMA pads; isolated buffer U53 so SMA load never reaches PH0 | `clock_mux.md §3.3,7` (High) |
| **OCXO_VC (PA4 DAC → loop filter → Vc pin1; PA3 sense)** | OCXO steering voltage, ultra-sensitive analog | 0.3–3.0 V (center 1.65 V) | µA | ≥0.2 mm | **guard / quiet analog region** | n/a | n/a | quiet analog GND, away from SW nodes | **Vc-path caps C0G/NP0 or film — NEVER X7R** (microphonic FM); never leave Vc floating; keep loop filter away from bucks/digital | `peripheral_map §2`; `hardware/CLAUDE.md` (High) |
| **RB_FB_NODE (U40A FB: R147/R148/R144/C125/R134)** | Rb buck feedback, high-impedance | ~0.6 V | µA | thin, short | guard | n/a | n/a | quiet GND | **Keep digipot wiper / SPI switching noise off this node**; fixed bounding R147/R148 set absolute V envelope; place R147/R148/R134/C125 tight to FB pin | `vcc_rb_supply.md §1,2`; `hardware/CLAUDE.md` (High) |
| **LSE_XTAL (PC14/PC15, Y2 32.768 kHz)** | RTC crystal | low | µA | short, guard ring | **guard ring + GND island under xtal** | n/a | match the two legs | local guarded GND, no signals under | Load caps tight; keep away from switchers and clock nets | `checklist §1` (High) |
| **HSE_XTAL_PHY (Y1 25 MHz @ U11)** | PHY reference crystal | 3.3 V | µA | short | guard ring | n/a | match legs | local GND island | Load caps at xtal pins; short legs | `checklist §8` (Medium) |
| **NOISY_SW / FAN / BL_PWM (FAN_PWM PE5, DISP_BL PE6, RGB PD12-14)** | PWM / switching control | 3.3 V | logic | ≥0.15 mm | std | n/a | n/a | keep off sensitive analog | Route FAN_PWM, BL PWM away from OCXO_VC / REF_VMID / ADC sense nets | `peripheral_map §8` (Medium) |
| **ADC_SENSE (PA6, PB1 SOC; PA3 Vc)** | supercap SOC + Vc analog inputs | ≤3.3 V | µA | ≥0.2 mm | guard | n/a | n/a | quiet analog GND | /2 dividers near MCU; keep away from SW/PWM; star to AGND if used | `peripheral_map §7` (High) |
| **I2C1_BUS (PB8 SCL / PB9 SDA, ~15 nodes)** | housekeeping I²C, 400 kHz | 3.3 V | logic | ≥0.15 mm | std | n/a | n/a | continuous GND | LTC4311 accelerator (U56) + single pull-up pair; keep total Cb in budget; route as a spine, short stubs to each device | `peripheral_map §4` (High) |
| **SPI4_BUS (PE11-14 + CS PE9/PD2/PE11, ~20–40 MHz)** | NOR + TFT + digipot | 3.3 V | logic | ≥0.15 mm | std | controlled if long | group SCK/MOSI loosely | continuous GND | TFT branch gets R210/R211 22 Ω series; keep SCK clean to NOR; digipot CS noise off FB | `peripheral_map §5`, `checklist §13` (Medium) |
| **MAG_GNDPOUR (under U61 IIS2MDC)** | magnetometer keep-out | n/a | **no DC current** | n/a | n/a | n/a | n/a | **continuous current-free GND pour, NO void, NO routed return** | Balanced go+return only; place U61 far from Rb/OCXO/bucks/PoE magnetics/fan; board edge/corner or external puck | `peripheral_map §4`; `hardware/CLAUDE.md` (High) |
| **SUPERCAP_THERMAL (DSF305Q3R0 ×2)** | backup energy | 2.55 V peak | charge/discharge A | wide | std | n/a | n/a | adjacent GND | **Placement ≤ ~75 °C** (2.5 V/85 °C derate at 2.55 V); keep away from Rb/OCXO ovens, bucks, bridge | `hardware/CLAUDE.md`; `peripheral_map §14` (High) |
| **PROG_DEBUG (PA13 SWDIO, PA14 SWCLK, PB3 SWO, NRST)** | SWD/trace header | 3.3 V | logic | ≥0.2 mm | std | SWCLK short | n/a | GND adjacent, ground pin on header | Place header accessibly; series R / pull on SWCLK optional; NRST cap | `peripheral_map §10` (High) |
| **TEST_POINTS (per subsystem docs)** | bring-up taps | various | n/a | n/a | n/a | n/a | n/a | n/a | RF: N1, N2, REF_VMID, 3V0_RF, U50 VCC, 10MHz_CLK_OUT (`rf_frontend §7`); mux: Y, CLK_OUT, 10MHz_RF_OUT, 3V3_CLK (`clock_mux §7`) | docs (High) |

### 2) Decoupling / placement-critical table

| RefDes | Related IC / net | Purpose | Must be close to | Max distance | Priority | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| C158 | U52 74LVC1G157 VCC pin5 | mux supply decouple | U52 pin 5 | <2 mm | High | `clock_mux §3.5` |
| C159 | U53 74LVC1G34 VCC pin5 | fanout buf decouple | U53 pin 5 | <2 mm | High | `clock_mux §3.5` |
| C157 + FB10 | 3V3_CLK rail entry | bulk + isolation | FB10 output | <5 mm | High | VDD-domain only, ≤VDD so PH0 not over-driven |
| C134/C137, FB9 | U51 LT3045 (RF island) Cin/Cout | low-noise island | U51 in/out pins | <3 mm | High | `rf_frontend §4.7` |
| R186, R185 (Kelvin GND) | U51 LT3045 SET/ILIM | reference accuracy | route GND back to U51 GND pin | device-level | High | LT3045 Kelvin requirement, same plane (`rf_frontend §7`) |
| 0.1 µF + 1 µF | U50 LTC6752 VCC pin5 (+ R143/D14) | comparator supply | U50 pin 5 | <2 mm | High | abs-max guard tight to pin (`rf_frontend §4.6`) |
| REF_VMID 0.1 µF | U50 −IN / R142 | threshold bias | U50 | <3 mm | High | `rf_frontend §4.6` |
| C149 | 10MHz_RF_IN | DC block | immediately after SMA/D11 | <3 mm | High | `rf_frontend §7` |
| C52, C61, FB4 | bias-T node A / V_ANT | RF return + decouple | L1 / antenna feed node | <3 mm | High | `antenna_supervisor §3` |
| OCXO Vc caps | PA4 loop filter / Vc | steering integrity | OCXO Vc pin | <5 mm | Critical | C0G/NP0/film only, never X7R (`hardware/CLAUDE.md`) |
| C115 (2.2 µF), C120 | U45 MCP1502-40 ref out / OV ref node | ref stability | U45 OUT / OV (−) node | <3 mm | High | `vcc_rb_supply §2,4` |
| C124 (boot), Cin | U40A MIC28516 BST / VIN | buck operation | U40A pins | <2 mm | High | hot-loop critical (`vcc_rb_supply §2`) |
| C126/127/128 | VCC_RB COUT | output bulk | L7 output | <5 mm | High | ≥63 V, DC-bias derate |
| Cin/Cout banks | U28/U29 main bucks | hot loop | FET/inductor | <2 mm | Critical | smallest Cin→FET→GND loop |
| INA228 ×8 0.1 µF (VS) | each INA228 VS pin | sensor supply | each INA pin | <2 mm | Medium | all on 3V3_STM |
| C28–C31 bank | U24 INA181 / U25 LMV393 | supervisor decouple | each V+ pin | <2 mm | Medium | `antenna_supervisor §11` |
| Load caps | Y2 LSE 32.768 kHz | xtal stability | PC14/PC15 pins | <3 mm | High | guard ring + GND island |
| Load caps | Y1 PHY 25 MHz | xtal stability | U11 xtal pins | <3 mm | High | short legs |
| VDD/VDDA + VREF+ caps | U12 STM32 each supply pin | MCU decouple | each VDD/VDDA pin | <2 mm | Critical | one cap per supply pin + bulk |
| C160 | bench fanout | DC block | after R189 → SMA | <5 mm | Medium | `clock_mux §3.3` |
| U56 LTC4311 | I2C1 SCL/SDA | rise-time accel | near bus midpoint/load | placement | Medium | `peripheral_map §4` |

---

### 3) Suggested KiCad net classes + custom rules

| Net class | Nets (examples) | Width | Clearance | Via | DiffPair W/G | Z target | Length match | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| `PoE_HV` | VOUT_P, VOUT_N, V_POE | ≥0.5 mm (poly/plane) | **≥0.5 mm air; ≥1.0 mm to SELV** | large / multiple | — | — | — | **Needs creepage confirmation (PD output voltage class) + Cu weight for current.** Stackup-dependent. |
| `PoE_ISO` | magjack center-tap pairs, primary side of FDMQ8205A | ≥0.3 mm | **isolation barrier per magjack pinout (≥1.5 mm)** | — | 100 Ω | within pair | — | **Mechanical/creepage confirmation required.** |
| `Power_Buck` | SW nodes, VCC_RB out, 5V, 3V3 mains | ≥0.4 mm (current-dependent) | 0.3 mm | thermal/multiple | — | — | — | **Width needs Cu weight + 10–20 °C rise calc once stackup set.** |
| `Shunt_Kelvin` | INA228/INA181 IN+/IN− sense pairs | thin sense, wide power | std | — | route as pair | — | match sense legs | Kelvin tap at pad, not power copper. Shunt values still **SHUNT-REVIEW (TBD)**. |
| `RF_50` | 10MHz_RF_IN, 10MHz_RF_OUT, GPS_RF_IN | per 50 Ω geom | guard | via-fence | — | **50 Ω SE** | — | **Z needs field-solver + stackup.** Continuous unbroken GND. |
| `DiffPair_USB` | USB_DP/DM | per geom | guard | — | per 90 Ω | **90 Ω diff** | intra-pair ≤5 mm | **Geometry needs stackup.** |
| `DiffPair_MDI` | RMII MDI pairs (magjack side) | per geom | std | — | per 100 Ω | **100 Ω diff** | within pair | **Geometry needs stackup.** |
| `Clk_CMOS` | OCXO_CLK_OUT, 10MHz_CLK_OUT, CLK_OUT, mux Y | ≥0.15 mm | guard | — | — | source-term @ driver | — | No receiver-end series R; short; continuous GND. |
| `Clk_RMII` | RMII_REF_CLK (PA1) + RMII data group | ≥0.15 mm | std | — | — | ~50 Ω | group ±25 mm to REF_CLK | Source-synchronous; loose match OK. |
| `Analog_Quiet` | OCXO_VC, RB_FB, REF_VMID, ADC sense (PA3/PA6/PB1) | ≥0.2 mm | guard | — | — | — | — | Away from SW/PWM; quiet AGND; Vc caps C0G/film only. |
| `Xtal` | LSE (PC14/15), PHY 25 MHz | short | guard ring | — | — | — | match legs | GND island under, no signals beneath. |
| `I2C_400k` | I2C1 SCL/SDA | ≥0.15 mm | std | — | — | — | — | LTC4311 + single pull-up pair; bus spine. |
| `Debug` | SWDIO/SWCLK/SWO/NRST | ≥0.2 mm | std | — | — | — | — | SWCLK short; accessible header. |
| `Default` | everything else | ≥0.15 mm | 0.15 mm | std | — | — | — | Baseline. |

**Rules that explicitly need confirmation before they can be finalized:**
- **All impedance targets** (`RF_50`, `DiffPair_USB`, `DiffPair_MDI`, `Clk_RMII`) — require committed **stackup + field-solver / board-house** numbers. Geometry placeholder only.
- **All current-driven widths** (`PoE_HV`, `Power_Buck`) — require committed **copper weight** + the 10–20 °C rise target to compute via IPC-2152.
- **`PoE_HV` / `PoE_ISO` clearance & creepage** — require the **PD-side voltage class and isolation/safety requirement** (is the PD front end isolated? `peripheral_map §14` open item: NCL/NCM/LCF direction & "digital isolator required only if PD front end is isolated"). This drives both the magjack isolation gap and the HV net clearance.
- **Magnetometer keep-out geometry** (`B = (μ₀/2π)·I/r`) — needs the worst-case adjacent DC-rail current and the acceptable field at the sensor to size the keep-out radius.

---

### Design-intent mismatches (doc-vs-doc / doc-vs-schematic to resolve before layout)

| Ref | Doc says | Schematic / other doc says | Severity |
|---|---|---|---|
| OCXO source term | `clock_mux.md` cites **R98** (and "R123" in one place) as OCXO 22 Ω source term; `hardware/CLAUDE.md` & `checklist §2` say **R123** | Designator collision unresolved (TODO marker in clock_mux) | Medium — confirm the real refdes before placing the term resistor |
| Bias-T choke | `antenna_supervisor §3` body says **L1 = 56 nH**; `checklist §7` and `hardware/CLAUDE.md` say **L1 47 nH** | Value mismatch (56 nH gives the cited 554 Ω @ 1.575 GHz; 47 nH does not) | High — wrong value changes RF isolation; resolve before layout |
| RF front-end designators | `rf_frontend.md` carries an explicit unresolved old→new designator remap (C133–C137, R134–R147, D11–D15) | Re-annotated schematic refs not confirmed 1:1 | Medium — refdes ambiguity blocks placement/BOM cross-check |
| R44 at PC12 | `peripheral_map §4` / checklist: "drop legacy R44 (double pull-up)" | `hardware/CLAUDE.md` TODO: "R44 is now a 49.9 Ω Ethernet PHY term; only R199 remains" | Low — verify R44 is not a stray second INA_ALERT pull-up |
| PG_IN_N net label | checklist/peripheral_map: fix `PG_IN_N`→`PG_INT_N` (one-pin net otherwise) | `hardware/CLAUDE.md` TODO marks it already `PG_INT_N` | Low — confirm in netlist |
| INA_ALERT_N dangling | `net_naming.md`: `INA_ALERT_N` is a **1-pin dangling net** defect on the MCU, should merge into `INA_ALERT_INT_N` | present in netlist | Medium — a 1-pin net = missing connection; fix before layout |

This is a constraint/rule package; it does not re-verify every IC pinout (that is the IC-by-IC review's job). The blockers below are the items that must be answered before net classes can be turned into final DRC rules.

## 14. Open questions (cannot verify — info needed)

- (PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)) Confirm R16 (RSNS) value sets the intended NCP1095 hard/soft overcurrent limit for ~25-30W cold-start with Rb+OCXO concurrent; pick sense-grade MPN/footprint.
- (PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)) Confirm R30 (INA228 #1 shunt) full-scale vs max Class-6 input current (~1.1A @ ~48V) and ADCRANGE setting.
- (PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)) Bench-validate GBR-low forces U7/U8 to body-diode mode so VOUT_P/V_KBIAS survive the AUX kill (doc open item 1).
- (PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)) Confirm FDMC8622 (Q2) datasheet pinout vs assigned 8-PowerWDFN footprint (S=1-3, G=4, D=5-8+pad) — orientation correctness.
- (PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)) Resolve all REVIEW-HV PoE caps (C6,C7,C9,C11) to exact MPN + voltage + dielectric; verify C11 47pF AUX filter matches NCP1095 Cb recommendation.
- (PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)) Source D4 12V Zener (MPN/footprint) and confirm R18 uprated to >=1/4W.
- (PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)) Confirm NCP1095 Class 6 (RCLASSA 232 / RCLASSB 909) is the intended classification (Type 3/bt, 51W) and that it advertises >= the project minimum Type 2 — Class 6 satisfies 'Type 2 min / Type 3 margin'.
- (PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)) Confirm AUX divider (R27 10k / R29 100k \|\| 265k internal) yields ~10.5V > AUX_H and that the kill network reference domains (GND/RTN vs VOUT_N) are wired so input stages do not re-assert as RTN rises (depends on fixing the Q3/R21/KILL_N miswire first).
- (5V/3V3 main power supply (sheet 3v3-main-power.kicad_sch)) MIC28516 EXTVDD (U28 pin23) is tied to GND. Confirm against the datasheet pin description that GND (not float) is the correct unused-EXTVDD state (eval board ties it low; not directly quoted). Confidence Medium.
- (5V/3V3 main power supply (sheet 3v3-main-power.kicad_sch)) U28 FREQ divider R90 200k / R91 100k (Vfreq = VIN/3): confirm the resulting switching frequency against MIC28516 datasheet Table 5-1 (FREQ-vs-Fsw). Topology correct, target Fsw unverified.
- (5V/3V3 main power supply (sheet 3v3-main-power.kicad_sch)) U28 ILIM resistor R93 2.21k (96uA source, V_CL=212mV): confirm current-limit trip current vs low-side RDS(on) gives adequate headroom over 5V-rail peak (incl. Rb cold-start surge through VOUT_P) but below inductor Isat.
- (5V/3V3 main power supply (sheet 3v3-main-power.kicad_sch)) U28 SS cap C63 10nF on SS pin: confirm soft-start time is acceptable for PoE inrush/PD power-up sequencing.
- (5V/3V3 main power supply (sheet 3v3-main-power.kicad_sch)) R97 top FB resistor = 15k exceeds the datasheet-recommended R1 range (3k-10k); confirm FB-node noise immunity or drop to <=10k with matched R98.
- (5V/3V3 main power supply (sheet 3v3-main-power.kicad_sch)) Verify the 8-UFDFN(Exposed Pad) library footprint pad numbering for U29/U38 once the AP3441 symbol is corrected (must match the corrected pin order, EP=PGND).
- (5V/3V3 main power supply (sheet 3v3-main-power.kicad_sch)) Confirm L3 (2.2uH, 4.15A Irms) has margin for the full 3V3 load incl 3V3_STM branch (estimate ~1.5-2.5A) plus ripple; SRP/DR73 derate at temperature.
- (Supercap backup supplies (U34/U35 TPS61094 ×2 + DSF305Q3R0 3F supercaps)) ZED-F9T V_BCKP current at max enclosure temperature is still unverified (datasheet only 45 uA @ 25 C) - confirm hold-time margin at hot-corner; nominal calc gives ~tens of hours vs ~4 h ephemeris window, so margin is large but should be confirmed.
- (Supercap backup supplies (U34/U35 TPS61094 ×2 + DSF305Q3R0 3F supercaps)) Confirm the intended SOC ADC scaling in firmware matches the as-built (direct, 1:1) sense now that no /2 divider exists; max sensed voltage = VCHG = 2.5 V.
- (Supercap backup supplies (U34/U35 TPS61094 ×2 + DSF305Q3R0 3F supercaps)) Confirm whether 66 uF on VOUT was an intentional hold-up choice; if so document the deviation from TI's 20-30 uF COUT recommendation and validate loop stability.
- (Supercap backup supplies (U34/U35 TPS61094 ×2 + DSF305Q3R0 3F supercaps)) Confirm C90/C91 symbol polarity orientation (supercaps are polarized) once a real radial footprint with a defined pin-1/+ pad is assigned.
- (Supercap backup supplies (U34/U35 TPS61094 ×2 + DSF305Q3R0 3F supercaps)) Decide EN/MODE pull-up reference (VOUT vs VIN) after a cold-start sequence check; either works but VIN-referenced is less subtle.
- (Supercap backup supplies (U34/U35 TPS61094 ×2 + DSF305Q3R0 3F supercaps)) Select L4/L5 specific inductor PN (Isat, DCR, footprint) and the C92-C97 / supercap specific MPNs (all currently BOM status SELECT).
- (Ethernet magnetics/input (sheet: ethernet-input.kicad_sch)) Is the 0826-1X1T-HS-F footprint/pinout identical to the GH-F symbol used? Confirm before generating the land pattern (HS-F is the 100W/2.5G ext-temp variant).
- (Ethernet magnetics/input (sheet: ethernet-input.kicad_sch)) Is 3V3_LAN intentionally a separate ferrite-isolated (FB1) PHY analog rail, or should it merge with main 3V3? If separate, add it to sts1000_net_naming.md.
- (Ethernet magnetics/input (sheet: ethernet-input.kicad_sch)) What HV rating/standard must C1 (SHIELD-couple cap) meet — confirm surge/ESD target (e.g. 2kV) for the deployment (outdoor-adjacent Observatory Ethernet run).
- (Ethernet magnetics/input (sheet: ethernet-input.kicad_sch)) Does the chosen ESD strategy rely on this integrated magjack's internal termination for surge, or is additional cable-side surge protection (GDT) required for the building/outdoor Ethernet run? (Mirrors the GPS-SMA outdoor-ESD concern.)
- (Ethernet magnetics/input (sheet: ethernet-input.kicad_sch)) Confirm LAN8742 nINTSEL/REGOFF strap levels (shared with LED1/LED2 = J1 pins 17-20 path) are correct for the intended REF_CLK source; this is already a peripheral_map §14 open item.
- (Ethernet magnetics/input (sheet: ethernet-input.kicad_sch)) Confirm J1 LED1/LED2 pin polarity (Bel table) matches the PHY LED drive/strap resistors on the Ethernet PHY sheet (R38/R39/R40/R41).
- (Ethernet PHY (LAN8742AI-CZ-TR) — sheet ethernet-phy.kicad_sch) Y1 footprint: assign and verify CTS 445I 4-pad SMD land pattern + pin-1; confirm CL=20 pF vs fitted 27 pF load caps (C14/C16 give ~19 pF with 3 pF XTAL pin cap + ~2.5 pF stray — slightly low; fine-trim once Y1 package stray is known, 33 pF would center it).
- (Ethernet PHY (LAN8742AI-CZ-TR) — sheet ethernet-phy.kicad_sch) J1 magjack: assign footprint; verify 1000BASE-T 0826 ICM pinout (TRD1=4/5, TRD2=10/11, center taps 6/12, LEDs 18/20) and internal termination of the two UNUSED pairs; resolve HS-F vs GH-F BOM suffix.
- (Ethernet PHY (LAN8742AI-CZ-TR) — sheet ethernet-phy.kicad_sch) U1 TPD4EUSB30 placement: confirm whether PHY-side ESD is intentional or should move to the RJ45 cable side; the 0826 may already include cable-side protection.
- (Ethernet PHY (LAN8742AI-CZ-TR) — sheet ethernet-phy.kicad_sch) nRST (LAN_RST_N, pin15): R35 10k pulldown holds PHY in reset by default; confirm firmware drives PD10 to deassert >=100 us (trstia) after VDD1A/2A/VDDIO are in spec and after strap setup time (tcss 200 ns). No RC delay on nRST — relies on MCU GPIO sequencing.
- (Ethernet PHY (LAN8742AI-CZ-TR) — sheet ethernet-phy.kicad_sch) PHYAD0 (pin10) = 0 via internal pull-down + R34 100R series to PA2/PB10 high-Z at POR — confirm firmware MDIO accesses the PHY at address 0.
- (Ethernet PHY (LAN8742AI-CZ-TR) — sheet ethernet-phy.kicad_sch) Confirm 3V3_LAN supply current budget through FB1 (BLM31KN601, 600 ohm @100 MHz, rated current): VDD1A+VDD2A draw must not cause excessive DC drop across the ferrite's DCR.
- (Ethernet PHY (LAN8742AI-CZ-TR) — sheet ethernet-phy.kicad_sch) REGOFF (pin3) = low via internal PD + R40 4.75k -> regulator ENABLED; VDDCR externally decoupled only (C17 470pF + C18 1uF), no external 1.2 V supply — correct for reg-on. Confirm no accidental high at POR from the LED/J1.20 path.
- (MCU core (STM32H563VIT6, U12)) Is field-selectable boot (flash vs system bootloader) actually required? If not, BOOT0 should be a single hard pulldown; if yes, expose it on a header rather than a 1:1 divider.
- (MCU core (STM32H563VIT6, U12)) Confirm firmware disables the internal VREFBUF when VREF+ is driven by external U14 (MCP1502-33), per STM32H5 reference manual - else contention on VREF+.
- (MCU core (STM32H563VIT6, U12)) Is C37 (1 nF) at VREF+ intentional vs a placeholder for the recommended 1 uF+100 nF? Confirm intended ADC sampling rate/impedance to size VREF+ reservoir.
- (MCU core (STM32H563VIT6, U12)) Confirm intended BOOT0 resting state and whether R49 OR R50 was meant to be the only populated part (no-DNP policy makes the divider as-drawn ambiguous).
- (MCU core (STM32H563VIT6, U12)) VBAT (pin6) is fed from the TPS61094 backup output (U35) plus R109/R111 100k and bulk caps - confirm this supercap-backed VBAT topology is intended and that VBAT stays in spec (1.65-3.6 V) during main-rail loss.
- (External watchdog (U64 TPS3430, WDT sheet)) Confirm on their own sheets that the thermal-cutoff and Rb OV-latch open-collector outputs actually wire-OR onto WDO_N (doc §6 claims three sources share R23). This review only sees U64 WDO + R23 on that net.
- (External watchdog (U64 TPS3430, WDT sheet)) Confirm WDT_EN drive: PA9 is GPIO push-pull driving SET1 high to arm. With SET0 hard-tied high and only SET1 moving, DS allows immediate disable<->enable (no 500µs tSET inter-pin spacing). Verify firmware never moves both SET pins simultaneously (SET0 is fixed, so OK by construction).
- (External watchdog (U64 TPS3430, WDT sheet)) Verify in the KiCad footprint editor that VSON-10 footprint maps the exposed pad to pad number 11 (symbol exposes pin 11 = GND); a name/number mismatch would leave the EP unconnected.
- (GNSS receiver (ZED-F9T) — U21 ZED-F9T-00B, U22 LT3045 LDO, U23 INA228 @0x44) Confirm ZED-F9T-00B internal pull-up on D_SEL (pin 47) so the UART/I2C-vs-SPI interface latches deterministically at POR before PD7 is driven.
- (GNSS receiver (ZED-F9T) — U21 ZED-F9T-00B, U22 LT3045 LDO, U23 INA228 @0x44) Confirm L1 bias-T inductor value (CLAUDE.md 47nH vs u-blox-recommended ~120nH multi-band) and that R77 series current-limit protects it on antenna short (cross-sheet: gps-antenna).
- (GNSS receiver (ZED-F9T) — U21 ZED-F9T-00B, U22 LT3045 LDO, U23 INA228 @0x44) ZED-F9T V_BCKP current at max enclosure temperature (datasheet only specs 45uA @25C) to validate TPS61094 supercap hold time (existing peripheral_map open item).
- (GNSS receiver (ZED-F9T) — U21 ZED-F9T-00B, U22 LT3045 LDO, U23 INA228 @0x44) Should INA228 U23 shunt R72=500mohm be re-sized? GPS load ~70-120mA gives only ~35-60mV across 0.5R (ADCRANGE-dependent); confirm it meets target current resolution.
- (GNSS receiver (ZED-F9T) — U21 ZED-F9T-00B, U22 LT3045 LDO, U23 INA228 @0x44) Verify pin-1 marker / rotation of the custom MODULE_ZED-F9T-00B footprint against the u-blox package drawing at layout (pad count 102 matches symbol, orientation not yet visually verified).
- (GNSS antenna bias + supervisor (gps-antenna.kicad_sch)) U27: is the intended part RT9742GGJ5 (1A, std pinout matching the symbol, with FLG) or RT9742VGJ5 (2A, active-high EN, M/V pinout, no FLG)? The two are mutually exclusive with the current symbol and the nFLG net.
- (GNSS antenna bias + supervisor (gps-antenna.kicad_sch)) If RT9742 (1A G-variant) is kept, does its ~1.1A current limit + the Q11/Q12 180mA foldback double-limiting cause interaction, and does 1A cover V_ANT capacitor inrush (C59 10uF + downstream) within tON?
- (GNSS antenna bias + supervisor (gps-antenna.kicad_sch)) Why are there TWO independent current senses on the same V_ANT path (U26/R89 upstream of the switch output, and U24/R77 in the limiter)? Is the U27 load switch + INA228 a deliberate addition that supersedes the doc's single-shunt description, and should the doc be rewritten to the as-built three-element (switch + 2 shunts) scheme?
- (GNSS antenna bias + supervisor (gps-antenna.kicad_sch)) L1: confirm 47nH vs 56nH; if 47nH, is the ~465Ω choke impedance at L1 band acceptable, or is a higher-value/second choke needed to keep >500Ω across the multi-band range?
- (GNSS antenna bias + supervisor (gps-antenna.kicad_sch)) Is the GPS SMA ESD/surge protection (polymer ESD Cj<=0.3pF + separate coax GDT, V_RWM>=6.5V) placed on the connector sheet? It is not present on gps-antenna.kicad_sch.
- (GNSS antenna bias + supervisor (gps-antenna.kicad_sch)) Does U27 (RT9742) need input/output bulk caps per Richtek app circuit (CIN/COUT) on this rail, and are C59/C64-C66 serving that role with correct placement?
- (GNSS antenna bias + supervisor (gps-antenna.kicad_sch)) Confirm U25 (LMV393) footprint selection (SOIC-8 vs VSSOP-8) before layout — currently unset.
- (OCXO + steering supply (Y3 OH300, U39 TPS7A52 LDO, U38 AP3441 buck, U36 OPA320 Vc buffer, U37 INA228 #5)) AP3441SHE-7B authoritative pinout: official Diodes datasheet (DS39754) could not be fetched (403/cert). The custom CM5IO symbol and LCSC's pin table disagree on EN/PG/VIN/LX placement. Must be resolved from the official package drawing before layout, and the same symbol is reused as U29 elsewhere.
- (OCXO + steering supply (Y3 OH300, U39 TPS7A52 LDO, U38 AP3441 buck, U36 OPA320 Vc buffer, U37 INA228 #5)) R126 OCXO-rail shunt value (currently 25 mOhm, status SHUNT-REVIEW) must be set from the actual OH300 oven warmup + steady current and the chosen INA228 ADCRANGE to keep V_SHUNT in range without excess drop on a 3.3V oven supply.
- (OCXO + steering supply (Y3 OH300, U39 TPS7A52 LDO, U38 AP3441 buck, U36 OPA320 Vc buffer, U37 INA228 #5)) Confirm AP3441 PG output structure (open-drain vs push-pull) and intended EN-sequencing logic for U39, then size the pull-up + R124/R125 so OCXO_PSU_PG meets TPS7A52 EN VIH.
- (OCXO + steering supply (Y3 OH300, U39 TPS7A52 LDO, U38 AP3441 buck, U36 OPA320 Vc buffer, U37 INA228 #5)) Is the +/-0.4 ppm Vc scaling actually required? If so the loop filter needs an attenuator/gain stage; if the full OH300 APR is intended, peripheral_map §14 wording should be updated.
- (OCXO + steering supply (Y3 OH300, U39 TPS7A52 LDO, U38 AP3441 buck, U36 OPA320 Vc buffer, U37 INA228 #5)) OPA320 powered from VDDA (STM32 analog 3.3V) — confirm VDDA can absorb the buffer's quiescent + load without degrading the ADC/DAC reference noise floor; consider whether Vc buffer should sit on a dedicated quiet rail.
- (OCXO + steering supply (Y3 OH300, U39 TPS7A52 LDO, U38 AP3441 buck, U36 OPA320 Vc buffer, U37 INA228 #5)) Open the custom .kicad_mod/.kicad_sym footprints (VSSOP10_DGS_TEX, RGR20_2P05X2P05_TEX, SOT95P280X145-5N, OH300 oscillator, DFN-8-1EP) to confirm pad numbering and pin-1 orientation — not opened in this review.
- (OCXO + steering supply (Y3 OH300, U39 TPS7A52 LDO, U38 AP3441 buck, U36 OPA320 Vc buffer, U37 INA228 #5)) CM5IO symbol library (holding AP3441SHE-7B) is embedded in the schematic but not registered in sym-lib-table; add it so the symbol is editable/reproducible.
- (Clock mux (OCXO/ext-ref -> PH0)) Confirm intended U52 package: order GW (SOT363-2/TSSOP6, 0.65 mm) and fix the footprint, OR switch MPN to the SOT457 (GS) variant the current footprint fits. Doc currently says SOT363-2.
- (Clock mux (OCXO/ext-ref -> PH0)) C160 doc calls for 50 V rating; as-built is 16 V (GRM155 0402). For a fanout DC-block driving ~1.6 Vpp into 50 ohm AC-coupled this is electrically fine - confirm whether the 50 V note in the doc is a hard requirement or can be relaxed, then reconcile.
- (Clock mux (OCXO/ext-ref -> PH0)) Firmware/EE: still-open per hardware/CLAUDE.md - confirm EXTREF_MON (PB14/TIM12) 10 MHz +/- acceptance band and MUX_SEL switch hysteresis (sec 4.1, open item).
- (Clock mux (OCXO/ext-ref -> PH0)) Confirm U53 ordered as Q100 grade to match U52 (automotive-grade project rule); pick vendor (Nexperia per doc vs TI per current symbol link).
- (External 10 MHz RF front end (refclock-input.kicad_sch)) U50 LTC6752 S5 fixed internal hysteresis value: confirm adequate for a 10 MHz sine at the lowest specified level (+6 dBm) without the optional Q->+IN positive-feedback (doc §4.6/§12 item 2). Could not extract the hysteresis mV from the datasheet PDF (binary) in this session.
- (External 10 MHz RF front end (refclock-input.kicad_sch)) Confirm U50 VCC (~2.85 V) stays >2.45 V min over full temp/Iq spread with R183=33R; decide whether to trim R183 (doc open item 3).
- (External 10 MHz RF front end (refclock-input.kicad_sch)) D8 (SZESD7410MXWT5G, SMA ESD on connectors sheet) has an EMPTY footprint field in the netlist/BOM -- assign the X2-DFN footprint before layout (out of this sheet but part of the RF chain).
- (External 10 MHz RF front end (refclock-input.kicad_sch)) EN/UV (U51 pin3) is driven from 5V_PSU_PG shared across U13/U28/U29/U38 enables -- confirm the asserted logic level (and source impedance) meets LT3045 EN/UV ~1.0 V threshold and does not exceed VIN; LT3045 EN/UV can take up to VIN so likely fine, but confirm the PG driver rail.
- (External 10 MHz RF front end (refclock-input.kicad_sch)) 10MHz_CLK_OUT is a single 33R (R184) at U50 Q feeding a Y-branch to BOTH U52 (mux I1) and PB14/TIM12 -- confirm the PB14 tap is a short stub and the series-at-driver term is sized for the branched load (doc open item 4).
- (External 10 MHz RF front end (refclock-input.kicad_sch)) C152 (1 uF VCC bypass) BOM Status=SELECT, no Mfr/MPN -- commit a part.
- (Rb buck supply (VCC_RB)) MCP41U83 power-on volatile-wiper default (zero/mid/MTP) is unconfirmed (Microchip PDFs not text-extractable via available tools). This sets pre-firmware VCC_RB. Confirm and/or rely on the EN-gating interlock (RB_PWR_EN deasserted until safe code written). Note: even worst-case code is hard-bounded to 4.46-24.35V by fixed R147/R148/R134 - good - but a 15V-nominal FE-5680A could still be over-stressed at 24.35V; confirm acceptable per installed Rb variant.
- (Rb buck supply (VCC_RB)) MCP41U83 SPI VIH (typ 0.7*VDD): if VDD must be 5V (to keep P0B<VDD), 3V3 MCU drive ~3.3V vs 3.5V VIH is marginal - confirm exact VIH spec or add level shift / keep VDD=3.3V with VREF<3.3V.
- (Rb buck supply (VCC_RB)) Confirm MCP41U83 SPI mode (CPOL/CPHA), wiper-write opcode/frame, and whether CRC is enabled by default (rejects writes if not handled) - could not extract from datasheet.
- (Rb buck supply (VCC_RB)) Worst-case VOUT_P (PoE/PD bridge rail) including transients vs MIC28516 70V abs-max - confirm headroom; C133/134/136 are 100V (ok for 57V) but verify ringing.
- (Rb buck supply (VCC_RB)) Finalize R159 shunt value/rating and the corresponding INA228 ADCRANGE/calibration for full-scale at the Rb load current.
- (Rb buck supply (VCC_RB)) MCP1502 (U45) turn-on/settle time vs MIC28516 soft-start (C119=10nF): does VREF establish before the FB injection and OV reference are needed? Resolve the ref-gating startup race or make the reference always-on per the doc.
- (FE-5680A RS-232 interface (rb-io sheet)) Confirm G6K-2F-Y DC3 maximum continuous coil voltage and coil temperature rise at the worst-case enclosure ambient (coil sees 3.3V on a 3.0V-rated coil = 110%).
- (FE-5680A RS-232 interface (rb-io sheet)) Verify the Omron G6K terminal-arrangement (bottom view) pad numbering against the schematic throw mapping (coil = pins 1/8; A-COM=3, A-NC=2(DOUT), A-NO=4(R167); B-COM=6, B-NC=7(ROUT), B-NO=5(R168)) so de-energized=RS-232 is guaranteed once a footprint is assigned.
- (FE-5680A RS-232 interface (rb-io sheet)) Decide the canonical net name for the PE4 relay-mode line (RB_SER_MODE vs RB_RS232_CMOS_SW) and make peripheral_map, subsystem doc, and schematic agree.
- (FE-5680A RS-232 interface (rb-io sheet)) Pick the D16 zener MPN/footprint and confirm V_Z holds the LED node near 3.3V across the 3–24V input range (residual ~0.4mA at 24V).
- (FE-5680A RS-232 interface (rb-io sheet)) Re-spec R171 body size to meet the 0.25W intent (0402 1/10W is marginal vs 91mW worst case), or re-derate.
- (FE-5680A RS-232 interface (rb-io sheet)) Bench-verify per FE unit: serial level (RS-232 vs CMOS), J1-8/9 data direction (fix in cable if reversed), lock polarity (RB_LOCK config bit), and that APC-817C1 (not A1/B1) is fitted for the 3V input corner.
- (FE-5680A RS-232 interface (rb-io sheet)) Resolve all custom footprint libraries via a project fp-lib-table before layout (affects U46, U47, plus the rest of the board).
- (SPI peripherals (NOR flash, U62)) Confirm pull-up resistor VALUES for R205 (NOR_RST_N), R207 (WP#), R212 (nCS) — netlist confirms presence on 3V3_STM and 0402 footprint, but values were not separately verified (10k typical).
- (SPI peripherals (NOR flash, U62)) Confirm the chosen 8-SOP footprint body/pad geometry against the exact Macronix MX25L25645GM2I (M2 = 208mil SOP) package drawing before layout.
- (SPI peripherals (NOR flash, U62)) WP#/SIO2 (pin3) and RESET#/SIO3 (pin7) are not wired as data lines to the MCU, only pulled up (RESET also driven by PE10). This correctly precludes Quad-SPI; confirm SPI4 single-SPI is the intended mode and 32 MB single-SPI throughput is adequate for FW-staging/web-asset use.
- (SPI peripherals (NOR flash, U62)) Confirm 256 Mbit (32 MB) capacity vs total firmware needs (MCUboot slots + NTS/web assets + logs); doc lists multiple consumers — verify budget.
- (I2C peripherals + display power) Does the LCDwiki MSP4030 display/touch module populate its own I²C pull-ups on the FT6336 touch bus? If yes, the missing PCA9306 high-side pull-ups (U63 SCL2/SDA2) may be covered; if no, they are a hard defect. Confirm against the module schematic before layout.
- (I2C peripherals + display power) Confirm exact RT9742VGJ5 'V'-suffix current-limit tier from Richtek DS9742-10 ordering info, then verify it clears measured display backlight-full current + Cin inrush with the 0.1Ω R107 shunt in series.
- (I2C peripherals + display power) Confirm INA228 U32 address: A1=GND, A0 tied to SCL line — verify the A0/A1 pin-strap combination actually yields 0x42 per INA228 address table (A0 tied to a switching SCL net is unusual; INA228 latches address at power-up, but confirm this is a static tie, not the live SCL).
- (I2C peripherals + display power) Confirm which physical TMP117 (U57=0x49 vs U58=0x48) is the OCXO-temp sensor vs ambient, and that firmware/peripheral_map address map agrees.
- (I2C peripherals + display power) Verify TMP117 WSON exposed pad (footprint pad) is tied to GND (or intentionally floated) — symbol has no EP pin so confirm at layout.
- (I2C peripherals + display power) Confirm PCA9306 EN drive level is acceptable at 3V3 (=VREF1) or add a VREF2 pull-up; verify VIH(EN) of PCA9306DCTT.
- (I2C peripherals + display power) Update canonical doc sts1000_3v3p_i2c_peripherals.md to the as-built always-on 3V3_STM topology and propagate to peripheral_map §4/§6.
- (Fault/UI aggregation (MCP23017 ×2: U55 @0x20, U54 @0x21)) Confirm the MCP23017 ML exposed-pad land dimensions against the DS20001952 package drawing before committing the KiCad std-lib footprint (4.25x4.25mm EP vs ~4.45mm nominal).
- (Fault/UI aggregation (MCP23017 ×2: U55 @0x20, U54 @0x21)) After reassigning the three bit-7 inputs off GPA7/GPB7: U54 is currently 16/16 full, so either (a) move two U54 inputs to U55's spare GPB2-6 (leaving GPA7/GPB7 as outputs/NC on both), or (b) add a third MCP23017 / route DISP_TOUCH_INT to a spare MCU EXTI. Decide and propagate to the doc bit-map, IPOL/INTCON masks, and firmware workers.
- (Fault/UI aggregation (MCP23017 ×2: U55 @0x20, U54 @0x21)) Confirm firmware sets IOCON.ODR=1 (open-drain) on both expanders before enabling INTs, and MIRROR=1 on U55 / MIRROR=0 on U54, matching the external INTA+INTB tie on U55 (push-pull would contend on the wire-OR).
- (Fault/UI aggregation (MCP23017 ×2: U55 @0x20, U54 @0x21)) Set GPPU (internal pull-up) or output-low on U55 spare GPB2-7 to avoid floating-input current and spurious INTs.
- (Fault/UI aggregation (MCP23017 ×2: U55 @0x20, U54 @0x21)) Close the stale 'drop R44' open item in CLAUDE.md / fault_aggregation.md §10 — verified R44 is not on this net.
- (I2C1 bus + rise-time accelerator (U56 LTC4311)) Confirm target I2C1 SCL frequency (100 kHz vs 400 kHz) from software_spec, then budget total bus capacitance (all ~16 device pin C + trace C) against the LTC4311 supported load to validate that 4.7k + U56 yields compliant rise times.
- (I2C1 bus + rise-time accelerator (U56 LTC4311)) Confirm intended canonical net name: keep I2C_SCL/I2C_SDA or rename to I2C1_SCL/I2C1_SDA to match the peripheral map's I2C1 designation (sts1000_net_naming.md).
- (I2C1 bus + rise-time accelerator (U56 LTC4311)) Populate U56 BOM line 525 footprint/package/pinout-match fields (currently blank / MPN-FROM-VALUE).
- (I2C1 bus + rise-time accelerator (U56 LTC4311)) Pre-layout placement intent: site U56 at the electrically farthest/highest-capacitance node of the multi-sheet I2C bus so the accelerator sees the worst-case edge, with C170 close-coupled to U56.
- (Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch)) Confirm the exact MSP4030/LCDwiki 14-pin module pinout for J4: is pin 11 LCD_RST or CTP_RST, and is commoning touch reset with display reset (DISP_RST) intended? This affects touch bring-up sequencing (release DISP_RST then I2C-init FT6336U).
- (Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch)) What is the 5V_DISP rail regulation tolerance? Drives whether SMF5V0A (D6, VRWM 5.0 V) is acceptable or must move to SMF5.5/6.0A.
- (Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch)) Confirm D7 value commit to 1.5SMCJ28A and that its standoff coordinates with the autonomous 26 V OV latch and FE-5680A absolute-max on VCC_RB.
- (Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch)) Confirm FE-5680A DE9 (J6) Tx/Rx direction (J1-8/J1-9) for the specific surplus variant before locking the DE9 footprint/pinout.
- (Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch)) Confirm U17 physically sits at the display flex J4 (DISP_TOUCH_INT enters at J4.13) so the touch-INT ESD clamps at the cable entry, not remotely.
- (Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch)) Lifecycle: verify SZESD7410MXWT5G is not end-of-life and identify a second source.
- (Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch)) Verify STM32H563 TAMP internal pull-up value / precharge timing supports the no-external-PU + 1 nF (C44) tamper input (RM0481).
- (Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch)) Clear the now-completed standing actions: PG_IN_N->PG_INT_N rename and INT/EXP_RST pin landings (PG_INT_N=PA10 confirmed here).
- (RGB status indicator (D5)) D5 IN-P55TATRGB pinout could not be independently re-confirmed from a machine-readable datasheet (Inolux and LCSC PDFs returned as unparseable binary). The KiCad symbol is internally consistent with the canonical doc's pinout (1=KB,2=KR,3=KG,4=AG,5=AR,6=AB), but a human should eyeball the official IN-P55TATRGB datasheet pinout drawing once, since the missing footprint's pad mapping must be checked against it anyway.
