- (RGB status indicator (D5)) Confirm LED_R/G/B (PD12/PD13/PD14) are valid TIM4 PWM-channel AF mappings on the LQFP100 (doc §9 says 'verify AF pairing before layout'). Pin assignment to U12.59/60/61 is correct; the timer/AF availability is a firmware/peripheral-map item, not visible in this sheet.
- (RGB status indicator (D5)) Confirm front-panel local ambient supports the blue 24.8 mA design point, or adopt the 20 mA fallback (doc §7).
- (netlist) INA228 address map: straps decode U30=0x42/U32=0x43 (doc says 0x43/0x42) and U37=0x47/U44=0x46 (doc says 0x46/0x47). Which is authoritative — fix the straps or the doc+firmware map? (Confirm against TI INA228 Table 7-2, p.19, which could not be rendered here.)
- (netlist) PIR proximity-wake: peripheral_map §159/§287/§411 specify a PIR on U55 GPB3, but no PROX_WAKE/PIR/WAKE net exists and U55 GPB3 is unconnected. Is the proximity-wake feature dropped (update docs) or omitted in error (add to schematic)?
- (netlist) U55 Port B map drift: V_DISP_EN_FAULT is on GPB1 in the schematic but the doc places it on GPB2 (GPB1 'freed'). Which bit assignment is correct for firmware?
- (netlist) Confirm R20 value/rail on POE_PG provides a valid logic-high EN for buck U28 when NCP1095 PGO (open-drain) releases.
- (netlist) Should U54 GPB7 and U55 GPA7 symbol pintypes be changed from 'output' to input/bidirectional to clear the false multi-driver flags, and U55 GPB2 get a no-connect flag?
- (library) 74LVC1G157GW-Q100H (U52): confirm the SOT457/SC-74 pin table (I1=1, GND=2, I0=3, Y=4, VCC=5, S=6) against Nexperia DS Rev table 3 — could not machine-read the PDF.
- (library) ZED-F9T-00B (U21) and ARJ-199 magjack: pin/pad maps were only count-checked (102=102, 22 pins), not individually audited vs the u-blox/Abracon land patterns — audit before layout.
- (library) Three orphan symbols (AD5292BRUZ, AD5270BRMZ, ADCLK925BCPZ) are registered in sym-lib-table but unused in the netlist; confirm intent and remove to prevent the wrong digipot/clock-buffer being placed. ADCLK925 also uses all-unspecified pin electrical types (ERC-weak).
- (library) Stray file 2026-06-14_01-24-03.kicad_sym (LIS2MDLTR) is not in sym-lib-table — delete or register; confirm it is not the intended magnetometer (project uses IIS2MDC).
- (library) Exposed-pad paste apertures: RGR20 pad21 and SON50P300 pad13 EPs have no F.Paste layer; define the stencil window/segmentation at layout for the bucks/LDOs/backup-boost thermal pads.
- (library) PCA9306 (U63) and SN65C3221 (U46) pin tables were confirmed by standard part knowledge, not a machine-read datasheet — spot-confirm against TI DS before layout.
- (power) NCP1095 classification: RCLA=232 ohm (R13) / RCLB=909 ohm (R14) dual-resistor scheme is bt-capable, but confirm against the NCP1095 datasheet class table that this maps to at least Class 4 (Type 2, 25.5W) or Class 5/6 (Type 3) as required for OCXO+Rb concurrent ~25-30W. Could not extract the class table (onsemi PDF 403; LCSC/Farnell were image-only).
- (power) Is a high-voltage bus TVS (e.g. SMAJ58A) intended on VOUT_P->VOUT_N? None found in the netlist/BOM; only D2/D3 (5VWM) protect the signal pairs. Confirm NCP1095 app-note transient protection on the 57V PD bus is satisfied by the 100V cap bank alone or add a clamp.
- (power) AP3441 (U29 3V3 buck, U38 OCXO pre-buck) Vin abs-max is 5.5V and they run from the 5.0V rail (only 0.5V margin). Confirm the 5V rail's worst-case overshoot/ripple/load-step stays under 5.5V, or retarget the 5V rail slightly lower.
- (power) Backup SoC sense: peripheral_map §7 specifies a /2 divider on PA6/PB1, but the netlist ties the TPS61094 SUP (supercap) node directly to the ADC with no divider and no series R/filter. Supercap <=2.55V so direct sense is electrically OK, but add a series R + cap for noise and reconcile the doc.
- (power) L4/L5 (TPS61094 backup buck/boost inductors, 2.2uH) have no MPN assigned (SELECT) and D4 (NCP1095 VAUX 12V zener) is a generic part - assign real PNs and confirm Isat for the boost-mode backup current.
- (power) RB_PWR_EN (PB7) fans out to both the Rb buck EN (via Q18) and U46.16 (SN65C3221 FORCEOFF/EN). Confirm tying the FE-5680A RS-232 transceiver enable to Rb rail power is intentional.
- (power) Confirm magjack J1 (0826-1X1T-HS-F) integrated magnetics expose all four pair center taps for Mode A+B PoE into the U7/U8 dual bridge (single-port jack - verify center-tap availability).
- (interfaces) O-PoE: Magjack J1 uses TRD1/TRD2 pairs only (TRD3/TRD4 NC) with VC1-4 power taps to the FDMQ8205A bridge. Confirm 0826-1X1T-HS-F brings out all four pair center-taps as VC1-4 for 802.3bt 4-pair (Mode A+B) PoE, and that the unused-data-pair behavior is intended for a 10/100 link.
- (interfaces) O-OCXO: Vc-path capacitors on the DAC loop filter (PA4->Y3 pin1) must be C0G/NP0 or film, never X7R. This review verified topology (R123 source term, PA3 sense) but did not open the OCXO sheet to confirm dielectric of every Vc-node cap (C109/C117 flagged 'SELECT OCXO-C0G?' in BOM).
- (interfaces) O-GPS: U21 VCC_RF (pin7) is left NC. Confirm the design intentionally uses the external bias-T for active-antenna power and does not need the module's internal RF supply pin.
- (interfaces) O-GPS reset: GPS_RST_N (PD11) and GPS_SAFEBOOT_N (PD15) have no external pulls. Confirm F9T internal pull-ups hold them deasserted while the MCU pins are high-Z during MCU reset.
- (interfaces) O-NOR WP: U62 nWP (pin3) goes to R207 10k - confirm it pulls HIGH (write-enable / HW-WP disabled) as intended, not low.
- (interfaces) O-NCP1095 status (PC7/PC2/PC3): direction and logic level, and whether a digital isolator is needed if the PD front end is isolated (carried open from peripheral_map but not resolvable from this interface pass).
- (interfaces) O-Display rail: confirm FT6336U touch I2C pull-ups on the gated 5V_DISP side reference 5V_DISP (PCA9306 U63 VREF2=5V_DISP) so the level translation is correct.
- (constraints) Is the NCP1095 PD front end isolated? This single answer drives PoE_HV net clearance, the magjack isolation gap, and whether NCL/NCM/LCF (PC7/PC2/PC3) need digital isolators (peripheral_map §14).
- (constraints) What is the committed layer stackup and copper weight? Required to convert every impedance target and current-width into a real DRC rule.
- (constraints) Confirm L1 bias-T choke value (47 nH vs 56 nH) against the schematic and the >500 Ω @ 1.575 GHz isolation requirement.
- (constraints) Are the INA228/INA181 shunt values and ADCRANGE settings finalized yet, or still per-rail TBD? Kelvin pad geometry depends on the chosen shunt footprint.
- (constraints) For the GPS SMA outdoor antenna run, confirm the two-part ESD scheme (polymer suppressor Cj ≤0.3 pF + separate coaxial GDT arrestor) is in the BOM — standard clock-line ESD parts meet neither the RF nor the bias requirement.
- (constraints) Confirm the magnetometer (U61) placement region and the worst-case adjacent DC-rail current so the current-free GND-pour keep-out radius can be sized.
- (board) Which symbol does digipot U43 actually instantiate — MCP41U83 (per docs) or AD5270/AD5292 (present in custom libs)?
- (board) Has the standing KiCad action set been applied (R44 dropped, PG_IN_N renamed, INT nets on PA10/PE0/PC12/PC0)? Doc TODOs hint R44 is now a 49.9 ohm PHY term.
- (board) FE-5680A DE-9 (J6) variant pinout — unresolved; blocks connector layout.
- (board) Where is the new PGB1010603MR / IND_PGB_0603_LTF part used (untracked custom lib added on this branch)?
- (board) Is there any enclosure/mechanical specification, or is layout expected to define form factor?

## 15. Final layout-handoff checklist

**1. Must fix before layout starts**
- [ ] [PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)] POE_KILL net / R21 / Q3 / KILL_N: KILL_N net = {Q1.C(C_3), Q5.C(C_3), R22.2} only — it has NO pull-up. Canonical sts1000_poe_kill.md requires R21 100k from V_KBIAS to KILL_N so KILL_N defaults HIGH=RUN. As wired, R21.1=V_KBIAS, R21.2=Net-(Q3-C); R21 is in Q3's collector, not on KILL_N. Q3 (BC857W PNP) is also reversed vs doc: doc wants E=V_KBIAS, C=HOLD; as built E=HOLD node (C9/R25/R27), C=via R21 to V_KBIAS, B=via R22 to KILL_N. A PNP sustain switch with its emitter on the floating HOLD node and no KILL_N pull-up cannot implement the documented default-RUN / self-sustaining-kill behavior. The whole AUX kill actuator is non-functional / indeterminate at power-up.
- [ ] [PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)] D1 / missing input TVS across VOUT_P-VOUT_N: No high-voltage surge TVS clamps the rectified PD bus (VOUT_P->VOUT_N = NCP1095 VPP->VPN). Canonical doc mandates D1=SMBJ58A TVS VPP->VPN (doc lines 78,125). In the schematic D1 is a BAV70LT1G small-signal array used for GBR steering, and no SMBJ58A/SMAJ/1.5SMC part exists on VOUT_P. D2/D3 are only 6.8V SOT-363 arrays in the gate-drive net, not a bus clamp. PD input has no avalanche surge protection for IEEE 802.3bt / IEC 61000-4-5 transients; only bulk C10 10uF/100V + C8 0.1uF/100V are present.
- [ ] [PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)] U10 (and all INA228) SDA/SCL swap: Net 'I2C_SCL' (carries MCU PB8=I2C1_SCL clock, U12.95) lands on U10 pin4 = SDA; net 'I2C_SDA' (PB9, U12.96) lands on U10 pin5 = SCL. INA228 DGS pinout is pin4=SDA, pin5=SCL (TI datasheet, verified) and the embedded symbol is correct. So the bus is crossed: the I2C clock physically reaches the INA228 data pin and vice-versa. Same crossover appears on U10,U23,U26,U30,U31,U32,U37,U44 — board-wide; it surfaces on this sheet at U10 (#1, 0x40). I2C to all power monitors will not enumerate.
- [ ] [5V/3V3 main power supply (sheet 3v3-main-power.kicad_sch)] U29 AP3441 (CM5IO:AP3441SHE-7B symbol): Custom symbol pin map is scrambled vs datasheet DS39754. Datasheet pins: 1=FB,2=PG,3=VIN,4=SGND,5=EN,6=LX,7=PGND,8=NC. Symbol has 4=PGND,5=nc,6=LX,7=EN,8=SGND. Net result as wired: the real EN pin (datasheet pin5) is tied to the symbol's no-connect -> the regulator can never be enabled; real PGND (pin7) is driven by 5V_PSU_PG (EN net) -> power ground forced to 5V; real SGND (pin4) goes to PGND net; real NC (pin8) goes to SGND net. Board-killing. Same wrong symbol is used for U38 (OCXO buck) elsewhere -> propagates.
- [ ] [5V/3V3 main power supply (sheet 3v3-main-power.kicad_sch)] U30/U31/U32 INA228 (and ALL eight INA228 board-wide): I2C SDA/SCL swapped between master and every slave. STM32 PB8(pin95)->net I2C_SCL, PB9(pin96)->net I2C_SDA (correct: PB8=I2C1_SCL, PB9=I2C1_SDA on STM32H5). But every INA228 has SDA(pin4) on net I2C_SCL and SCL(pin5) on net I2C_SDA. Master clock line lands on slave data pins and vice-versa -> bus non-functional. Confirmed identical on U10/U23/U26/U37/U44 too.
- [ ] [Supercap backup supplies (U34/U35 TPS61094 ×2 + DSF305Q3R0 3F supercaps)] C90 / C91 (DSF305Q3R0): Footprint is the placeholder string "Radial", not a real KiCad footprint. The DSF305Q3R0 is a specific radial can (3.5 mm pin pitch, defined diameter/height). Cannot be laid out as-is.
- [ ] [Supercap backup supplies (U34/U35 TPS61094 ×2 + DSF305Q3R0 3F supercaps)] fp-lib-table (project): fp-lib-table is EMPTY, but U34/U35 reference footprint via library nickname "TPS61094DSSR:SON50P300X200X80-13N". The .kicad_mod exists in hardware/libraries/ as a loose file, not in a TPS61094DSSR.pretty library, so the nickname will not resolve at layout/PCB-update.
- [ ] [Ethernet magnetics/input (sheet: ethernet-input.kicad_sch)] J1: Magjack 0826-1X1T-HS-F has NO footprint assigned (Footprint field empty in symbol and netlist; fp-lib-table is empty; no in-repo land pattern). Cannot place/route this part — hard blocker for layout.
- [ ] [Ethernet magnetics/input (sheet: ethernet-input.kicad_sch)] J1: Symbol is instantiated from the `0826-1X1T-GH-F` library but Value/MPN/datasheet = `0826-1X1T-HS-F` (a different gigabit variant). Pin NAMES match the HS-F drawing, but the footprint/land pattern must be the HS-F's, not GH-F's.
- [ ] [Ethernet magnetics/input (sheet: ethernet-input.kicad_sch)] U1: TPD4EUSB30 footprint is the bare string "10-USON" with no library prefix and no fp-lib-table — unresolved, cannot place.
- [ ] [MCU core (STM32H563VIT6, U12)] U12 pin94 BOOT0 (R49/R50): BOOT0 is tied to a resistive divider: R49 10k to 3V3 + R50 10k to GND, so BOOT0 idles at ~1.65 V. That is an indeterminate logic level for the boot-mode strap (must be a hard 0 or 1). With the project no-DNP policy both resistors are populated, so the part may boot to bootloader or flash unpredictably and is noise-sensitive.
- [ ] [MCU core (STM32H563VIT6, U12)] U12 footprint assignment: The placed U12 instance has Footprint = "100-LQFP" (no library prefix) which does NOT exist in the repo; only LQFP-100_STM.kicad_mod (+ -L/-M) exist, and the symbol's own default is "LQFP-100_STM" (also unprefixed). There is no fp-lib-table anywhere in the project. The footprint will not resolve for layout.
- [ ] [GNSS receiver (ZED-F9T) — U21 ZED-F9T-00B, U22 LT3045 LDO, U23 INA228 @0x44] U22 pin 6 (PGFB) / net Net-(U22-PGFB): LT3045 PGFB (pin 6) is shorted to the LDO input: net Net-(U22-PGFB) contains U22 pin1(IN), pin2(IN), pin6(PGFB), FB3, C46, fed from 5V via FB3. PGFB is the power-good comparator feedback input (PG asserts when PGFB>0.3V, 7mV hyst). Tying it to VIN makes PG report 'good' off the 5V input regardless of whether VOUT(3.3V) is actually present, so the 3V3_GPS_LDO_PG flag to U55 GPA0 is meaningless. Datasheet requires an OUT->PGFB->GND resistor divider: V_PGtrip=0.3V*(1+Rpg2/Rpg1).
- [ ] [GNSS receiver (ZED-F9T) — U21 ZED-F9T-00B, U22 LT3045 LDO, U23 INA228 @0x44] U22 pin 4 (PG) / net 3V3_GPS_LDO_PG: LT3045 PG is an open-collector/open-drain output. Net 3V3_GPS_LDO_PG connects only U22 pin4 to U55 (MCP23017) GPA0 with NO external pull-up. The pin can pull low but never high, so power-good can never read asserted at the expander unless the MCP23017 internal pull-up (GPPU) is enabled in firmware — which is fragile and not a hardware guarantee.
- [ ] [GNSS antenna bias + supervisor (gps-antenna.kicad_sch)] U27: BOM MPN RT9742VGJ5 (M/V-variant) does not match the schematic symbol pinout. Symbol used is the standard RT9742GGJ5 (pin1=OUT,2=GND,3=nFLG,4=EN,5=IN). Per Richtek DS9742-10, the M/V variant uses the 'For RT9742M/V only' pinout (pin5=EN,4=VOUT,3=VIN,2=GND) and HAS NO FLG PIN — yet the schematic wires pin3=nFLG to V_ANT_EN_FAULT→U55.25. Pins will land on the wrong silicon functions.
- [ ] [OCXO + steering supply (Y3 OH300, U39 TPS7A52 LDO, U38 AP3441 buck, U36 OPA320 Vc buffer, U37 INA228 #5)] U37 (INA228 OCXO): Address straps wired A1=VS(3V3), A0=I2C_SCL which per TI INA228 Table 7-2 decodes to 0x47 (1000111), not the required 0x46. 0x47 is already assigned to the Rb-rail INA228 (U44) -> I2C address collision; OCXO power monitor unreachable.
- [ ] [OCXO + steering supply (Y3 OH300, U39 TPS7A52 LDO, U38 AP3441 buck, U36 OPA320 Vc buffer, U37 INA228 #5)] U38 (AP3441 buck) PG / U39 EN chain: AP3441 PG (U38.2, open-drain) sits on Net-(U38-PG) with NO pull-up to any rail. Its only path is R125(6.81k) -> OCXO_PSU_PG -> R124(10k) -> GND, which also drives U39 (TPS7A52 LDO) EN pin (U39.14). An open-drain output with no pull-up cannot present a valid logic-high, so OCXO_PSU_PG cannot reach the LDO EN threshold -> OCXO LDO never enables -> OCXO unpowered.
- [ ] [OCXO + steering supply (Y3 OH300, U39 TPS7A52 LDO, U38 AP3441 buck, U36 OPA320 Vc buffer, U37 INA228 #5)] U38 (AP3441SHE-7B): Custom CM5IO schematic symbol pinout (FB=1,PG=2,VIN=3,PGND=4,NC=5,LX=6,EN=7,SGND=8,PAD=9) cannot be reconciled with the LCSC-published pin table (EN=1,FB=2,GND=3,LX=4/5,VIN=6,PG=7,NC=8,EP=PGND). Official Diodes PDF could not be fetched to adjudicate. If the symbol is wrong, EN/PG/VIN/LX are mis-mapped -> buck non-functional / shorted at power-up.
- [ ] [Clock mux (OCXO/ext-ref -> PH0)] U52: Footprint mismatch. MPN 74LVC1G157GW-Q100H is the GW suffix = SOT363-2 / TSSOP6 (body width 1.25 mm, 0.65 mm lead pitch, per Nexperia DS 74LVC1G157_Q100 Rev.6 2025-09-09, ordering/package section). Assigned footprint SC-74_TSOP6_SOT457_NEX is SOT457 / SC-74 / TSOP6 (0.95 mm pitch, pads at x=+/-1.35255, y=-0.95/0/+0.95 in the .kicad_mod). That is the GS-suffix package, not GW. Footprint will not solder to the ordered part.
- [ ] [Clock mux (OCXO/ext-ref -> PH0)] U53: No footprint assigned. Symbol Footprint property is empty (clock-mux.kicad_sch), BOM footprint column blank (sts1000_bom.csv line 522), and netlist comp has no footprint. Cannot be placed/routed.
- [ ] [External 10 MHz RF front end (refclock-input.kicad_sch)] U51 PGFB (pin 6): PGFB is tied to VIN (net Net-(U51-PGFB) = U51.1/IN, U51.2/IN, U51.6/PGFB, FB9.1, C154.1) instead of to a resistor divider OUT(3V0_RF)->PGFB->GND. LT3045 PG asserts when PGFB>300 mV (datasheet: PG=0.3V*(1+RPG2/RPG1)); with PGFB at ~5 V it is permanently above threshold, so PG (pin4) always reads GOOD regardless of whether the 3.0 V island is actually in regulation. PG is wired to MCP23017 U55 GPA2 (net 3V0_RF_LDO_PG) and consumed as a fault/status input, so firmware will see a false always-good. Power-good monitoring of the RF island is non-functional.
- [ ] [External 10 MHz RF front end (refclock-input.kicad_sch)] D20, D21 (3V3 zeners): Both island/VCC clamp diodes are generic Device:D_Zener valued '3V3' with NO footprint assigned and NO MPN (BOM Status=SELECT, Footprint/Mfr/MPN all blank). Cannot be placed in layout (no footprint) and cannot be ordered. D20 = doc's D13 island shunt clamp (doc wants TVS >=1 W); D21 = doc's D14 VCC abs-max guard (doc wants >=0.5 W).
- [ ] [External 10 MHz RF front end (refclock-input.kicad_sch)] REF_VMID node (Net-(U50--)): Missing 0.1 uF bypass on REF_VMID. The -IN/VMID node = R179(10k->3V0_RF), R180(10k->GND), R182(100k), U50.4(-IN) only -- no capacitor. Doc §4.6/§9 require '0.1 uF bypass' on REF_VMID and §5.4 settling math assumes 5k*0.1uF=0.5 ms. Without it the comparator threshold reference is unbypassed (noisy threshold -> jitter, false edges) and the documented settling budget is invalid.
- [ ] [External 10 MHz RF front end (refclock-input.kicad_sch)] U49 VDD (pin 5): Missing local 0.1 uF decoupling on the TMUX1101 VDD. U49.5 is on 3V0_RF, whose only nearby cap is C156 (10 uF Cout at the LDO). Doc §4.4 and BOM line ('— 0.1 uF U49 VDD decoupling') require a dedicated 0.1 uF at U49 VDD. Absent in schematic and BOM.
- [ ] [Rb buck supply (VCC_RB)] U44 (INA228) pins 4/5: I2C bus SWAPPED: pin4 SDA -> net I2C_SCL, pin5 SCL -> net I2C_SDA. INA228 will not communicate.
- [ ] [Rb buck supply (VCC_RB)] U44 (INA228) pins 1/2 address straps: A1->VS(3V3), A0->I2C_SDA yields 0x46, which COLLIDES with the OCXO INA228 (#5 = 0x46). Peripheral map requires Rb INA228 = 0x47.
- [ ] [Rb buck supply (VCC_RB)] C126/C127/C128 (COUT 47uF 16V X6S): Output bulk caps on VCC_RB rated only 16V, but VCC_RB DC max = 24.35V and TVS clamp ~45V. Caps will fail short. Canonical doc itself specifies >=63V.
- [ ] [Rb buck supply (VCC_RB)] U43 (MCP41U83) VDD vs P0B: VDD pin1 = 3V3 but terminal P0B pin8 = VREF_4V096 (4.096V). Pot terminal exceeds VDD by ~0.8V -> internal switch/ESD diode conducts, clamps/corrupts VREF and can damage the part. (When buck enabled, VREF is live.)
- [ ] [Rb buck supply (VCC_RB)] L7: No footprint assigned (fp=NONE) -> cannot lay out. Also value/MPN conflict: schematic+doc say 40uH; BOM MPN SRP1265A-6R8M is 6.8uH/11.5A. Inductance drives ripple/stability/Isat.
- [ ] [Rb buck supply (VCC_RB)] U41 (LMV393): No footprint assigned (fp=NONE) and BOM MPN unresolved (status MPN-FROM-VALUE, generic 'LMV393'). Blocks layout.
- [ ] [Rb buck supply (VCC_RB)] C182: VREF_4V096 reference output cap C182 (1uF 0402) is in the schematic/netlist but has NO BOM line -> BOM incomplete; part won't be ordered.
- [ ] [FE-5680A RS-232 interface (rb-io sheet)] (project) fp-lib-table: No fp-lib-table exists in the project. Custom-library footprint references in this block (U46 'SN65C3221EPWR:SOP65P640X120-16N', U47 'SOT23_NXP') cannot resolve in the PCB editor. The SOP65P640X120-16N.kicad_mod exists only as a loose file in hardware/libraries with no library nickname registered.
- [ ] [FE-5680A RS-232 interface (rb-io sheet)] K1: G6K-2F-Y DC3 relay has NO footprint assigned in either the schematic or the BOM. Cannot place/route the mode-select relay.
- [ ] [FE-5680A RS-232 interface (rb-io sheet)] L8, L9: 600Ω@100MHz line ferrites have NO footprint assigned (BOM/sym empty). MPN Fair-Rite 2508056017Y2 is an 0805 body.
- [ ] [FE-5680A RS-232 interface (rb-io sheet)] D16: Lock-input 3V3 zener has NO footprint and NO MPN (BOM status SELECT, value just '3V3').
- [ ] [FE-5680A RS-232 interface (rb-io sheet)] U48: APC-817C1 footprint field is the placeholder string '4-SMD', not a valid library:footprint, so it will not resolve for layout.
- [ ] [SPI peripherals (NOR flash, U62)] U62 (MX25L25645GM2I-08G): VCC pin in the custom symbol ntp-server-stm32:MX25L25645GM2I-08G has NO pin number (pin ""). Netlist shows VCC on 3V3_STM via pin "", so it will not map to footprint pad 8 — VCC pad floats in PCB with no ERC/DRC catch. Board would be unpowered.
- [ ] [SPI peripherals (NOR flash, U62)] U62 (MX25L25645GM2I-08G): No footprint assigned (Footprint field empty in schematic, netlist, and BOM). Cannot be placed/routed.
- [ ] [I2C peripherals + display power] U33 pin3 (nFLG) / R105: RT9742 FLG is an open-drain active-low fault output but R105 (10k) is wired as a pull-DOWN to GND (R105.1→GND, R105.2→V_DISP_EN_FAULT). An OD output with a pull-down sits permanently LOW; U55 GPB1 cannot distinguish fault from no-fault, and the open-drain transistor fights the pull-down with no defined high level.
- [ ] [I2C peripherals + display power] U63 (PCA9306) SCL2/SDA2 — nets I2C_DISP_SCL / I2C_DISP_SDA: No pull-up resistors on the 5V_DISP (VREF2/high-voltage) side of the PCA9306. The PCA9306 only provides a weak gate-bias device; per TI/NXP datasheet each side of the translator MUST have its own bus pull-ups. The low side has R202/R203 (4.7k to 3V3_STM), but the display side has none in the schematic.
- [ ] [Fault/UI aggregation (MCP23017 ×2: U55 @0x20, U54 @0x21)] U54 GPA7 (pin 24) = DISP_TOUCH_INT: Input signal mapped to MCP23017 GPA7, which Microchip (DS20001952 Rev D, June 2022, and the article cited in this part's own symbol Description) states must NOT be used as an input on the I2C MCP23017: an input transition coincident with an I2C read can corrupt SDA and hang the bus. This is the shared housekeeping I2C bus (~21 nodes incl. all 8 INA228, TMP117, ATECC608B), so a hang takes down all power/thermal monitoring.
- [ ] [Fault/UI aggregation (MCP23017 ×2: U55 @0x20, U54 @0x21)] U54 GPB7 (pin 4) = INA_ALERT_VCC_RB: Input on GPB7 (output-only restricted pin) — same SDA-corruption/bus-hang hazard. This carries the Rb-rail INA228 #6 ALERT.
- [ ] [Fault/UI aggregation (MCP23017 ×2: U55 @0x20, U54 @0x21)] U55 GPA7 (pin 24) = POE_PG: Input on GPA7 (output-only restricted pin) — same hazard. Carries PoE power-good.
- [ ] [Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch)] D7: TVS on VCC_RB is an uncommitted placeholder value '1.5SMCxxA'. VCC_RB spans 5-24 V with an autonomous 26 V OV latch; an unselected standoff voltage is a hard pre-layout/BOM gap and a safety-coordination item.
- [ ] [Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch)] D8, D9: SZESD7410MXWT5G (10 MHz ref IN/OUT ESD) have NO footprint assigned in the schematic/netlist.
- [ ] [Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch)] J2,J4,J6,J7,J8,J9,J10,J11: Eight connectors have empty Footprint fields (fan, display flex, FE-5680A DE9, GPS SMA, 2x 10 MHz SMA, tamper, 7-button header). Cannot lay out without footprints.
- [ ] [Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch)] TP1: Test point on ETH_PPS_OUT has footprint DQA0010A (a 10-pad USON ESD land) — a gross footprint mismatch that would place 10 pads for a single test node.
- [ ] [Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch)] J4 pin 11: J4.11 is tied to DISP_RST (LCD controller reset), but on the MSP4030/LCDwiki 14-pin module pin 11 is CTP_RST (capacitive-touch-panel reset), not LCD_RST (pin 4). As drawn the touch-panel reset and display reset are commoned, OR the touch reset is misrouted.
- [ ] [RGB status indicator (D5)] D5: Assigned footprint 'Library:LED_IN-P55TATRGB' does not exist: there is no fp-lib-table in the project at all, and no matching .kicad_mod in hardware/libraries. The symbol's default footprint is the KiCad-standard 'LED_SMD:LED_Inolux_IN-P55TATRGB_PLCC6_5.0x5.5mm_P1.8mm', but the D5 instance overrides it to a non-resolvable library. Layout cannot place D5 and the symbol-pin to footprint-pad mapping (load-bearing for correct R/G/B color routing) cannot be verified.
- [ ] [netlist] INA228 group (U10,U23,U26,U30,U31,U32,U37,U44) pins 4 & 5: Board-wide SDA/SCL pin swap: every INA228 wires pin 4 (SDA per TI datasheet) to net I2C_SCL and pin 5 (SCL) to net I2C_SDA. Symbol pinfunctions are correct and the MCU/MCP23017/TMP117/ATECC are all wired correctly, so the INA228 wiring is the defect. All 8 power monitors would be non-functional (clock on the data pin), breaking the entire monitoring and fault-aggregation subsystem.
- [ ] [netlist] INA_ALERT_3V3, _3V3_GPS, _3V3_STM, _5V_DISP, _OCXO, _VCC_RB, _V_ANT, _V_POE: All 8 INA228 ALERT pins (pin 3, open-drain per datasheet) drive MCP23017 U54 Port B with no external pull-up. Without a pull-up (or firmware enabling MCP23017 GPPU), the de-asserted ALERT line floats and cannot be read.
- [ ] [library] U43 MCP41U83 symbol (hardware/libraries/ntp-server-stm32.kicad_sym, symbol "MCP41U83", pins 1-7): Symbol pin-number-to-function map disagrees with Microchip DS20007000 TSSOP-14 pinout for pins 1-7. Symbol: 1=VDD,2=SDO/A1,3=SCK/SCL,4=SDI/SDA,5=nCS/A0,6=SPI2C,7=DGND. Datasheet order: 1=CS/A0,2=SDI/SDA,3=DGND,4=SPI2C,5=VDD,6=SDO/A1,7=SCK/SCL. Wrong pad mapping mis-wires VDD/VSS/SPI/wiper-config on the part that sets VCC_RB; risks driving the Rb out of its safe rail.
- [ ] [library] U62 MX25L25645GM2I-08G symbol (hardware/libraries/ntp-server-stm32.kicad_sym): VCC pin is defined with an empty pin number (number ""). A pin with no number will not map to any footprint pad; U62 also has no footprint assigned in sts1000_bom.csv.
- [ ] [library] U59 LIS2DH12 (LGA-12_STM) and U61 IIS2MDC (LGA-12_2X2X0P7_STM) footprints: Pad numbering is internally self-consistent (1-4 left, 5-6 bottom, 7-10 right, 11-12 top) and matches the symbols, but pin-1 corner orientation and exact pad x/y vs the ST recommended land pattern were not confirmed against the datasheet package figure (datasheet PDFs could not be machine-read in this environment). The pin-1 silk marker location appears inconsistent with pad-1 placement in LGA-12_STM.
- [ ] [power] L7 (Rb buck inductor, Rb Power sheet / sts1000_bom.csv): Value column says 40uH but assigned MPN is SRP1265A-6R8M which is a 6.8uH part (identical MPN to L2). MIC28516 adaptive-on-time Rb buck stepping VOUT_P (37-57V) down to ~15V at 6-10W needs a deliberately chosen inductor; 6.8uH vs 40uH changes ripple/saturation/CCM by ~6x.
- [ ] [power] R106 + 3V3_STM net: 3V3_STM (the 'always-on housekeeping' rail powering STM32 VDD x5 and all I2C peripherals) is connected to 3V3 ONLY through R106 = 0.5 ohm sense shunt (INA228 U31 0x41 across it). It is NOT a separately-regulated rail, so it cannot be 'always-on independent of the main 3V3'; both collapse together. A 0.5 ohm shunt on the full STM rail also drops ~250mV at 0.5A into the STM32 VDD and burns ~125mW.
- [ ] [power] D7 (VCC_RB TVS, Connectors/Rb): TVS on the Rb rail is a placeholder MPN '1.5SMCxxA' with no chosen clamp/standoff voltage. The Rb buck has an autonomous 26V OV latch and VCC_RB can be set 5-24V; the TVS standoff must sit above max VCC_RB but below the 26V trip and the FE-5680A abs-max.
- [ ] [interfaces] B1: I2C1 / LTC4311 U56 EN + PA9: U56 ENABLE (pin 3) is hard-tied to 3V3_STM (always enabled). PA9 — which the peripheral map §4/§8 designates as I2C_BUF_EN to drive the accelerator EN for firmware bus-recovery — is instead wired to WDT_EN (U64.SET1). Net 'WDT_EN' = U12.68(PA9), U64.6, R213. Result: the documented firmware I2C stuck-bus recovery via the accelerator is not implementable, and docs disagree with the schematic.
- [ ] [interfaces] B2: RMII / LAN8742 U11 config straps: U11 MODE0 (pin8), MODE1 (pin7), MODE2 (pin11=CRS_DV), PHYAD0/RXER (pin10) have NO pull resistor at the PHY pin — they connect only through R31-34 (100 ohm) to the MCU RMII pins, which are high-Z at power-on reset. The PHY's RMII-vs-MII mode, 10/100 advertisement, and PHY address are therefore undefined at reset. nINTSEL (pin2) / REGOFF (pin3) strap via LED resistors R39/R38 must also be confirmed to latch nINTSEL low for REF_CLK-OUT mode.
- [ ] [interfaces] B3: Missing footprints on connectors and NOR: J1 (magjack 0826-1X1T-HS-F), J5 USB-C has a footprint but J7/J8/J9 (SMA coax, generic 'Conn_Coaxial'), J6 (FE-5680A housekeeping) and U62 (MX25L25645G NOR) have no assigned footprint. Layout cannot proceed without them.
- [ ] [interfaces] B5: GPS SMA surge protection: GPS_RF_IN (J7) has a polymer ESD suppressor (L10 = PGB1010603MR, Cj~0.3pF) and bias-T (L1 47nH), but no on-board coaxial gas-discharge arrestor. The peripheral map / CLAUDE.md require a polymer ESD + separate coaxial GDT for outdoor antenna runs (RF needs Cj<=0.3pF AND 5V bias needs V_RWM>=6.5V).
- [ ] [interfaces] B6: Net-name / doc drift (non-blocking but fix before layout-freeze): PB14 net is 'CLK_OUT'-style misnamed '10MHz_CLK_OUT' though it is the EXTREF_MON capture of mux input B; PH0 net is named 'CLK_OUT' for an oscillator input; PE4 net 'RB_RS232_CMOS_SW' vs doc 'RB_SER_MODE'. Connectivity is correct in all three; only names drift from the canonical peripheral-map names, which hardware/CLAUDE.md treats as a defect.
- [ ] [constraints] PoE_HV / PoE_ISO net classes: HV clearance/creepage and magjack isolation gap cannot be finalized without knowing the PD-side voltage class and whether the NCP1095 PD front end is isolated (digital isolator on NCL/NCM/LCF). peripheral_map §14 leaves this open.
- [ ] [constraints] All impedance + current-width rules: Stackup and copper weight are TBD, so every Z target (50 Ω RF, 90 Ω USB, 100 Ω MDI) and every current-driven width (PoE_HV, buck SW/rails) is a placeholder.
- [ ] [constraints] L1 bias-T choke value: antenna_supervisor §3 body uses 56 nH (gives the cited 554 Ω @ 1.575 GHz); checklist §7 and hardware/CLAUDE.md say 47 nH. The two values give different RF isolation.
- [ ] [constraints] INA228 / INA181 shunt values: All sense-shunt values are still SHUNT-REVIEW (TBD) in sts1000_bom.md — Kelvin routing constraints are defined but the resistor footprints/power ratings are not finalized.
- [ ] [constraints] INA_ALERT_N dangling net: net_naming.md flags INA_ALERT_N as a 1-pin dangling net on the MCU — a missing connection, not just a naming issue.
- [ ] [constraints] OCXO source-term designator (R98 vs R123): clock_mux.md references R98 (and R123) for the OCXO 22 Ω source term; checklist/hardware CLAUDE say R123. Unresolved refdes.

**2–3. Must define before placement / routing**
- [ ] [PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)] C6,C7,C9,C11 (PoE HV caps): BOM marks C6 (1nF), C7 (1uF), C9 (1uF), C11 (47pF) as '100V?' with status REVIEW-HV and no MPN. C7/C9 are 0603 X7R 1uF rated only '100V?'; these sit on V_KBIAS/HOLD (VOUT_N+12V) so 100V is likely fine, but C6 is on COSC (NCP1095 osc, low V) yet marked 100V?. Voltage ratings and dielectrics are unconfirmed and parts unsourced.
- [ ] [PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)] C8 reference (VPP decouple): Doc specifies C8 100nF VPP->VPN. Netlist has C8.1=VOUT_P, C8.2=GND(=RTN). RTN!=VPN in the pass-switch-off state (RTN rises to VPP). For the NCP1095 VPP local decouple the RTN(GND) reference is acceptable, but it differs from the documented VPP->VPN. Minor, but confirm intended reference for the input decoupling vs surge return.
- [ ] [PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)] R16 / R30 shunts (25m, 150m): R16 (RSNS 25m, NCP1095 PSNS overcurrent sense) and R30 (150m, INA228 #1 V_POE shunt) are BOM status SHUNT-REVIEW with no MPN and '0.5% per rail TBD'. R16 footprint listed 1206 in BOM but doc/RSNS practice expects a tight-tolerance sense part; R16 value sets NCP1095 ILIM (VOC 1.2V/IOC 6.4A). 25m -> hard-limit ~48A, soft ~6.4A: confirm R16 actually targets the intended current limit for ~30W cold-start.
- [ ] [PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)] GBR / FDMQ8205A body-diode reversion (doc open item 1): NCP1095 GBR(11) drives only D1(BAV70 common-cathode), whose anodes steer the U3-U6 N-FET gate-drive bias (via D2/D3). During AUX kill, GBR low must force the FDMQ8205A array (U7/U8) to body-diode rectification so VOUT_P (and V_KBIAS) survives. This is an unverified dynamic behavior of a custom discrete ideal-diode gate-drive; if GBR-low instead collapses the active gates incorrectly it could oscillate offline<->reset. FDMQ8205A is a passive quad-MOSFET array (2x P-ch + 2x N-ch), so correct external gate commutation is essential and must be bench-validated.
- [ ] [PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)] D4 Zener (12V) unsourced: D4 sets V_KBIAS = VOUT_N+12V (bias rail for the kill driver). BOM status SELECT, no MPN, no footprint, value just '12V'. Power dissipation ~ (VOUT_P-12V)/R18 * 12V; at 57V port, ~1.8mA*12V=22mW - OK in SOD-123 but part must be chosen.
- [ ] [PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)] R18 power rating: R18 24.9k drops ~38V at ~1.8mA -> ~81mW at 57V port (doc). BOM assigns R18 = ERJ-2RKF2492X, an 0402 rated 1/10W (100mW). Headroom is only ~1.2x at max port voltage and worse under surge; doc explicitly flags 'R18 rated >=1/4W' as an open item.
- [ ] [PoE front end + power tree input (sheet PoE.kicad_sch)] Q2 FDMC8622 pass FET — Net-(Q2-S) multi-pad: PSNS(U9.9) and R16 top tie to Q2 pins 1,2,3 (S_1,2,3) and PGATE(U9.10) to Q2 pin4(G); Q2 pins5,6,7,8 (D) to GND/RTN. This matches an 8-PowerWDFN where source is pins1-3 and drain is the pad/pins5-8. Confirm the FDMC8622 footprint pin-1/source mapping matches the symbol (custom/generic '8-PowerWDFN'); a source/drain swap here is catastrophic (pass FET in backwards).
- [ ] [5V/3V3 main power supply (sheet 3v3-main-power.kicad_sch)] U29 PG / net 3V3_PSU_PG (R94 2.2k, R92 10k): 3V3 buck Power-Good is unreadable: U29 PG (open-drain, pin2) -> R94 (2.2k) -> 3V3_PSU_PG node -> R92 (10k) -> GND, with MCP23017 U55 GPA4 sensing the node. There is NO pull-up to any rail. The node can only ever sit near GND, so PG always reads 'fail/low'. Contrast U28 5V_PSU_PG which has R95 properly pulled to 5V.
- [ ] [5V/3V3 main power supply (sheet 3v3-main-power.kicad_sch)] R96 (24.9k) + C67 (0.1uF) from U28 SW node to FB (Net-(U28A-FB)): A series R96-C67 couples the U28 switch node (Net-(C68-Pad2)) directly into the FB pin. If intended as Hyper-Speed-Control ripple injection it may be legitimate, but the values/topology are unverified and as drawn this injects large switching ripple into the high-impedance FB node. Net-(C67-Pad1) is an internal 2-node net (R96<->C67) only.
- [ ] [5V/3V3 main power supply (sheet 3v3-main-power.kicad_sch)] L2 (SRP1265A-6R8M) / L3 (DR73-2R2-R): Both inductors have NO footprint assigned in the netlist/schematic (empty footprint field) even though MPNs and current ratings exist in the BOM (L2 6.8uH 11.5A, L3 2.2uH 4.15A). Cannot lay out without footprints. Also verify saturation/Irms margin vs the per-rail current estimates below.
- [ ] [Supercap backup supplies (U34/U35 TPS61094 ×2 + DSF305Q3R0 3F supercaps)] PA6 (BKP_GPS_SOC_V) / PB1 (BKP_STM_SOC_V): peripheral_map §lines 265-266 specify a /2 divider on each SOC sense; the schematic connects PA6/PB1 directly to the SUP node with no divider. If firmware applies the documented /2 scale it will report 2x the true supercap voltage.
- [ ] [Supercap backup supplies (U34/U35 TPS61094 ×2 + DSF305Q3R0 3F supercaps)] U34/U35 VOUT (C92/C94/C96 and C93/C95/C97): 3x22uF = 66uF nominal on each VOUT vs TI recommended COUT 20-30uF effective (NOM 20, MAX 30). Even after X7R DC-bias derate (~45-50uF eff) this exceeds the recommended max; over-capacitance can lengthen boost soft-start and reduce loop margin.
- [ ] [Supercap backup supplies (U34/U35 TPS61094 ×2 + DSF305Q3R0 3F supercaps)] L4 / L5: Inductor value 2.2uH is correct per datasheet but the BOM line has no MPN, no footprint, no saturation/DCR selection (status SELECT).
- [ ] [Supercap backup supplies (U34/U35 TPS61094 ×2 + DSF305Q3R0 3F supercaps)] U34/U35 EN, MODE: EN and MODE are pulled high to VOUT (100k) rather than to VIN. At cold start VOUT=0 -> EN=MODE=low -> Forced bypass (VOUT=VIN via bypass FET) -> VOUT rises -> EN/MODE pull up -> Auto buck/boost. Self-bootstrapping works, but pulling enable from the rail the part is generating is non-obvious and depends on the bypass-mode cold-start path; also 100k vs the internal 800k pulldown gives only ~0.89xVOUT at the pin.
- [ ] [Ethernet magnetics/input (sheet: ethernet-input.kicad_sch)] C1: SHIELD-to-digital-GND chassis-coupling cap is rated only 16V (4.7nF X7R 0402). This node bridges chassis/cable-shield to board ground and will see ESD/surge/common-mode HV in field use; 16V is grossly under-rated.
- [ ] [Ethernet magnetics/input (sheet: ethernet-input.kicad_sch)] U1: TPD4EUSB30 is a USB-3.0-targeted ESD array (not Ethernet/MDI-qualified, not AEC-Q101). Project policy requires AEC-Q100/Q101 where available. Working voltage 5.5V and 0.7pF are electrically adequate for 3.3V-biased 100M MDI, but the part class is mismatched to an industrial PoE product.
- [ ] [Ethernet magnetics/input (sheet: ethernet-input.kicad_sch)] ETH_LEDY / ETH_LEDG: Magjack LED anode/cathode orientation (Bel table: PIN17=−,PIN18=+ yellow; PIN19/20 green/orange bi-color) must agree with LAN8742 LED-pin strap polarity (the same pins set REGOFF/nINTSEL straps). A polarity/strap conflict can either invert the LEDs or mis-strap REGOFF/nINTSEL at POR.
- [ ] [Ethernet PHY (LAN8742AI-CZ-TR) — sheet ethernet-phy.kicad_sch] Y1: 25 MHz crystal has NO footprint assigned in the schematic (Footprint field empty) — layout cannot place it. BOM specifies CTS 445I23E25M00000 (25.000 MHz, CL=20 pF SMD), so a footprint (CTS 445I 3.2x2.5 mm 4-pad SMD) must be assigned and reconciled with the BOM line.
- [ ] [Ethernet PHY (LAN8742AI-CZ-TR) — sheet ethernet-phy.kicad_sch] J1: Magjack (Bel Fuse 0826-1X1T-HS-F integrated-magnetics RJ45) has NO footprint assigned in the schematic — layout blocker. Also BOM 'Spec' column lists 0826-1X1T-GH-F while MPN is 0826-1X1T-HS-F (suffix mismatch).
- [ ] [Ethernet PHY (LAN8742AI-CZ-TR) — sheet ethernet-phy.kicad_sch] U1: TPD4EUSB30 ESD array sits on the PHY-side MDI (U11 pins 20-23, between PHY and magjack J1), i.e. on the transformer-isolated side. ESD/surge from the RJ45 cable enters on the CABLE side; protection placed PHY-side of the magnetics provides little real surge/ESD benefit. Pinout itself is correct (D1+=1,D1-=2,GND=3/8,D2+=4,D2-=5; NC 6,7,9,10 tied to lines harmlessly).
- [ ] [Ethernet PHY (LAN8742AI-CZ-TR) — sheet ethernet-phy.kicad_sch] J1: A GIGABIT (1000BASE-T, 4-pair) integrated-magnetics jack is used with a 10/100 (2-pair) PHY. Only TRD1/TRD2 are driven; pairs 3 & 4 (and their center taps) are unused and must be properly terminated (Bob-Smith/75R + 1nF to chassis) to avoid radiated emissions / floating windings.
- [ ] [MCU core (STM32H563VIT6, U12)] U12 pin14 NRST: NRST connects only to the SWD header J3.5. No external reset capacitor (ST AN5711 recommends ~100 nF NRST->GND for noise/reset-glitch immunity) and no external pull-up (relies on internal ~40k). For a grandmaster that must not glitch-reset, the missing NRST cap is a reliability gap.
- [ ] [MCU core (STM32H563VIT6, U12)] U12 pin21 VREF+ / U14 MCP1502T-33 / R48 / C37 / C38: VREF+ decoupling at the MCU pin is only C37 1nF; the 2.2 uF reservoir C38 sits on the far side of series R48 50 ohm (on the MCP1502 OUT). ST recommends 1 uF + 100 nF directly at VREF+. The MCP1502 has a small max direct CL, so the 50 ohm + 2.2 uF is the reference-stability network - but it isolates the bulk charge from the pin. During ADC SAR sampling VREF+ will droop/settle through 50 ohm into 1 nF, degrading ADC accuracy (this MCU steers the OCXO via ADC-sensed Vc, so VREF integrity is timing-critical).
- [ ] [External watchdog (U64 TPS3430, WDT sheet)] WDT_KICK / U64 pin 7 (WDI): No external pull resistor on the WDI net. TI SBVS366 pin-function (p.5): 'If the watchdog is disabled, then WDI cannot be left unconnected and must be driven to either VDD or GND.' WDI has no internal pull. PB2 is push-pull so WDI is driven once GPIO is configured, but during the pre-config boot instant PB2 is Hi-Z and WDI floats. The doc's claimed pulldown R169 is actually a 10k resistor in the Rb-IO circuit (pin2 on Net-(Q21-B)), not on WDT_KICK.
- [ ] [GNSS receiver (ZED-F9T) — U21 ZED-F9T-00B, U22 LT3045 LDO, U23 INA228 @0x44] U23 pin 1 (A1): INA228 address pin A1 is strapped to bare net '3V3', but the device VS/VBUS (pins 6,8) are on '3V3_GPS'. A0 (pin2)=GND. A1=VS/A0=GND decodes to 0x44 (correct per doc), but the strap references a DIFFERENT rail than the part's own supply. If 3V3 and 3V3_GPS sequence differently, the address pin level is momentarily ambiguous relative to VS.
- [ ] [GNSS receiver (ZED-F9T) — U21 ZED-F9T-00B, U22 LT3045 LDO, U23 INA228 @0x44] U21 pin 47 (D_SEL) / GPS_DSEL = PD7: D_SEL (interface select: high/open=UART+I2C, low=SPI) is driven only by STM32 PD7. At POR the MCU GPIO is high-Z until firmware configures it; the module latches D_SEL at boot. F9 series has an internal pull-up on D_SEL (defaults to UART/I2C) so this is likely safe, but there is no board-level guarantee of the POR level.
- [ ] [GNSS receiver (ZED-F9T) — U21 ZED-F9T-00B, U22 LT3045 LDO, U23 INA228 @0x44] L1 bias-T inductor (gps-antenna sheet, feeds GPS_RF_IN): Cross-sheet: the antenna bias is injected onto GPS_RF_IN via L1. CLAUDE.md lists L1=47nH, but the ZED-F9T integration manual recommends a multi-band bias-T inductor of ~120nH (Murata) for L1/L2/L5 coverage; 47nH may not present adequate RF isolation across all bands and can load the L5/L2 RF.
- [ ] [GNSS antenna bias + supervisor (gps-antenna.kicad_sch)] L1: Schematic/BOM value is 47nH (LQG15HS47NJ02D) but the canonical doc §3/§8/§11 state 56nH. At 47nH the bias-T choke impedance at 1.575GHz is ~465Ω, which is BELOW u-blox's >500Ω guideline the doc relies on (56nH gives 554Ω).
- [ ] [GNSS antenna bias + supervisor (gps-antenna.kicad_sch)] U26.3 (INA_ALERT_V_ANT): INA228 ALERT is open-drain and has no discrete pull-up; net only connects U26.3 to MCP23017 U54.2. Valid high relies on MCP23017 internal ~100k weak pull-up (firmware-enabled, GPPU).
- [ ] [GNSS antenna bias + supervisor (gps-antenna.kicad_sch)] U27 EN / ANT_BIAS_EN / R88: R88 10k pulls U27 EN low; RT9742 V-variant EN is active-high, so V_ANT defaults OFF at power-up. This contradicts doc §7's stated intent that the antenna default ON (via Q14/R78) for fast warm restart when the F9T pin is undriven — the upstream U27 now overrides that.
- [ ] [GNSS antenna bias + supervisor (gps-antenna.kicad_sch)] R89: BOM value field reads '100m' (0.1Ω) but the assigned MPN KDV08DR150ET is 0.15Ω. The INA228 shunt-cal and overflow range depend on the true value.
- [ ] [OCXO + steering supply (Y3 OH300, U39 TPS7A52 LDO, U38 AP3441 buck, U36 OPA320 Vc buffer, U37 INA228 #5)] C98, C99, C101: All three Vc-path / loop-filter capacitors are GRM155R71C104KA88J = X7R dielectric. The Vc node is FM-sensitive; X7R microphonics/piezoelectric effect modulate the carrier. Direct violation of project hard rule 'OCXO Vc-path caps: C0G/NP0 or film, NEVER X7R'. C101 (0.1uF directly on OCXO Vcontrol) is the worst offender.
- [ ] [OCXO + steering supply (Y3 OH300, U39 TPS7A52 LDO, U38 AP3441 buck, U36 OPA320 Vc buffer, U37 INA228 #5)] Loop filter (R120/R121/R118/R119/C98/C99 + U36): OPA320 is a unity-gain buffer, so Vc = +IN voltage = essentially full DAC 0-3.3V range (R121 10M bias contributes ~1%). No attenuator implements the peripheral_map target of scaling DAC 0-3.3V to +/-0.4 ppm; OCXO sees full pulling range, degrading steering resolution and disciplining/holdover stability.
- [ ] [Clock mux (OCXO/ext-ref -> PH0)] U53: MPN/grade not pinned. Symbol Value=74LVC1G34 (generic) with TI datasheet link (sn74lvc1g34.pdf); BOM MPN=74LVC1G34, flagged MPN-FROM-VALUE. Canonical doc (sts1000_clock_mux.md sec5/A) requires Nexperia 74LVC1G34GW-Q100 (AEC-Q100 Grade 1, -40/+125 C) to match U52 grade. As-entered, no automotive grade is enforced and vendor is ambiguous.
- [ ] [Clock mux (OCXO/ext-ref -> PH0)] U52: MPN entered via MPN-FROM-VALUE (BOM line 521); MANUFACTURER field blank. Vendor/orderable PN not pinned, and the package descriptor in the footprint name is self-contradictory (SC-74 + TSOP6 + SOT457 are three different package families).
- [ ] [External 10 MHz RF front end (refclock-input.kicad_sch)] U51 PG (pin 4) / net 3V0_RF_LDO_PG: PG is open-collector (datasheet) and the net has only U51.4 and U55(MCP23017) GPA2 -- no external pull-up. It relies entirely on the MCP23017 internal weak pull-up (GPPU) being enabled by firmware; if GPPU is off the line floats and the status read is indeterminate.
- [ ] [External 10 MHz RF front end (refclock-input.kicad_sch)] U49 / U50 / U51 MPN: Placeholder MPNs not orderable and ambiguous on grade: U49='TMUX1101DCK' (needs reel suffix, e.g. DCKR), U50='LTC6752xS5' (the 'x' is a temp-grade placeholder: must commit LTC6752IS5 or HS5, base/non-latching -- NOT -2/-3 which are 5.25 V separate-supply), U51='LT3045xDD' (must commit E/I/H/MP grade). Project rule requires AEC/automotive -40/+85 where available -> choose I or H grades. BOM Status=MPN-FROM-VALUE, no Mfr/Digikey.
- [ ] [External 10 MHz RF front end (refclock-input.kicad_sch)] U50 VCC margin (R183 33R + D21): VCC guard holds U50 VCC at ~2.85 V nominal (3.0 V island - Iq*33R, Iq~4.5 mA). LTC6752 S5 single-supply min operating ~2.45 V. With island tolerance (LDO set by 1%-grade R186) + D21 leakage + Iq spread, the 2.85 V sits ~0.4 V above min -- adequate but not generous, and a 3.3 V zener (soft knee) on D21 can leak near 3.0-3.3 V.
- [ ] [Rb buck supply (VCC_RB)] U45 (MCP1502) nSHDN pin4: Reference is GATED by RB_PWR_EN (nSHDN <- Net-(Q19-C) via Q19/Q20), not always-on. VREF_4V096 feeds BOTH the digipot terminal AND the OV-latch comparator reference. On RB_PWR_EN assertion, VREF ramps from 0 concurrently with the buck soft-start (SS cap C119=10nF, fast) -> startup race: FB injection setpoint and OV trip threshold are briefly undefined; rail could overshoot or OV could false-trip before VREF settles.
- [ ] [Rb buck supply (VCC_RB)] U40 (MIC28516) SVIN/PVIN on VOUT_P: VOUT_P is the PoE/PD bridge rail, up to ~57V (per poe_kill doc, R18 sized at VOUT_P=57V). MIC28516 abs-max VIN=70V -> only ~13V headroom; surge/ringing on a 57V PoE rail could approach the limit.
- [ ] [Rb buck supply (VCC_RB)] R159 (shunt): Shunt value unresolved (BOM status SHUNT-REVIEW, 20m placeholder). Doc notes 100m drops 150mV/225mW at 1.5A (too large); ~20m with ADCRANGE=1 gives +/-2A FS. Affects INA228 scaling and power dissipation.
- [ ] [Rb buck supply (VCC_RB)] D7 (1.5SMCxxA TVS): MPN unfinalized (value '1.5SMCxxA', BOM status SELECT). Doc requires 28V standoff (1.5SMCJ28A): 24.35V max < 28V standoff < ~31V VBR < ~45V clamp. Must be 28V variant to not clip normal operation yet protect below TVS.
- [ ] [Rb buck supply (VCC_RB)] R144 (RINJ 10.7k): Ripple-injection value is a bench-trim starting point; FB AC load R2\|\|Rctrl ~505 ohm attenuates injected ripple. Adaptive-on-time MIC28516 needs adequate FB ripple for stable operation across 5-24V.
- [ ] [FE-5680A RS-232 interface (rb-io sheet)] K1: 3 VDC coil (G6K-2F-Y DC3, 91Ω) driven from the 3.3 V rail = 110% rated coil voltage → ~36 mA, ~120 mW vs 100 mW nominal. Within the relay's continuous-voltage limit at 23°C but runs hot; at an 85°C enclosure the coil temperature-rise margin should be checked.
- [ ] [FE-5680A RS-232 interface (rb-io sheet)] U47: Footprint inconsistency: schematic symbol default FP = 'SOT23_NXP' (custom) but BOM FP = 'TO-236AB'. Combined with the missing fp-lib-table, the PESD15VL2BT footprint is unresolved.
- [ ] [FE-5680A RS-232 interface (rb-io sheet)] K1 throws: Relay NC/NO throw assignment (pins 2/3/4/5/6/7) is correct in the netlist topology but the de-energized=NC=RS-232 default must be confirmed against the Omron terminal-arrangement diagram once a footprint is assigned (pad-to-throw mapping).
- [ ] [SPI peripherals (NOR flash, U62)] U62 VCC decoupling: Because the VCC pin is unmapped, presence/placement of a dedicated 100 nF bypass cap on U62 pin 8 cannot be verified. 3V3_STM has many bulk/bypass caps but none provably adjacent to U62.
- [ ] [I2C peripherals + display power] sts1000_3v3p_i2c_peripherals.md (canonical doc): Doc still specifies a gated 3V3_P / PERIPH_EN=PC11 rail with PCA9517/TCA4311 back-power-isolation buffer for these peripherals, but the schematic + root CLAUDE.md have eliminated 3V3_P and put all peripherals on always-on 3V3_STM. The doc's entire bus-topology section (§2/D7) and rail enumeration (§6) are stale.
- [ ] [I2C peripherals + display power] U63 pin8 (EN) / DISP_EN: PCA9306 EN is driven by a 3V3 push-pull GPIO (via R104). Datasheet wants EN biased to the high side (VREF2=5V) and >=1V above VREF1 for best translation; here EN(high)=3V3=VREF1, giving zero headroom over VREF1.
- [ ] [I2C peripherals + display power] U33 RT9742VGJ5 current-limit tier vs display inrush + R107 0.1Ohm drop: RT9742 'V' suffix selects one ILIM tier (family is 0.5/1/1.5/2/2.5/3A). Open item: confirm the V-tier ILIM exceeds the LCD module backlight-full + Cin inrush, and that the 0.1Ohm series shunt (R107) plus switch RDS(on) leave enough rail headroom at 5V.
- [ ] [Fault/UI aggregation (MCP23017 ×2: U55 @0x20, U54 @0x21)] U54/U55 footprint EP: Assigned KiCad std-lib footprint QFN-28-1EP_6x6mm_P0.65mm_EP4.25x4.25mm specifies a 4.25x4.25mm exposed pad; Microchip MCP23017 ML package drawing nominal EP is ~4.45mm. Body 6x6 and 0.65mm pitch are correct, but EP land should be confirmed against the exact /ML package drawing before layout.
- [ ] [Fault/UI aggregation (MCP23017 ×2: U55 @0x20, U54 @0x21)] U55 GPB2-7 (pins 27,28,3,4) spare inputs: Six spare expander I/O left unconnected/floating. Floating CMOS inputs raise quiescent current and can produce spurious INT/INTCAP reads.
- [ ] [I2C1 bus + rise-time accelerator (U56 LTC4311)] I2C_SCL / I2C_SDA bus: A single 4.7k pull-up pair (R202/R203) serves an I2C1 bus carrying ~16 device loads (U10,U12,U23,U26,U30,U31,U32,U37,U44,U54,U55,U56,U57,U58,U59,U60,U61,U63) routed across ~10 schematic sheets. The LTC4311 (U56) is present precisely because bus capacitance is high, but C_bus is not yet budgeted against the LTC4311's supported load or the target SCL frequency. If total C_bus or rise time is out of range the bus is marginal even with the accelerator.
- [ ] [Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch)] D6: SMF5V0A (VRWM 5.0 V) sits on the 5V_DISP rail. A 5.0 V standoff on a nominal 5 V rail leaves ~0 V margin; at the rail's upper tolerance (e.g. 5.25 V) the TVS leaks/clamps, causing standby current and possible nuisance regulation interaction.
- [ ] [Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch)] RTC_TAMPER / C44 / TAMP: Tamper relies on the STM32 TAMP internal precharge pull-up (no external PU) with C44=1 nF. Correctness depends on RM0481 TAMP config (TAMPPRCH/TAMPFLT) and the actual internal R_PU charging 1 nF inside the precharge window; unverified against datasheet.
- [ ] [Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch)] L10 (GPS SMA ESD): Single polymer suppressor (PGB, 0.06 pF, 150 V) protects the GPS SMA. Capacitance and bias-voltage requirements are met, but per project rule an outdoor antenna run also needs a separate coaxial gas-discharge arrestor — not present on-board.
- [ ] [Connectors, USB-C console, panel UI, display IF (connectors.kicad_sch)] D8/D9 SZESD7410: Distributor listing flags SZESD7410MXWT5G as 'Active Obsolete' at one source — possible lifecycle/sourcing risk for a long-life instrument.
- [ ] [RGB status indicator (D5)] R59/R60/R61: Ballast resistors are 0402 in the schematic, but doc §4 and §10 explicitly require 0603 ('do not use 0402 on red/blue'). Dissipations (B 37 mW, R 48 mW, G 16 mW) are within a 0402's ~63-100 mW rating, so this is not an immediate thermal failure, but it directly contradicts the canonical design and removes the intended margin.
- [ ] [RGB status indicator (D5)] D5: Blue design point is 24.8 mA = the 25 C absolute-max DC forward current; I_F derates to 0 at 80 C T_OP. If the front-panel local ambient is warm, the blue die is over-driven. Doc §7 flags this but it is unverified.

**4. Can resolve during layout**
- [ ] Apply net-class widths/clearances from §12–13 once stackup + copper weight chosen.
- [ ] Confirm controlled-impedance targets (RMII MDI 100Ω diff, USB 90Ω diff, RF 50Ω) with board-house field solver.

**5. Can defer until post-layout review**
- [ ] DRC, copper-pour audit (magnetometer keep-out), thermal sim of OCXO/Rb/bucks, supercap temperature verification.
